antarbhāvavyavahāre ca * samānavidhitvāt * samānalakṣaṇayogitvāditi panyāsaḥ kathaṃ sādhyānna viśiṣyate ? lakṣaṇaikatvasya tadvyavahārādanyatvāt । samānā vidhirupāyo lakṣaṇaṃ yeṣāṃ tāni tathoktāni, teṣāṃ bhāvastattvaṃ tasmāditi । tadevāha * yathā 〈prasiddhasamayasyāsandigdha〉 liṅgadarśanaprasiddhyanusmaraṇābhyām atīndriye 'rthe bhavatyanumānamevaṃ śabdādibhyo 'pīti । yathā hi gṛhītasambandhasya liṅgadarśanānantaram avinābhāvasambandhasmaraṇaṃ tābhyāma atha paricchedya bhavatyanamānama । anamīyate 'neneti parāmarśajñānamevopacāreṇa vyutpattyā vā, tad vivakṣitam । “evaṃ śabdādibhyo 'pīti” dārṭāntikavyākhyānam ।

<II,164>

[II,164,1]

anye tu parāmarśajñānasyāsattvameveti manyante । taccāsat, avinābhāva sambandhasmaraṇasya aniyatatvānniyatadeśe pratipattirna syāt, upanayavaiyarthyañce. tyuktamataḥ pūrvameva nyāyyam ।

[II,164,4]

atra tadguṇasaṃvijñānapakṣe śabdasyāpyanumāne 'ntarbhāvaḥ । tathā ca śabda śravaṇāt samayānusmaraṇe sati parāmarśajñānaṃ tasmāt parokṣārthapratipattiriti । ayaṃ gośabdaḥ kakudādimadarthavān gośabdatvāt pūrvopalabdhaivaṃvidhagośabdavaditi, sambandhāvagamenārthapratipādakatvācca dhūmavat ।

[II,164,8]

tadetadasat, gośabdasya kakudādimadarthavattāyāḥ pratipādayitumaśakya tvāt । tathā hi, śabdasyārthena anyasambandhābhāvād vācyavācakatvenārtha pratipādakatve sādhye gośabdatvamahetuḥ, pratipādakatvasya pratipattyavaseyatvāt, svābhāvikasambandhānupapatteśca । dhūmo hi svābhāvikasambandhena sarvaprāṇabhṛtā manumeyārthapratipādakaḥ, na caivaṃ śabdaḥ, puruṣecchāsampāditasamayāpekṣasyārtha pratipādakatvāt । svābhāvikasambandhe hi vināpi saṅketaṃ mlecchādiśabda śravaṇād arthapratipattiḥ syāt । saṅketāpekṣasya tu arthapratipādakatve sa evāstu, alaṃ nityasambandheneti । na ca nityasambandhābhāve 'tiprasaṅgaḥ, naimittika śabdānāṃ dravyatvādinimittasadbhāve satyeva saṅketāt, yādṛcchikaśabdānāntu puruṣecchā nu〈〉 vidhānāditi । yatra ca viśiṣṭānupūrvīmattvasadbhāvastadeva niyamena vācakam, itaracca vācyamiti vyavasthā saṅketajñānasyobhayaniṣṭhatvā viśeṣāditi ।

[II,164,20]

saṅketastu śabdād vṛddhavyavahārataśca pratīyate । tathā hi, “idamasya vācakam”, “idamasya vācyam” iti vākyāt saṅketapratipattiḥ । vṛddhavyavahārād yathā “devadatta ! gāmabhyāja śuklāṃ daṇḍena” iti prayogād avyutpanno 'nvaya vyatirekābhyāṃ devadattādiśabdeṣu saṅketaṃ pratipadyate । vṛddhavyavahartṛṇāmapi saṅketapratipattiranyato vyavahārādityanāditvaṃ parihāraḥ । yad vā ādipuruṣaḥ sākṣādraṣṭā keṣāñcit saṅketakartā astīti । vākyarūpastu śabdo 'rthapratipattau samayamapi nāpekṣata iti sambandhabalenārthapratipādakatvamasiddham ।

<II,165>

[II,165,1]

na ca śabdasyānumānatvameva niṣidhyate, vivakṣākāśa ? yora dhigame liṅgatvāt । yathāhi, ākāśādhigame sarvaḥ śabdo 'numānam, vivakṣākāryastu vivakṣādhigame 'pīti । na ca śabdajñānavallaiṅgikajñānamāptoktatvamapekṣate । tathā hi, śabdajñāne kimida samyaṅa mithyā veti saṃśayotpattāvāptoktamanāptoktaṃ 〈cā? vā〉nvīkṣate, laiṅgikantu pakṣadharmatvādikamiti vyatirekaḥ ।

[II,165,6]

tadāha * śrutismṛtilakṣaṇo 'pyāmnāyo vaktṛprāmāṇyāpekṣaḥ * iti । na ca paraṃ laukikaḥ śabdo vaktṛprāmāṇyamapekṣate śrutismṛtilakṣaṇo 'poti ।

[II,165,8]

nanu vaktṛprāmāṇyenāmnāyaprāmāṇyābhyupagame bahūnā manyo 'nyāśrayatvaṃ syāt । tathā hi, arthaprāptyā āptoktatvaṃ śabde niścīyate niścayāccārthāva bodhe sati pravartamānasyārthaprāptiriti । tathā pauruṣeye vacasi satyāsatyatvo palabdhervede 'pi puruṣānupraveśe tadāśaṅkāyāmaprāmāṇyameva syāt । na ca sākṣādatīndriyārthadraṣṭā puruṣaḥ sambhavatīti kathaṃ tadvācakāni vacāṃsi tatpūrvakānīti ?

[II,165,14]

yadi cānyasmād vedavākyādarthaṃ pratipadya vacanaracanāṃ kuryāt, tasyāpi nityatvena kiñcid bādhitaṃ syāt, anityatve tu tatkarturapyanyasmād vākyā darthāvabodha ityanavasthā syāt । na cānityatvaṃ vedavākyānāṃ pramāṇaprasiddhamiti kathaṃ vaktṛviśeṣāpekṣaṃ prāmāṇyam ?

[II,165,18]

arthapratipattau ca śabdasya svābhidhāśaktibalenaiva vyāpāro nāptoktatvama pekṣamāṇasyeti । sā ca tasya svātmabhūtaiva, na paścāt pareṇa sampādyata iti svata eva prāmāṇyam । na cāptoktatvaṃ śakyate pratipattuṃ pratipakṣā ? bandhā । deraviṣayatvāt । aprāmāṇyantu duṣṭapuruṣapraṇītatvāpekṣamiti parataḥ ।

[II,165,22]

tathā sarvapramāṇānāmapi prāmāṇye na parāpekṣitā sambhavati, svakāraṇe bhyo 'rthāvabodhasvarūpāṇāmutpatteḥ । yadi cāvidyamānamarthaparicchedakatvaṃ pari niṣpanne vijñāne kārakāntarādutpadyate, pratipadyemahi parataḥ prāmāṇyam, na caitadastītyāha,
<II,166>
	svataḥ sarvapramāṇānāṃ prāmāṇyamiti gṛhyatām /
	na hi svato 'satī śaktiḥ kartumanyena śakyate // <= ślo. vā. 2.76>

[II,166,3]

na ca jñānasyārthaparicchedakatvaṃ kāraṇaguṇapūrvakam, indriyeṣu tadabhāvāt tadāha,
	vyāpāraḥ kārakāṇāṃ hi dṛṣṭo janmātirekataḥ /
	pramāṇe 'pi tathā mā bhūditi janma vivakṣyate // <= ślo. vā. pṛ. 151>

[II,166,7]

yathā hīndriyāṇāṃ janmavyatirekaṇāparo vyāpāro naivaṃ jñānasya, anantara meva phalasampādakatvāt । dṛṣṭañca pareṇāpi viśeṣaṇādijñānasya viśeṣyādijñāna janmani prāmāṇyamiti । athopajātamapi jñānaṃ na kārakapariśaddherbodhaṃ vinā arthaparicchedakatvabhāk ? tarhi tatrāpi kārakapariśuddhigrahaṇaṃ vācyamityana vasthā । tadāha,
	jāte 'pi yadi vijñāne tāvannārtho 'vadhāryate /
	yāvat kāraṇaśuddhatvaṃ na pramāṇāntarāgatam // <= ślo. vā. pṛ. 60>
	tatra jñānāntarotpādaḥ pratīkṣyaḥ kāraṇāntarāt /
	yāvaddhi na paricchinnā śuddhistāvadasat samā // <= ślo. vā. pṛ. 60>
	tasyāpi kāraṇe śuddhe tajjñānasya pramāṇatā /
	tasyāpyevamitīsthañca na kaścid vyavatiṣṭhate // <= ślo. vā. pṛ. 61>

[II,166,18]

atha vidyamānamapi pramāṇasya prāmāṇyaṃ na pramāṇāntarasaṃvāda vinā pramāṇavyavahārakāraṇam ? tarhi pramāṇaparamparāyāmapakṣīṇaśaktavivakṣitajñāna pramāṇavyavahāro na syāt । tadāha,
	sammatyā yadi ceṣyeta pūrvapūrvapramāṇatā /
	pramāṇāntaramicchanto na vyavasthāṃ labhemahi // <= ślo. vā. pṛ. 50>

[II,166,23]

yadi ca kasyacit svata eva prāmāṇyamiṣyeta param, ādyasyaivāstu ityāha
	kasyacittu yadīṣyeta svata eva pramāṇatā /
	prathamasya tathābhāve pradveṣaḥ kiṃ nibandhanaḥ //
	<= ślo. vā. pṛ. 69>

<II,167>

[II,167,1]

prathamottarayoḥ parasparāpekṣaṃ prāmāṇyamityabhyupagame cetaretarāśrayatvaṃ syāt । ataḥ svata eva prāmāṇyam aprāmāṇyantu parataḥ । tathā hi, laukikā nāmava śabdānāmaprāmāṇyam, puruṣadoṣānupraveśāt, vaidikānāntu tadabhāvāda prāmāṇyaśajhaiva nāstīti ।

[II,167,5]

arthandriyāṇāṃ kācakāmalādidoṣavaśādaprāmāṇyaṃ na svarūpataḥ । tathā hi, kāmalādidoṣasadabhāve sati mithyājñānajanakatvaṃ na tadabhāva iti ।

[II,167,7]

jñaptau cāvabodhakatvena mithyāmaterautsargikamānatvaṃ na nivṛttamiti pakapratyayānmithyātvāvagatau vyāvartate । na cāsmatpakṣe śuktikājñānenāpi 4〈〉 śuktikājñānasya bādhāyāmanavasthā, kārakaśuddhigrahaṇaparamparā veti pacyam, avabodhakatvenautsargikasya pramāṇatvasya doṣa? 7 darśanamātreṇaiva 〈āva ? ānava〉 sthānāt । tadāha,
	yadā svataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ tadānyaṃ naiva mṛgyate /
	nivartate ca mithyātvaṃ doṣajñānādayatnataḥ // <= ślo. vā. pṛ. 61>
	doṣajñāne tvanatpanne nāśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikā /
	eva tricaturajñānajanmano nādhikā matiḥ // <= ślo. vā. pṛ. 64>
ityanavasthāparihāraḥ ।

[II,167,17]

tadetat sarvamaviditārtham, sarvapramāṇānāmutpattau jñaptau ca parāpekṣitopa yaḥ । tathā hi āptoktatvamapekṣamāṇaḥ śabdo 'rthe samyag jñānamupajanayati, parantareṇeti dṛṣṭam । yacca bahūnāmanyonyāśrayatvamuktam, tanna yuktam, patitvasyāgṛhyamāṇasyaiva śabdasahakāritvābhyupagamāt । arthaprāptau ca śāntareṇa paścāt tadgrahaṇamiṣyata eva । tathā hi, laukikaśabdānāmartha cāptaktitvaṃ niścīyate । pratyakṣeṇāpi gṛhyata ityanye । tathā ca śrotravyā " vākyaśravaṇe sati cāṇakyoktaṃ kālidāsoktañcaitadityabādhyamānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ, vadikavākyānāntu pradhānārtheṣu avisaṃvādādāptāktatvānaścayaḥ ।

[II,167,25]

yadi pauruṣeye vacasi dvaividhyopalabdhervede 'pi puruṣānupraveśe 'prāmāṇyaśaṅkā bāta dūṣaṇam, tanna, tatkarturdoṣābhāvāt । tathā hi, yasya rāgādidoṣo 'sti, <II,168> tadvacanamevāpramāṇamityupalabdham, vedakartuśca tatsadbhāve pramāṇābhāvaḥ । sākṣādatīndriyārthadraṣṭā puruṣaḥ sambhavatītyuktamadhastāt । ataḥ “tadvacanādā mnāyasya (vedarāśeḥ) ?〈〉 prāmāṇyam” iti sūtrakāreṇoktam ।

[II,168,4]

atha śabdasyānityatve satyāptoktatvena prāmāṇyaṃ syāt, tattu nāstā tyāśaṅkayāha * liṅgāccānitya 〈〉 ḥ śabdaḥ * <= vai. sū0> iti । paraṃ pratyakṣa ṇoccāraṇāt prāg ūrdhvañcānupalambhādanityaḥ śabda iti pratīyate, liṅgācceti, tattu vakṣyāmaḥ śabdaparokṣāyām । vedānāñcānityatve 'numānam, anityāni vedavākyāni vākyatvādabhayābhimatavākyavat । tathā * buddhipūrvā vākya kṛtiḥ 5 vākyaracanā, vede 〈buddhipūrvā〉 vākyaracanātvād ubhayābhimatavākya racanāvat । yaccedaṃ vedaracanāyāḥ sarvadā anyathātvopalambhāditi vaidhamyaṇa pratyavasthānam, tat sarvānumāneṣu samānamiti । evaṃ (vede ?) * buddhipūvā dadātiḥ * vede buddhipūrvo dadātiśabdaḥ dadātītyuktatvād ubhayābhimata dadātītiśabdavat ।

[II,168,14]

yā ceyaṃ puruṣānupraveśe satyaprāmāṇyaśaṅkā, sā nityatve 'pi na nivartata, śrotuḥ puruṣasya tatrāpyanupraveśāt, tadvaiguṇyena cāprāmāṇyopalabdheḥ । tathā hi, śroturapratibhādemithyājñānotpattau kāraṇa tvaṃ tadabhāvaśca samyag jñānotpattā vityupalabdhameva । na ca nityatvaṃ vedānām ekāntena prāmāṇyahetuḥ, tadbhāvajāpa śrotrāntaḥkaraṇayoḥ pratipattṛdoṣānupraveśena kvacidaprāmāṇyāt ।

[II,168,19]

svābhidhāśaktibalenaiva śabdasya prāmāṇyamityabhyapagame ca amulyagna kariṇastiṣṭhantītyevamāderaprāmāṇyaṃ na syāt । athānāptapraṇītatvena visavā dādaprāmāṇyameṣām ? tarhi yadāptapraṇītam, tadeva pramāṇamiti prāptam । yasa hi puruṣagatasya rāgāderaprāmāṇye 'nvayavyatirekābhyāṃ vyāpārastathā tadguṇāda prāmāṇye prītyubhayaṃ parataḥ ।

[II,168,24]

abhidhānasya ca varṇa tvā ? | nupūrvīsaṅketavyatirekeṇa atīndriyā śaktirna vidyate, tasyāḥ pūrvameva pratiṣedhāt, varṇatvādisadbhāve ca kāryakaraṇāta, sa ca parata evaṃ pratiniyatajātisambandhasyādṛṣṭakāryatvāt । saṅkatasyā pyanyat kāraṇamuktamiti ।

<II,169>

[II,169,1]

yattu sākṣādarśanādiḥ puruṣasya rāgādivināśe vyāpriyate na jñānotpattā pratyuktam, tadasat, samyagjñānotpattāvanvayavyatirekopapatteḥ । yathārthadraṣṭā tacchaṣyāṇāmupadeṣṭā ceti samuditamāptalakṣaṇaṃ yathārthopadeśe hetustadantareṇānu aśāt । yadi cānvayavyatirekavato 'pi yathārthadarśitvāde rāgādivināśa eva vyāpāraḥ । tarhi rāgāderapyetadavināśakatvamevetyubhayaṃ parataḥ syāt । tasmād ! diraprāmāṇyotpattāviva yathārthopalambhāderapi samyagjñānotpattau vyāpāro 'bhyupagantavyaḥ ।

[II,169,8]

tathendriyāṇāmapi kācakāmalādidoṣasadbhāve 〈'pi ?〉 mithyājñānameva tadabhāva samyagjñānajananādubhayaṃ parataḥ । pareṇāpyabhāvasya kāraṇatvamanekadheṣṭam । yathā sadupalambhakapramāṇapañcakavyāvṛttermānasajñānotpattau pakṣadharmatādyanata pāya ca liṅgasya mithyājñānotpattāvityādi । atha kācakāmalāderdoṣasya । yājñānotpattau kāraṇatopalabdhaḥ, tadabhāve tasyaivānupalabdhirna samyagjñāna ta cet, na, anvayavyatirekavato 'kāraṇatve 'tiprasaṅgāt 〈yadi ? tathā〉 ca deṣābhāve 'nvayavyatirekavānapi na samyagjñānotpattau kāraṇaṃ, tatsadbhāve 'pi na mithyājñānotpattāvityubhayaṃ svataḥ syāt । sargaścendriyāṇāmubhayarūpasya kāryasyopalabdharubhayārthamiti jñāyeta ।

[II,169,17]

nanu doṣasadbhāve sati indriyaṃ mithyājñānaṃ janayati, tadabhāve ca yam jñānamityabhyupagamād ubhayābhāve ca ubhayavikalaṃ vijñānaṃ kuryādi dacodyam, ubhayavikalasyendriyasyāsambhavāt । yathā hi pūrvamasatāṃ doṣāṇā tarūvaṃñca pradhvaṃsa iti nāstyubhayavikalamindriyam । na cobhayaviśeṣavikalaṃ jñānatvasāmānyaṃ sambhavati, sāmānyavato viśeṣayogāt । yathā gotvasāmānyādhārasya śāvaleyādiviśeṣa iti ।

[II,169,22]

yaccedaṃ na kāraṇaguṇapūrvakaṃ paricchedakatvaṃ tadiṣyata eva, anubhava mānasyandriyādutpannasyārthaparicchittirūpatvāt । tajjanakañcendriyādikāraka antarāpekṣañceti parataḥ prāmāṇyam । kārakasāmagrayantu na paścādabhāvinimittamapekṣata iti । tadapekṣayā tabhayaṃ svata iti na mithyājñānaṃ parataḥ syāt ।

<II,170>

[II,170,1]

atha jñātṛvyāpāro jñānaṃ tacca arthaparicchede 'napekṣamiti svataḥ ? nanmithyājñāne 'pi samānam । atha mithyājñānaṃ doṣamapekṣate ? tarhi samyaga jñānamapi tadabhāvādyapekṣata iti । na ca jñātṛvyāpāraḥ sambhāvyate, arthaprati patteranyathābhāvāt । tathā hi sarva kārakaṃ caramasahakārisadabhāve sati kārya karotīti na tasmādanyo vyāpāraḥ, sadbhāve 'pi nityatāyāṃ sarvakāryotpatti prasaṅgastasyānapekṣakāraṇatvābhyupagamāt । anityatve tu tadutpattāvāpa nirvyāpārasya kāraṇatvāyogādanyo vyāpārastadutpattāvapyanya ityanavasthā syāt । caramasahakārirūpe tu vyāpāre nāyaṃ doṣastata sadbhāve kāya karaṇaṃ na tadabhāva iti ।

[II,170,10]

yaccedaṃ kārakaśuddhagrahaṇāpekṣitāyāṃ dūṣaṇam, tadapāstam, anabhyupagama neti । atha pramāṇasya prāmāṇyaṃ vinaiva pramāṇaṃ vijñāyata iti, tadasat, savasya prameyasya pramāṇaparicchedyatvopalabdheḥ । tathā ca prāmāṇyaṃ pramāṇaparicchā prameyatvād ghaṭādivat । na cānavasthā, sarvatrāvaśyaṃ prāmāṇyagrahaṇānabhyupa gamāt । yatra hi jñānodaye sati kimidaṃ samyaṅamithyā veti saṃśayotpattistatrava pramāṇāntarāpekṣā, arthaprāptiparyantavyavahārasambhave vā apekṣāvinivṛttanāna vasthādidoṣaḥ ।

[II,170,17]

yadi ca jñānadharmatvāt prāmāṇyasya svasaṃvedyatvamiṣyeta. aprāmāṇyamapyana syāditi kathaṃ parataḥ ? tathā mithyājñānotpāde na pravartate mithyātvasya pratipanna tvāt, samyagjñānotpattau ca samyaktādhyavasāye kimidaṃ samyaṅ mithyā vāra saṃśayādyabhāvaḥ ।

[II,170,21]

yaccedam avabodhakatvena pramāṇasya prāmāṇyaṃ doṣādarśanamātreṇavāvāta ityuktama, tatra yadi doṣādarśanadoṣajñānānatpattirna tayā prāmāṇyaṃ jñāpyata, nāra kriyata iti kathamaniścitasthiteravasthānavacanama ? atha doṣadarśanasya bābā pratyayasya mithyātvajñāpakatvamiva tadabhāvajñānasya prāmāṇyajñāpakatvamiṣyata, ". tasyāpi prāmāṇyamanyasmād vijñāyata ityanavasthā syāta । atha jñānāla saṃśayaṃ vinā na sarvatra prāmāṇyagrahaṇāpekṣeti parihāraḥ ? tarhi na svata prāmāṇyam, utpattau jñaptau ca parāpekṣitvābhyupagamāt ।

<II,171>

[II,171,1]

atha indriyādikārakeṣu vidyamānaṃ samyaktvaṃ na kāraṇaguṇaprakrameṇa śāneṣutpadyata iti svataḥ ? tadaprāmāṇye 'pi samānam । tatrāpi hi viparyayādi rūpatā na indriyādiṣu vidyamānā jāyata iti ।

[II,171,4]

bodhātmakapramāṇāpekṣayā tu svataḥ prāmāṇyaṃ vivakṣitamityabhyupagamasya coda nāyā vaktṛviśeṣāpekṣaṃ prāmāṇyamityabhyupagamenāvirodhād avivāda eva syāt, asya hi samarthanārtham anyapramāṇānāṃ parataḥ prāmāṇyopadarśanāt । na ca coda nāyāḥ svataḥ prāmāṇyābhyupagame, codanājanitaṃ jñānaṃ pramāṇam, doṣajitaiḥ rikarjanyamānatvāt, liṅgāt pratyakṣabuddhivaditi parīkṣārthaṃ prayāso ghaṭate । atha aparaṣā vyāmohavyāvartanadvāreṇa samyagjñānasampādanārtha parīkṣāvākyam ? tajja nitajñāne 'pi vyāmohe sati anyā parīkṣā syādityanavasthā । sā coktanyāyenaiva rāhayata iti kathaṃ na parataḥ pramāṇasya prāmāṇyamutpadyate jñāyate veti ।

[II,171,12]

śeṣañcātra dūṣaṇapratisamādhānam asmadgurubhivistareṇābhihitamiti neho m । ataḥ śabdasyāptoktatvena prāmāṇyānnānumāne 'ntarbhāvaḥ ।

[II,171,14]

atha śabdānāmarthena pratibandhābhāvād aprāmāṇyameva । tathā ca dṛśya kalpyāvarthāvekīkṛtya tatsamāropeṇa śrotuḥ pravṛttinivṛttī ityuktam । yo 'yaṃ vikalpagata ākāraḥ, sa eva bāhyo 'rtha iti manyamānaḥ pratipattā pravartate, na māhyārthapratipattau arthadarśane sati vivakṣākrameṇa, śabdotpattikāle 'rthasya kṣaṇikatvenātikrāntatvāt ।

[II,171,19]

pratyakṣānumānaviṣaya〈syā ? 〉tirikta<?> viṣayābhāvācca, na śabdaḥ māṇāntaram । tathā hi svalakṣaṇaviṣayaṃ pratyakṣaṃ sāmānyaviṣayamanumānam । yadvavidhyāt pramāṇadvaividhyamiti kathaṃ śabdo 'rthāntaratve sati pramāṇam ?

[II,171,22]

yadi cendriyeṇa samānaviṣayaḥ śabdo bhavedandhānandhayoraviśeṣaḥ syāt । tadāha,
	anyadevendriyagrāhyamanyaḥ śabdasya gocaraḥ /
	śabdāt pratyeti bhinnākṣo na tu pratyakṣamīkṣate //

[II,171,26]

anyadeva rūpādisvalakṣaṇamindriyagrāhyam, tasmādanyaḥ śabdasya gocaro '<II,172>poha 〈〉viṣaya iti gṛhyatām । yataḥ śabdāt pratyeti bhinnākṣaḥ pradhvastanayanaḥ, na tu pratyakṣaṃ yathā bhavati tathekṣate । samānaviṣayatve vā anandhasyevāndhasyāpi śabdādaparokṣaiva pratipattiḥ syāt । tathātve indriyāgnisambandhādivad dāha śabdādapi dāhārthapratipattiḥ syādityāha,
	anyathaivāgnisambandhād dāhaṃ dagdho 'bhimanyate /
	anyathā dāhaśabdena dāhārthaḥ sampratīyate //

[II,172,7]

tasmānnendriyeṇa samānaviṣayatvaṃ śabdasya । tathā padādiśabdasya svalakṣaṇa viṣayatve tasya nirbhāgatayā śuklādiśabdānāmapi paryāyatā bhavet । apoha viṣayatve tu nāyaṃ doṣaḥ, vibhinnānāṃ samāropavyavacchedaparatvāditi ।

[II,172,10]

vāstavārthaviṣayatve ca śabdānāṃ puruṣecchābaśena aniyatārthatvaṃ na syāt । vyavahārastu śabdānmayā pratipannaṃ śabdena ca pratipādayāmīti, pratipādyaprati pādakayostamirikadvayadvicandradarśanavad bhaviṣyatīti । yathaikastaimirikaścandradvayaṃ pratipadya pratipādayati, aparaśca pratipadyate, tathā sarvatra vyavahattaṇāmayaṃ śabdo vyavahāra iti । atha parīkṣakāstarhi śabdārdhādhyavasāye sati mithyātvaṃ manyamānāḥ pravartante ? lokavyavahārānusāritayā, “lokavyavahāraṃ prati sadṛśau bālapaṇḍitau” iti nyāyāt । mithyājñānasya cārthapratipādakatvaṃ kvacidupa labdham । yathā maṇipradīpaprabhayomaṇibuddhyābhidhāvatomithyājñānāviśeṣe 'pi viśeṣo 'rthakriyāṃ prati ।

[II,172,19]

tadetadasat, śabdādarthādhyavasāye sati pravartamānasya arthāvisaṃvādena akṣajajñānavad abhrāntatvena prāmāṇyopapatteḥ । tathā hi indriyajñānasyāpi samyaktve na arthāvisaṃvādaṃ vinā pramāṇāntaramasti, sa ca śābdajñāne 'pyastīti kathamapramāṇam ?

[II,172,23]

pratibandho 'pi kāryaviśeṣopalabdherindriyāṇāmiva śabdasyāpyarthena vācyaḥ । sa ca vācyavācakālambanaṃ saṅketajñānameva, anyasyāsambhavāt । tasya ca viśeṣāṇāmānantye 'pi ekasāmānyasyopagrahādupapattirityuktameva । yadi ca śabdānāmaprāmāṇyam, pramāṇādisvarūpāvabodhārthaṃ śāstramanarthakaṃ syāt, pramāṇā disvarūpasya pāramparyeṇāpi tasmādapratīteḥ ।

<II,173>

[II,173,1]

yadi ca vivakṣāsūcakatvenaiva prāmāṇyamiṣyeta, tarhi sarvavākyānāṃ tatrāvya bhicārādaviśeṣeṇa prāmāṇye vādiprativādinovivāde jayaparājayavyavasthā na syāt । atha yadvākyamarthapratibandhāṃ?ddhāṃ〈〉 vivakṣāṃ sūcayati, tadeva pramāṇaṃ na sarvamiti cet, na, śabdavad vivakṣāṇāmapi ekāntena arthapratibandhābhāvāt । tathā ca artha darśanānusmaraṇakrameṇa vivakṣākāle nārthasyāvasthānamastīti । ato bāhyārthādhyavasāye satyeva pravartante na “dṛśyavikalpyāvāvekīkṛtya tatsamāropeṇa” iti ।

[II,173,9]

na ca dṛśyasyānupalabdhervikalpyenakīkaraṇaṃ yuktam, upalabhyamānapadārthe hi candrādau dvittvādisamāropasyānyatropalabdheḥ, śabdārthapratipattau bādhakānupapatteśca mṛṣaiṣā kalpanā ।

[II,173,11]

yaccedaṃ vivakṣākrameṇa śabdotpattikāle nārthasyāvasthānamastīti, tada pāstam, kṣaṇikatvānabhyupagamena ।

[II,173,13]

atha sāmānyaviśeṣavyatiriktaviṣayābhāvādapramāṇatvaṃ śabdānām, tadasat, ekāntena pramāṇeṣu vyavasthānabhyupagamāt । tathā ca, āgamādātmā pratīyate, punarutpādaliṅgaiḥ yogabalācca pratyakṣato 'pīti saṃplavaḥ । kvacid vyavasthā ca । yathā āgamasya medhyāmadhyapratipattau, indriyāṇāṃ svaviṣayeṣviti । ataḥ pratyakṣādiviṣaye 'pi śabdasya pravṛtterna viṣayāntarābhāvastadaprāmāṇye heturiti । viṣayadvaividhyena ca pramāṇadvittvāvadhāraṇe dūṣaṇaṃ gurubhivistareṇābhihitamiti nehocyate ।

[II,173,20]

yattu śabdānāṃ svalakṣaṇaviṣayatve andhānandhayoraviśeṣaprasaṅga ityuktam, tadasat, viṣayaikatve 'pi karaṇabhedena pratipattyorbhedāt । andhasya hi śabdād rūpaviṣayaṃ vijñānamutpadyate, na tu cākṣuṣamiti । yasya ca aparokṣaṃ cākṣuṣaṃ vijñānamasti, asau anandhaḥ । śabdo hi vyavahitamapyartha prakāśayati, sannikṛṣṭañca indriyam ityanayovibhinna pratipattijanakatvam ।

[II,173,25]

yattu tvagindriyāgnisambandhādiva dāhaśabdādapi dāhārthaḥ sampratīyatetyu, ktam, tatra yadi dāho duḥkham, tatpratīyata eva dāhaśabdāt । na caivaṃ śroturduḥkhi<II,174>tvaprasaṅgaḥ, duḥkhāsamavāyāt । yasya hi duḥkhaṃ samavetamupajātam, sa eva duḥkhī, na tu dāhaśabdād ātmani samavetaṃ duḥkhamutpadyate । kiṃ tarhi ? parātmasamaveta mapi tato vijānātīti । sphoṭādilakṣaṇastu dāhastvaco 'gnisambandhādupajā yate, na dāhaśabdāditi । tasmādevāgnisambandhādutpannasphoṭādikāryastajanita duḥkham ātmāntaḥkaraṇasambandhād anubhavatīti duḥkhītyatidiśyate । dāhaśabdañca anyathaiva anutpannasphoṭādikāryo duḥkhaṃ parātmagataṃ pratipadyate, ityadūṣaṇametat ।

[II,174,8]

na ca svalakṣaṇasya nirbhāgatayā śuklādiśabdānāṃ paryāyatvaprasaṅgaḥ, dharmardhāmaṇorvyatirekāt pratyayabhedasya bhedalakṣaṇatvādityuktam । tasmād bhinna pravṛttinimittānāṃ śabdānāmekārthatve 'pi na paryāyatvamiti ।

[II,174,11]

na cāpohaḥ śabdārthaḥ, tasyaivāsambhavāditi vakṣyāmaḥ ।

[II,174,12]

yattu vāstavārthaviṣayatve puruṣecchāvaśena aniyatārthatvaṃ na syāmiti, tadasat, naimittikaśabdānāṃ nimittavaśena pravṛtternāniyatārthatvam, yādṛcchikā nāntu puruṣecchāvaśena aniyatārthatvamiṣyata eva, bādhakānupapattaśca na taimiri kasya dvicandradarśanavacchāndo vyavahāraḥ । tathā hi, taimirikasya dvicandradarśane timirotpatteḥ prāgūrvañca bādhakamasti, anupajātatimirasya tu sarvadā, na caivaṃ śabdavyavahāre ।

[II,174,18]

yattu mithyājñānāviśeṣe 'pyarthakriyāsiddhiḥ, yathā maṇipradīpaprabhayo rityuktam, tadaparijñānāt । tathā hi, samīpattino yanmaṇāveva vijñānaṃ tade vārthakriyājanakam, na prabhāyāmiti । śābdajñānantu arthaprāptiparyantavyavahāropa labdherindriyajajñānavad bhrāntaṃ na bhavatīti ।

[II,174,22]

na ca vāstavasambandhābhāve śabdānām aśvaśabdādaśvādhyavasāyo gośabdācca gavyadhyavasāya iti vikalpaniyamo ghaṭate, dṛṣṭaścāsāviti । tathāśvaśabde 'pi sambandhāgrahe sambandhipratyayo na syādityalamativistareṇa ।

[II,174,25]

tadevaṃ tādātmyatadutpattipratibandhasya pūrvameva pratiṣedhāt śabdānāntu <II,175> samayavaśenārthapratipādakatvād upapannam anumānādarthāntaratve sati prāmāṇyamiti ।

[II,175,3]

(“prasiddhābhinayasya ceṣṭayā pratipattidarśanāt tadapyanumānameva”)

[II,175,4]

atha ceṣṭāpramāṇāntaramiti kecit, tanniṣedhārthamāha * prasiddhābhinayasya ceṣṭayā pratipattidarśanāt tadapyanumānameva * prasiddho 'bhinayaśceṣṭā kāyiko vyāpāro 'rthaviśeṣāvinābhūto yasyāsau tathoktaḥ, tasya ceṣṭayā arthaviśeṣe prati pattiḥ । yathā mukhāñjalisaṃya, gād viśiṣṭāt pipāsāpratipattiḥ, tasya tayā pūrvamavinābhāvopalabdheḥ । tathā ca, ayaṃ pipāsānvitaḥ, viśiṣṭamukhāñjali saṃyogavattvāt, tadanyaivaṃvidhadevadattavat । ataḥ pakṣadharmatvādibalena gamakatvād etadapyanumānameveti । evamanyāpi ceṣṭā nāṭyaśāstraprasiddhā anumāne 'ntarbhāvanīyeti ।

[II,175,12]

(“āptenāprasiddhagavayasya gavā gavayapratipādanādupamānamāptavacanameva ।”)

[II,175,13]

athopamānaṃ pramāṇāntaramiti kecit, taniṣedhārthamāha <x> āptenā prasiddhagavayasya gavā gavayapratipādanād upamānamāptavacanameva * iti । āptena prasiddhagogavayasārūpyeṇa aprasiddhagavayasya gavā gavayapratipāda nāditi । yathā gaurevaṃ gavaya ityupamānamiṣṭam । tad āptavacanameva na pramāṇāntaramiti । na cāsya upamārūpatvāt pramāṇāntaratvam, vidhyarthavādā dibhedenāpi pramāṇānantyaprasaṅgāt । atha satyapyavāntarabhede nāmīṣām āpto padeśād bhedaḥ, tadupamāne 'pi samānam ।

[II,175,20]

atha vākyādupalabdhasādṛśyasyāṭavyāmaṭato gavayārthito madīyā gauranena sadṛśīti jñānamupamānam, asadetat, phalābhāvāt । ajñānanivṛttiḥ phala mityuktam, nivṛtteḥ pradhvaṃsatvāt । tathā hi, yadi jñānānutpattiḥ, viparītaṃ vā jñānamajñānam ubhayathāpi tannivṛttiḥ pradhvaṃsa eva । pramājanakañca pramāṇam । na ca heyādibuddhayaḥ phalam, tadapāye sati kālāntareṇa sukhaduḥkhādiviniśca yānantaramutpattaḥ । na ca sādṛśyasya prameyatvam, tajjñānasyāphalatvāt । abhyu pagame vā anyat pramāṇaṃ vācyamiti ।

<II,176>

[II,176,1]

atha gavayajñānamupamānaṃ madīyā gauranena sadṛśīti jñānaphalam, sādṛśyā vacchinnaḥ piṇḍaḥ, tadavacchinnaṃ vā sādṛśyaṃ prameyamiti । na cedaṃ jñānamindri yajam, aṭavyāṃ vyavasthitasya gṛhāvasthitapiṇḍaviṣayatvenotpatteḥ । na cānu mānajam, liṅgavyāpārānupalabdheḥ । gosādṛśyantu gavaye gṛhyamāṇamapyasiddham, vyadhikaraṇatvāt । tathā ca, madīyā gauranena sadṛśī, asya tatsadṛśatvād iti vyadhikaraṇataiva । anupapadyamānasyārthasyābhāvād nārthāpattijam । śabda vināpyutpatterna śābdam । abhāvasya ca niyataviṣayatvam । na ceda smaraṇam, gavayasādṛśyasya gopiṇḍe pūrvamananubhūtatvāt । ataḥ pramāṇāntaraphalametadityā śayaḥ parasya ।

[II,176,10]

yadi ca gosādṛśyāvacchinnaṃ gavayapiṇḍam indriyārthasannikarṣādevopalabhyate, tadā pratyakṣaphalameva, na pramāṇāntaraphalam । tatra ki smaraṇāpekṣamindriyamevaṃ jñānaṃ janayati, anapekṣaṃ vā ? anapekṣasya jñānajanakatveprasiddhagopiṇḍasya smaraṇe 'pyetat syāt । atha piṇḍamātrasmaraṇe, aśvādipiṇḍasmaraṇe 'pi syāt, atha gavayasādṛśyāvacchinnasmaraṇāpekṣaṃ janakam, tatrāpi yadi smaraṇa mātramapekṣeta, gajādismaraṇe 'pi syāt । atha gopiṇḍasmaraṇāpekṣam, tatrāpi ki gopiṇḍamātrasmaraṇamapekṣate, gavayasādṛśyāvacchinnaṃ gopiṇḍasmaraṇaṃ vā । gopiṇḍamātrasmaraṇe 'śvādipiṇḍasmaraṇe 'pi ? ṇḍe 'pi syāt । gavayasādṛśyā vacchinnagopiṇḍasmaraṇāpekṣitve pūrvamevānubhavo vācyastadantareṇa saṃskārānutpatteḥ smaraṇasyaivābhāvāt । ataḥ savikalpakajñānābhāve 'pi gavayasādṛśyāvacchinne gopiṇḍe pūrvamanubhavo 'bhyupagantavyaḥ । yena hi saṃskārotpattau smaraṇād madīyayā gavā sadṛśo 'yaṃ gavaya iti jñānaṃ syāt । pūrvañca gavayasādṛśyāvacchinnagopiṇḍe 'nubhavaprasiddhau gavayopalambhād madīyā gauranena sadṛśīti kathametat smaraṇaṃ na syāt ? tathā pṛṣṭo bravīti etatsadṛśī mayopalabdhā, na tu pramāṇāntaraṃ nirdiśatīti manyamānaḥ praśasto bhagavān antarbhāvamāheti ।

[II,176,25]

anye tu yathā gaurgavayastatheti vanecaravākyāta sādṛśyopalambhe sati upajātasaṃskārasyāṭavyāṃ paribhramato gośādṛśyāvacchinnagavayadarśane sati avinābhāvasambandhasmaraṇānantaraṃ tathā cāyaṃ gosadṛśa iti jñānamupamānaṃ <II,177> manyante । tasmāccānantaraṃ gavayanā me?māyamiti saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhapratipattiḥ । phalaṃ saṃjñāsaṃjñirūpama, saṃjñāvacchinno vā piṇḍaḥ prameyamiti । na ca vākyādeva saṅketapratipattirgavayapiṇḍasya parokṣatvāt, “pratyakṣa saṃjñākarma” <= vai. sū0> iti sūtravyāghātācca ।

[II,177,5]

na yuktametat, vākyādeva saṅketasya pratītatvāt । tathā hi, sādṛśya vākyasyāyamartho yo gosadṛśaḥ, sa gavaya ityevaṃ vyavahartavyaḥ । sa ca vākyādupala bdhasaṅketaḥ sādṛśyāvacchinnaṃ piṇḍamupalabhamānaḥ paraṃ vyavaharati “ayaṃ gavayaḥ” iti, na tu saṅketaṃ pratipadyate pratipiṇḍam, anyatrāpi saṅketaprasaṅgāt । tathā hi, yatra yatra gotvaṃ paśyasi, tatra tatra gośabdaḥ prayoktavyaḥ, tasmācca asāvarthaḥ pratipattavya iti saṅketagrahe sati gopiṇḍopalambhādayaṃ gauriti pratipadyate, na tu gonā 〈 me ? māyami〉 ti, vyavahārābhāvaprasaṅgāt । na tu sūtravyāghātaḥ, pratyakṣaśabdasya dṛḍhapramāṇopalakṣaṇatvāt । dṛḍhapramāṇaparicchinne 'rthe saṃjñā pravartate । yathā deśāntaravyavasthito 'pi pitā svaputrasya nāma karoti “yajñadatta nāmāsau” iti ।

[II,177,15]

atha jātiśabdasya pratyakṣa evārthe saṅketaḥ, na, atīndriyeṣu asaṅketa prasaṅgāt । dṛṣṭañca manaḥ śabdasyātīndriye 'pi manasi dṛḍhapramāṇaparicchinne saṅketaḥ । tathā ayaṃ gavaya iti kathaṃ punarbhavān jānātīti pareṇa pṛṣṭo vane careṇa mamākhyātamiti vacanameva nirdiśati, na tu sādṛśyāt pratipannamiti । kārakeṇa ca vyapadeśaḥ । yathā cakṣuṣā pratipannamanumānācca pratipanna miti, tathā niviṣayavācyapramāṇamupamānam । athāsti saṃjñāsaṃjñirūpaṃ prameyam, na, sambandhapratipatteḥ phalatve sambandhinaḥ prameyatvānupapatteḥ । atha sambandha iva sambandhinaḥ pratipattireva ubhayaniṣṭhatayā upacāreṇābhidhīyate । tathāpi na saṃjñāsaṃjñirūpaṃ prameyam, saṃjñāyāstadabhāvāt । atha svayamuccārya śabdaṃ pratipadyate, na, vivakṣākrameṇa śabdotpattikāle sādṛśyajñānasya pramāṇasyāsambhavāt । atha jagato vistīrṇatayā kvacidutpanno gavayaśabdaḥ prameyaḥ, na, tasyāśrūyamāṇasya prameyatvānupapatteḥ । atha apratibandhanyāyena dūrasthasyāgamane brahmabhāṣitasyāgamanaṃ syāt ।

<II,178>

[II,178,1]

na ca sannihitaḥ kvacit tadaiva śabdamuccarati, asaṃvedanāt । atha smṛtisamāropitasya gavayaśabdasya prameyatvam, na, tatkalpanāyāṃ kāraṇābhāvāt । sādṛśyajñānānantaraṃ ayaṃ gavayanāmeti pratipadyate, na cāntarāle tatsmṛteranupraveśa pramāṇamastīti । saṃjñāvacchinnasya tu piṇḍasya prameyatvena sambandhajñānaṃ syāt, tasyobhayālambanatvāditi । tathā pareṇāpi anumānādupamānasya bhedamupadarśayatā “yathā tathetyupasaṃhārāpamānasiddharnā viśeṣaḥ” iti vākyarūpamupamānamiṣṭamava । tasya cāgame 'ntarbhāvo na doṣāyeti ।

[II,178,8]

(“darśanārthādarthāpattistadapyanumānameva ।”)

[II,178,9]

atha arthāpatteranumāne 'ntarbhāvārtha * darśanā dāpattistadapyanumāna meva * iti vākyam । dṛśyata iti darśanaṃ tasmādupalabhyamānādarthādanyathānuṣa padyamānād arthasyāptiḥ prāptiḥ prasaṅga iti । taduktam,
	pramāṇaṣaṭakavijñāto yatrārtho nānyathā bhavet /
	adṛṣṭaṃ kalpayedanyā sārthāpattirudāhṛtā //
	<= ślo. vā. 45. pṛ0>
iti ṣaḍbhedā arthāpattiḥ । tatra pratyakṣapūrvikā tū yathā sphoṭādilakṣaṇa kāryamupalabhya tadanyathānupapattyā vaḍherdāhikā śaktiḥ pratīyate । na cātra pramāṇāntareṇa avinābhāvagrahaṇam, śakteḥ pramāṇāntarāgocaratvāt । anupa labdhāvinābhāvaśca liṅgaṃ na bhavatyeva । ataḥ pramāṇāntarametat ।

[II,178,19]

anumānapūrvikā tu yathā dhūmādagni pratipadya tadanyathānupapattyā tadviśaṣa pratītiriti । upamānapūrvikā ca yathā aṭavyāṃ gavayadarśanāntaraṃ madīyā garinana sadṛśīti gāṃ pratipadya tadanyathānupapattyā vāhadohādisāmarthyapratipattiḥ । arthāpattipūrvikā tu rūpopalambhānyathānupapattyā avagatasya cakṣuṣaḥ paricchādakā śaktiḥ pratīyata iti । āgamapūrvikā tu jīvati devadatte gṛhe nāstāra vākyād gṛhe 'sattvaṃ pratipadya tadanyathānupapattyā bahirbhāvapratipattiḥ । na bahirbhāvāvinābhūtaṃ kiñcilliṅgamastīti pramāṇāntaraphalametat ।

<II,179>

[II,179,1]

abhāvavikā tu yathā sadupalambhakapramāṇapañcakavyāvṛttyā devadattasya gṛhe 'sattvaṃ pratipadya tadanyathānupapattyā bahirdeśasambandhaḥ pratīyate ।

[II,179,3]

antarbhāvamāha * tadapyanumānameva * na pramāṇāntaram । tathā ca sphāṭādikāryeṇa agneratīndriyā śaktiḥ pratīyate, ityasadetat, tasyāścaramasaha kārivyatirekeṇa pūrvameva pratiṣedhāt । pratibandhakābhāvaviśiṣṭo 'gnisaṃyoga eva agnaḥ śaktiḥ, tatsadbhāve kāryakaraṇāt । agnitvantu nijā śaktiḥ, sāpi pratyakṣava । yaccānumānāta sāmānyāvabodhe satyāpattito viśeṣāvabodha iti, tapāstameva, sāmānyaviśeṣasya sādhyatvāditi vadatā । upamānasya tu smara śādarbhade 'pi tatpūrvikārthāpattiranumānameva, vyāpteḥ pūrvameva grahaṇāt । tathā ca sādṛśyāvacchinno gopiṇḍo vāhādisamarthaḥ, tatpiṇḍatvāt pūrvopalabdhaivaṃvidha gāpiṇḍavat । arthāpattipūrvikāpi arthāpattiranumitānumānameva । tathā ca rūpo palāndhaḥ karaṇakāryā kriyātvāt, chidikriyāvaditi । cakṣuḥ prasiddham, saccānumitaṃ śaktimat karaṇatvāt vāsyādivaditi ।

[II,179,14]

yā ceyaṃ jīvati devadatte gṛhe nāstītyanyathānupapattyā bahirbhāvapratipattiḥ, tāpyanumānameva, vyāpteḥ pūrvameva grahaṇāt । tathā hi devadatto bahirdeśasambandhī jāvanasambandhitve sati gṛhe 'nupalabhyamānatvād viṣṇumitravat । jīvanasamba dhitvañca devadattasya arthāpattivādināpi āgamādeva pratipattavyam, anyathā athopattirna pravartata । samānañcaitadabhāvapūrvikāyāmapyarthāpattāviti ।

[II,179,19]

pramāṇapañcakābhāvenāpi jīvato devadattasya gṛhe 'sattvapratipattau bahirdeśa sambandho 'numīyate । evamanyadapyudāharaṇamarthāpatteravirābhāvopadarśanena anumāna eva antarbhāvanīyama, tathotpatti vinā anyathānupapatterupadarśayitumaśakyatvāditi ।

[II,179,23]

atha virodhinaḥ sādevispharjanādiśabdaśravaṇād tadanumitau virodhinyeva kulādau pratipattiḥ pramāṇāntaramiṣṭaṃ kaiścit । tadanumitānumānameva, cāptaḥ pūrvameva grahaṇāt । prayogastu vispharjanaśabdo bhujaṅgakāryoṃ visphūrjana śabdatvāt pūrvopalabdhaivaṃvidhavispharjanaśabdavat । evamanumitaḥ sarpaḥ sannihitena parādhinā tadvān, vispharjanaśabdakartatvāt pūrvopalabdhaivaṃvidhāhivaditi ।

<II,180>

[II,180,1]

(“sambhavo 'pyavinābhāvitvādanumānameva ।”)

[II,180,2]

sambhavaḥ pramāṇāntaramiṣṭaṃ paraiḥ । tanniṣedhārthaṃ * sambhavo 'pyavinā bhāvitvādanumānameva * iti vākyam । yatra hi sahasraṃ tatrāvaśyaṃ śataṃ sambhava tītyavinābhāvasya grahaṇāt । tathā ca sahasraṃ svasamudāyi śatavat sahasratvāt pūrvopalabdhasahasravat ।

[II,180,6]

(“abhāvo 'pyanumānameva । yathā utpanna kārya kāraṇasabhāve liṅgam, evamanutpanna kārya kāraṇāsadbhāve liṅgam ।”)

[II,180,8]

kāryānatpādena kāraṇābhāvaḥ pratīyata ityabhāvarūpatayaiva pramāṇāntaramiti kecit । taniṣedhārthaṃ na paraṃ sambhavaḥ * abhāvo 'pyanamānameva * iti । * yathā utpannaṃ kārya kāraṇasadbhāve liṅgam * avinābhāvasya pūrvameva grahṇāt, tathā * anutpanna kārya kāraṇāsadbhāve * kāryānutpādasya kāraṇābhāvenāvyabhicārāt । tathā ca kāryānatpattiḥ kāraṇābhāvavatī kāryānatpattitvād ubhayābhimata kāryānutpattivat ।

[II,180,14]

atha sadupalambhakapramāṇapañcakavyāvṛttyā vastuno 'bhāvasya grahaṇamiti pramāṇāntaramabhāvaḥ । yathā hi, bhāvāṃśaparicchede bhāvasya vyāpārastathā tadabhāvaparicchede abhāvasyāpyabhyupagantavyaḥ । taduktam,
	pratyakṣādyavatārastu bhāvāṃśo grahyate yadā /
	vyāpārastadabhāvasyāpyabhāvāṃśe jighṛkṣate //
	<= ślo. vā. pṛ. 478>

[II,180,20]

tathā hi, na pratyakṣeṇābhāvasya grahaṇam , tena sambandhābhāvāt ।
	sambaddhaṃ vartamānañca gṛhyate cakṣurādinā /
	<= ślo. vā. pṛ. 160>

[II,180,23]

pratyakṣābhāvādanamānasyāpya pravṛttiḥ, tasya sambandhigrahaṇāpekṣitvāt । evaṃ śabdasyāpi । upamānārthāpattyoścāvyāpārāta pramāṇapañcakābhāvana prameyābhāvasya grahaṇamiti । taduktam,
<II,181>
	pramāṇapañcakaṃ yatra vasturūpe na jāyate /
	vastusattāvabodhārthaṃ tatrābhāvapramāṇatā //
	<= ślo. vā. pṛ. 473>

[II,181,4]

nanvevaṃ tarhi vyavahite 'pyarthe pramāṇapañcakavyāvṛtteḥ sadbhāvādabhāvagrahaṇa saḥ । na, vastugrahaṇapratiyogismaraṇāderapi vyāpārāt । taduktam,
	gṛhītvā vastusadbhāvaṃ smṛtvā ca pratiyoginam /
	mānasaṃ nāstitājñānaṃ jāyate 'kṣānapekṣayā //
	<= ślo. vā. pṛ. 482>

[II,181,9]

vastuno bhūtalādeḥ sadbhāvaṃ gṛhītvā pratiyoginaṃ ghaṭañca smṛtvā indriya pāra vinaiva manasā pratipadyate neha bhūtale ghaṭo 'stīti । tathā devakulaṃ dṛṣṭavā hānagato hastinā deśāntaravyavadhānād indriyasambandhaṃ vināpi pareṇa pṛṣṭastadaiva hastinaḥ nāstitāṃ pratipadyate । taduktam,
	vastumātraṃ gṛhītvāpi paścāt kiñcit smarannapi /
	tatrānyenāstitāṃ pṛṣṭastadaiva pratipadyate //
	<= ślo. vā. pṛ. 483>

[II,181,16]

tathā,
	pratyakṣāderanutpattiḥ pramāṇābhāva ucyate /
	sātmanaḥ pariṇāmo vā vijñānaṃ vānyavastunī //
	<= ilo. vā. pṛ. 475>

[II,181,20]

sarvametadasat, pratyakṣādinaiva abhāvasya pratīteḥ । tathā ca, akṣavyāpārād 19 mūtale ghaṭo nāstīti jñānama aparokṣamatpadyamānaṃ dṛṣṭam । atha indriyāṇāṃ bhūtalagrahaṇe vyāpāro nābhāva iti cet, na, bhūtalagrahaṇe pramāṇābhāvāt । viśeṣaṇasya hi pūrva grahaṇaṃ paścāda viśeṣyasya, bhūtalañca viśeṣyamiti na tasya pūrvaṃ grahaṇe pramāṇamasti । upetyavādena tūcyate, yadi vastumātragrahaṇe sati pratiyogismaraṇaṃ ghaṭāvaruddhabhatalopalambhe 'pi tatsmaraṇe nāstitājñānaprasaṅgaḥ । <II,182> atha viśiṣṭa vastugrahaṇe sati pratiyogismaraṇam, tarhi yena viśeṣaṇena viśiṣṭa tada vastu pūrva pratipattavyamiti kim indriyādeva pratīyate, prāmāṇāntarād veti । indriyādeva pratipattyabhyupagame kathaṃ nābhāvaḥ pratyakṣaviṣayo viśiṣṭatā yāstadrūpatvāt । na cānumānādeāpāre pramāṇamasti ।

[II,182,5]

yadi ca anyayā pramāṇapañcakavyāvṛttyaiva viśiṣṭatā pratīyate, tatrāpyanya vastugrahaṇābhyupagame viśiṣṭatāgrahaṇamevābhyupeyamityanavasthā syāt । tasmādi ndriyeṇaiva itarapadārthaviviktaṃ bhūtalamupalabhya pratiyoginaṃ smaratītyabhyupagama ghaṭābhāvasya pratotatvād alaṃ pramāṇapañcakavyāvṛttyeti ।

[II,182,9]

sadaṃśaprakāśakasyaiva asadaṃśe 'pyanvayavyatirekābhyāṃ vyāpāropalabdhana pramāṇapañcakāparicchedya vastuni abhāvasya pramāṇateti vācyam । na cendriyaṇa sambandhābhāvādagrahaṇam, tasya kāryeṇaiva sadbhāvasiddheḥ । tathā ca pareṇāpi aparokṣajñānasadbhāvena indriyāryayoryogyatālakṣaṇaḥ sambandho 'bhyupagataḥ, saca rūpādāvi vābhā ve 'pyabhyupagantavyaḥ, kāryasyobhayatrāviśeṣāt tathā vaiśeṣikarīpa aparokṣajñānasadbhāvena indriyārthayoḥ ghoḍhā sambandho 'bhyupagata ityabhāvana viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvo 'styeva, tena hi satā aparokṣajñānotpatteḥ ।

[II,182,16]

sadupalambhakapramāṇapañcakavyāvṛttyā tu abhāvagrahaṇe kathaṃ ṣaḍeva pramāṇānā tyavadhāraṇam, pramāṇāgrahe tasyānupapatteḥ । na hi sadupalambhakapramāṇābhāvasya paricchedyatve anyat tasya paricchedakaṃ pramāṇamasti । atha pramāṇapañcakā bhāvasthānekatvāt kaścit kasyacid grāhako bhavati ? evaṃ tarhi tasyāpyanyana grahaṇaṃ tasyāpyanenetyanavasthā syāt । na ca pramāṇavyaktaranekatvāt tadagraha" tanniṣṭhasya ṣaḍevetyavadhāraṇasya sambhavaḥ syāt । vaiśeṣikāṇāntu pramāṇavyā nāmānantye 'pi eka lakṣaṇamupagrāhakamastīti yuktaṃ pramāṇagrahaṇaṃ savāra dhāraṇamiti ।

[II,182,24]

yaccedaṃ devakūlamātraṃ dṛṣṭavā niṣkrānto 'nyena pṛṣṭastadeva hastyādernāstitā pratipadyata ityuktam, tanna, asya smaraṇatvāt । yadyapi pūrvaṃ hastītyādi savikalpakaṃ jñānaṃ notpannama; tathāpi hastyādyabhāvaviśiṣṭe devakule nirvi<II,183>kalpaka jñānamutlannam । anyathā hi yadāhaṃ devakulamadrākṣam, na tadā taṃ samīpa pātana hastinamiti praśnānantaraṃ smaraṇaṃ na syāt । tattu dṛṣṭam । yasya pastunaḥ pūrvaṃ nābhāvaḥ paricchinnastatra parapraśnānantaraṃ saṃśete, na nirīkṣitaṃ mayā ki tatra devadatto 'sti uta nāstīti । na cedānīmabhāvaṃ niścinoti bhāgamasyāpi pramāṇāntareṇārthatathābhāvapratipattiḥ । nāptopadeśena kadācit sambhavāt । ataḥ pūrvameva hastyādyabhāvasya pratīteryuktametat smaraṇaṃ na mayā tatra 9 dṛṣṭa ityādi । abhāvasya ca prameyatvaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgāvasare vyavasthāpitameveti ।

[II,183,8]

(“tathaitihyamapyavitathamāptopadeśa eveti ।”)

[II,183,9]

atha anirdiṣṭapravaktakaṃ pravādapāramparya yathā iha vaṭe yakṣaḥ prativasatīti, cāpa yadi pramāṇāntareṇa arthatathābhāvapratipattirna āptopadeśāvarthāntaratva syāha tathaitihyamavitathamāptopadeśa eva । tathā hi pūrvapramāṇāni nārthāntaram, tathā aitihyamapi avitathaṃ yathārthamāptopadeśa eva, na pramāṇāntaram । viparyaye tu aprāmāṇyamiti ।

[II,183,14]

(“pañcāvayavena vākyena svaniścitārthapratipādanaṃ parārthānumānam । vayavenaiva vākyena saṃśayitaviparyastāvyutpannānāṃ pareṣāṃ svaniścitārtha tipādanaṃ parārthānumānaṃ vijñeyam ।”)

[II,183,17]

atha prāk sūcitasya parārthānumānasya vyākaraṇārthaṃ * pañcāvayavena ityādi prakaraṇam । parārthānumiti〈riti〉lakṣyanirdeśaḥ । * pañcāvayavena vākyena svaniścitārthapratipādanam * iti lakṣaṇam । svaniścitārthaḥ sādhyaḥ, pratipādyate 'neneti svaniścitārthapratipādanaṃ liṅgam, tat pañcāvayavena vākyena sahitaṃ parārthamanumānam । pratipattirvā pratipādanam, svaniścitārthaviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ pañcāvayavena vākyena janitam, yataḥ kārakasamūhād bhavati tat parārthānumānamiti sādhyā vākyārthavādinā vyākhyānam । liṅgavākyārthapakṣe tu arthyate 'nenetyartho liṅgam, pratipādyata iti pratipādanam, pañcāvayavena kākyena pratipādyamānaṃ liṅgaṃ parārthānumānamiti । yadvā svaniścitārthapratipattiḥ pratipādanam, tacca pañcāvayavena vākyena janitaṃ parārthānumānamiti ।

<II,184>

[II,184,1]

nanvetasmin pakṣe kathaṃ svārthād viśiṣyate parārthānumānam, cakṣurādinā śabdena vā liṅga pratipadya tasmāt sādhyaṃ pratipadyata iti kutaḥ svārthaparārtha iti bhedaḥ ? na ca parasampāditācchabdālliṅga pratipadyata iti viśeṣaḥ, cakṣurāderapi parasampāditatvāt śabdarūpatāvailakṣaṇyantu vaidharmyamātrameva । ataḥ sādhyavākyārthapakṣo doṣānupapatte(ra?)āhya iti । tathā ca kevalaṃ liṅgaṃ cakṣarādinā pratipannaṃ sādhyapratipattau svārthānumānamaśabdasahitam, śabdasahitantu parārthānumānamiti viśeṣaḥ । tasmādityanena samarthaliṅgaparāmarśānantaram anitya evāyam iti sādhyapratipatteḥ saṃvedanācca sādhyameva vākyārthaḥ । tasmādityevamantameva vākyam । śeṣañca abhiprāyanivedanamiti, na tvārtham, sādhyavākyārthapakṣe bādhakānupapatterityalamativistareṇa ।

[II,184,11]

pūrvasya saṅgrahavākyasya vivaraṇam ‘pañcāvayavenaiva vākyena, na vyavayavena daśāvayavena veti । keṣām ? * saṃśayitaviparītā ? yastā vyutpannānām * svaniścitārthapratipādanaṃ parārthānumānaṃ vijñeyam ।

[II,184,14]

atha niravayavatvād vākyasyānupapannametat pañcāvayaveneti । tathā ca varṇānāṃ na samuditānāmarthapratipādakatvam, kramabhāvināmāśuvināśitvena samudāyāsambhavāt । na vyastānām, ekasmādevārthapratītāvanyeṣāmuccāraṇa vaiyarthyāt । upalabhyate ca śabdād uccaritārthapratipattiḥ । atastadanyathānupa pattyā varṇakalāpādatiricyamānaḥ sphoṭātmā pratīyata iti । tathā gauriti śabdoccāraṇād abhinnākāraṃ vijñānaṃ śrotravyāpārādutpadyamānaṃ dṛṣṭam । na cedaṃ saṃśayaviparyayavyatirekādavayavijñānavad abhinnamarthaṃ vinā bhavatīti । varṇoccā raṇantu sphoṭasvarūpābhivyaktaye kriyata iti na vyartham ।

[II,184,22]

asadetat, pūrvavarṇānugṛhītasyāntyavarṇasya svānubhavasahakāriṇo 'rthaprati pādakatvāt । yathā ca, ekasmin varṇe jñānam, tena kriyate saṃskāraḥ; punarvi tīyavarṇa jñānam, tenāpi pūrvavarṇasaṃskārasahakāriṇā saṃskāra iti krameṇa antyavarṇajñānam, tasmāt pūrvasaṃskārābhivyaktāvaśeṣavarṇānusmaraṇe sati antya varṇādarthapratipattiḥ । na caivaṃ ghaṭādyanubhavajanitasaṃskārasya anubhavāntarasahakāriṇaḥ saṃskārārambhakatvenātiprasaṅgaḥ, tatra viśiṣṭādṛṣṭābhāvāt । tadabhāvastu kāryā<II,185>bhāvenaiva jñāyata iti । atra ca kāryasya sadbhāvād viśiṣṭo 'dṛṣṭaḥ kāraṇatvena kalpyata iti ।

[II,185,3]

anye tu śabdārthopabhogaprāpakādṛṣṭaniyamitāḥ pūrvavarṇānubhavajanita saṃskārāḥ pūrvavarṇeṣvekaṃ smaraṇamārabhante tatsahakārī cāntyo varṇaḥ padam । yadvā saṃskāramekaṃ vicitramārabhante, tasmācca pūrvavarṇeṣvekaṃ smaraṇamiti ।

[II,185,6]

anye tu pūrvavarṇānāṃ tajjñānānāñca atītānāmapi antyavarṇasahakāri tvam, anvayavyatirekopapatteḥ । yathā hi, vartamānasya kāraṇatvam anvayavyatire kābhyāṃ vijñātam, evamatītasyāpīti । yad vā pūrvavarṇavināśāstajjñāna pradhvaṃsāśca samīpatino 'ntyavarṇasahakāriṇa iti kṣīṇārthāpattiḥ । evaṃvidha kalpanānabhyupagame ca varṇoccāraṇavaiyarthyameva syāt । na ca sphoṭābhivyakta ? akamuccāraṇam, samastavyastavikalpānupapatteḥ । na samastairabhivyajyate, samudāyānabhyupagamāt, na vyastaiḥ, ekenaivābhivyaktau śeṣoccāraṇavaiyarthya prasaṅgāt । atha kalpanā āśrīyate, sā arthapratipattāvapi samarthetyalaṃ sphoṭaparikalpanayā । abhinnākārañca jñānamantyavarṇaviṣayaṃ varṇatvaviṣayaṃ vā ।

[II,185,15]

yad vā ghanāvasthitipratyakṣeṣviva varṇeṣu bhrāntamabhinnākāraṃ vijñāna miti na sphoṭasiddhiḥ । śabdābhivyaktāviva sphoṭābhivyaktāvapi doṣā iti samānatayā śabdaparīkṣāyāmevābhidhāsyanta ityalam ।

[II,185,18]

vākyakalpanā tvekasmin pade jñānasyotpādaḥ, saṃskārasya saṅkatasmara ṇasya ca utpadyamānatā, tataḥ saṃskārasya saṅketasmaraṇasya ca utpādaḥ, padārtha pratipatterutpadyamānatā, padajñānasya vinaśyattā, tataḥ padārthapratipatterutpattiḥ, smaraṇasya vinaśyattā, padajñānasya vināśaḥ, saṃskārasya dvitīyapadajñānasya ca utpadyamānatā, tato dvitīyapadajñānasyotpādaḥ, pūrvasaṃskārasacivena padārtha jñānena saṃskārasyotpādaḥ, saṃskārāntarasyotpadyamānatā saṅketasmaraṇasyā pyutpadyamānatā, padārthapratipattevinaśyattā, pūrvasaṅketasmaraṇasya vināśaḥ, tato dvitīyapadajñānasaṃskārasyotpādaḥ saṅketasmaraṇasyāpyutpādaḥ, padajñānasya vinaśyattā, padārthapratipatterutpadyamānatā, pūrvapadārthapratipavināśa ityayaṃ <II,186> nyāyastāvad yāvadantyapade jñānam । tena ca kalpanayā tatsaṃskārābhivyaktera śeṣapadārthaviṣayaṃ smaraṇaṃ janyate । tena ca svānubhavena ca viśiṣṭamantyapadameva vākyam, tasmācca vākyārthapratipattiriti ।

[II,186,4]

nanu padajñānotpatteḥ pūrvam adṛṣṭavaśāt padapadārthaviṣayasmaraṇotpādābhyupa game tasya padajñānāt saṅketasmaraṇakāle nāvasthānamiti padārthapratipatterūdhva kathaṃ vākyārthapratipattiḥ ? na ca padārthapratipatti vinaiva vākyārthapratipattiḥ, adarśanāt । atha padajñānādūcaṃ kalpanayā tatsaṃskāreṇa smaraṇaṃ janyate tataḥ padajñānasya vinaśyatteti saṅketasmaraṇakāle tasyānavasthānāt padārthapratipattya bhāve na vākyārthapratipattiriti dūṣaṇaṃ tadavasthameva ?

[II,186,10]

asadetat, vākye saṅketānupapatteḥ । antyapadaṃ vākyameva, tad antyārthastu vākyārtha iti । yadā ca pūrvavarṇatajjñānādūrdhvaṃ kalpanayā tatsaṃskāreṇa smaraṇa janyate, tataḥ padajñānasya vinaśyatteti saṅketasmaraṇābhāvaviśiṣṭo 'ntyo vaṇaḥ padam, tadeṣā kākyakalpanā । anyathā pūrvavarṇeṣu jñānadvāreṇa saṃskārād vicitrasmaraṇānugṛhīto 'ntyo varṇaḥ padamityabhyupagamena padārthajñānānantara padajñānaṃ syāt, varṇajñānavyavadhānāt ।

[II,186,16]

anye tu pūrvārthasya pratisamādhānārthamantyapadajñānānantaraṃ kalpanayā tatsaṃskāraḥ saṅketānubhavajanitasaṃskāraśca ekaṃ smaraṇamārabhate, tataḥ padātha jñānasyotpādaḥ, padajñānasya vinaśyattā, smaraṇānubhavayoścāvirodha iti । tataḥ smaraṇānubhavaviśiṣṭād antyapadād vākyārthapratipattiriti ।

[II,186,20]

anye tu yadyapyantyapadajñānānantaraṃ saṅketasmaraṇāt padārthāvabodhe sāta padajñānaṃ vinaṣṭam, tathāpi punastasminneva jñānamutpadyate, tataḥ kalpanayā tatsaṃskārāt smaraṇotpāde sati antyapadād vākyārthapratipattiriti ।

[II,186,23]

asadetat, śabdasya viramya vyāpārapratiṣedhāt । ekadā padaṃ svaviṣaya jñānaṃ kṛtvā punarna karotīti ।

[II,186,25]

anye tu pratijñādipadasya padāntaroccāraṇakāle 'pi ākāśe padānta rambhakatvenāvasthānaṃ tāvad yāvadantyapadama, tataḥ pañcabhiḥ padaiḥ śrāpadeśe <II,187> vākyam avayavibhūtamārabhyate, tato vākyārthapratipattiriti । nirastañcaitad anubhavana । na hi pūrvapūrvapadasyottarottarapadakāle sarveṣāñca vākyakāle 'nubhavo 'stīti ।

[II,187,4]

anya tu ekasmin pade jñānam, tena kriyate saṃskāraḥ, pudvitīyapadajñānam, tena prāktanena saṃskāreṇānyaḥ saṃskāra iti tāvad yāvadantyapade śānamiti; tataḥ prāktanasaṃskārābhivyaktī padacatuṣṭayaviṣaya smaraṇamutmayate, tadviśiṣṭañcāntyapadaṃ vākyamiti । na cātrānubhavena virādhaḥ, karaṇāṃśasyaiv kīrtanāt ।

[II,187,9]

anya smaraṇenānubhavasyāvirodhaṃ manyamānāḥ kalpanāmāśrayante । padajñānāt sakatasmaraṇasyotpādaḥ, padārthapratipatterutpadyamānatā, tataḥ padārthajñānasyotpādaḥ pūrvapadajñānasya vinaśyattā, dvitīyapadajñānasyotpadyamānatā, tato dvitīyapadajñānasyotpādaḥ, padārthajñānasya vinaśyattā, padajñānasya vināśaḥ, saṅketasmaraṇasyotpadyamānatetyanena krameṇa antyapadajñāne sati vākyārthapratipattiḥ । na cātra pūrvapadapadārthānasmaraṇena prayojanamasti, tatkāyasya vinaśyadaśānanaṃva kṛtatvāt । pūrvapadānurakte hi dvitīyapade jñānamutpannam, tadanuraktaṃ tṛtīyapadamiti aśeṣapadānuraktam antyapada vākyamiti ।

[II,187,17]

etaccāsat, pūrvapadānurāgasyāntyapade 'pratibhāsanāt । yathā hi, daṇḍīti jñānaṃ daṇḍānuraktameva, naivaṃ dvitīyādipadajñānaṃ pūrvapadānuraktamiti । na cāyaṃ niyamaḥ sambhavati pūrvapadānantarameva dvitīyādipadoccāraṇam, katipayakālavyavadhānapi uccāraṇe 'rthapratipattidarśanāditi pūrvaiva kalpanā nyāyyā ।

[II,187,21]

athāstvevaṃ vākyaparikalpanā vācakatvantu niṣidhyata, anyavyatirekābhāvāt । padārthabhyastu vākyārthapratipattiḥ । yatra hi pramāṇāntareṇāpi padārthaprasiddhistatrāntareṇāpi vākyaṃ vākyārthaprattipatirdṛṣṭā । yathā,
	paśyataścakṣuṣā rūpaṃ heṣāśabdaśca śṛṇvataḥ /
	khuranikṣepaśabdañca śveto 'śvo dhāvatīti dhīḥ //
	<= ślo. vā. pṛ. 94>

<II,188>

[II,188,1]

tathā ca dūrāccakṣuṣā śvetaṃ rūpamupalabhya heṣāśabdena vā aśvatvajāti manuminoti, khuranikṣepaśabdena ca dhāvanakriyāmavagatya vākyaṃ vināpi vākyārtha pratipadyate । satyapi ca vākye padārthānāmapratipatterna vākyārthaprati pattiḥ, yathā prasiddhapadārthaiḥ kaviiivaracite vākya iti । tasmādabhihita. padārthānām ākāṅkṣāyogyatāsannidhidvāreṇa vākyārthagamakatvamiti ।

[II,188,6]

na yuktametat, śabdasyāprāmāṇyaprasaṅgāt । tathā ca padarūpasya tāvad aprāmāṇyam, anuvādakatvāt । taduktam,
	padamabhyadhikābhāvāt smārakānna viśiṣyate /
	yaccādhikyaṃ bhavedetat sa padasya na gocaraḥ //
	<= ślo. vā. pṛ. 412>

[II,188,11]

vākyantu pāramparyeṇāpyavācakamiti kathaṃ śabdaḥ pramāṇaṃ syāt ? atha padairabhihitānāñca padārthānāṃ gamakatvāditi pāramparyeṇa śabdaḥ pramāṇam ? tāha śrotraparicchinnasya śabdasyārthaparicchede vyāpārāditi pāramparyeṇa pratyakṣasyāpi codanāviṣaye sannidhiprāmāṇyopapatteḥ kathaṃ codanaiva dharma pramāṇam । pramāṇamava codaneti nāsyāvadhāraṇasya vyāghātaḥ । vākyasyārthaparicchedakatvānabhyupagame ca pramāṇāntarāsambhavāt padārthānāṃ pratyakṣādiṣvantarbhāvaścintanīyaḥ ।

[II,188,17]

tatrendriyārthasannikarṣeṇa saha vyāpārānupalabdherna pratyakṣe 'ntarbhāvaḥ । avi nābhāvasyānupapatternānumāne । anupapadyamānārthāsambhavānnārthāpattau । upamānā, bhāvayośca niyataviṣayatvameva । pramāṇāntarasya ca anabhyupagamādayuktametat ।

[II,188,20]

na ca padānāṃ svārthapratipattāveva caritārthatvama. uktanyāyena vākyātha pratipattāvapi vyāpārāt । viramya vyāpārastu ekamarthaṃ pratipādya punastama pratipādayantīti pratiṣiddhaḥ ।

[II,188,23]

yaccedaṃ vināpi vākyaṃ vākyārthapratipattirityuktam, tadaparijñānāt । vākyena hi janitā vākyārthapratipattiḥ, pratyakṣānumānasampāditāḥ śvetā72. dhāvatīti buddhayaḥ । yadapīdaṃ padārdhāpratipattau satyapi vākyena vākyā pratipattiriti, tadasat, pūrvapadārthasmaraṇānugṛhītasya antyapadasya vākyatvā avaśyamarthapratipādakatvamiti vyabhicārābhāvaḥ ।

<II,189>

[II,189,1]

anvitābhidhānantu na sarvapadānām, ekenaiva kriyākārakasaṃsargānvitasya padārthasyābhidhāne śeṣapadoccāraṇavaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt । atha antyaṃ padamanvitābhidhāyakam ? tasyāpi pūrvapadānapekṣitve taduccāraṇavaiyarthyam, sāpekṣitve tu na asmatsiddhāntād bhedaḥ ।

{§ avayavoddeśaḥ pratijñāvaidharmyañca}

[II,189,6]

(“avayavāḥ punaḥ pratijñāpadeśanidarśanānusandhānapratyāmnāyāḥ । tatrā yādaśo 'virodhī pratijñā । pratipipādayiṣitadharmaviśiṣṭasya rdhāmaṇoḍa śaviṣayamāpādayitum uddeśamānaṃ pratijñā । yathā dravyaṃ vāyuriti ।”)

[II,189,9]

(“āvarodhigrahaṇāta pratyakṣānamānābhyupagatasvaśāstrasvavacanavirodhino nayāddaśā nirastā bhavanti । yathā anuṣṇo 'gniriti, pratyakṣavirodhī. nambaram ityanumānavirodho, brāhmaṇena surā peyā ityāgamavirodho, vaiśeṣikasya sat kāryam iti bruvataḥ svaśāstravirodhī, na śabdo 'rthapratyāyaka iti svavacanavirodhī ।”)

[II,189,14]

ke punaravayavāstadāha * pratijñāpadeśanidarśanānusandhānapratyāmnāyāḥ * vākyadeśatvāt । na punaḥ paropagatā jijñāsādayaḥ, teṣāmaśabdarūpatvāt ।

[II,189,16]

tata upadeśakrameṇāvasaraprāptāyāḥ pratijñāyāstāvallakṣaṇamacyate * anumeyoddeśo 'virodhī pratijñā * iti । anumeyaḥ pratipipādāya vārāṣṭatā hi astitvādyapekṣayā sarvapadārtheṣvastoti pratipipādayiṣita । yo hi dharmaḥ pratipādayitumiṣṭaḥ, tadviśiṣṭo dharmī pakṣaḥ । tasyoddeśamātraṃ sādhāvaruddhaṃ pareṣāma aniścitārthābhidhāyakaṃ vacanaṃ pratijñeti । apadeśasya "vaṣayāpādanam arthaḥ prayojanamasyeti prayojanopanyāsaḥ । prayogastu, pratijñā 2tarasmād bhidyate, pratyakṣādyaviruddhānumeyoddeśatvāt, yastu na bhidyate, na pāsāvevaṃ yathā udāharaṇādiriti । anumeyoddeśo vā pratijñeti vyavahartavyaḥ, kānumeyoddeśatvāt, yaścaivaṃ na vyavahriyate, na cāsāvevam, yathā apadeśa iti । udāharaṇantu * yathā dravyaṃ vāyuriti * ।

[II,189,26]

nanu ca asādhanāṅgaṃ pratijñāvacanama, tadantareṇāpi sambandhavacanamātrā<II,190>darthapratīteḥ । tathā hi, yad yat kṛtakam, tattad anityaṃ dṛṣṭam, yathā ghaṭaḥ, tathā ca kṛtakaḥ śabda ityatra sāmarthyādeva pratijñārthasiddhayarthaṃ tadabhidhānam । atra ca prameyasya pramāṇenaiva siddheḥ sāmarthya kiṃrūpamiti cintyam । na pratyakṣa svarūpam, indriyārthasannikarṣaṇa vipratipattiviṣayasyāparicchedāt । evamāga menāpīti । athānumānameva sāmarthya tadavaśyamarthapratipattau pakṣadharmatvādikama pekṣata iti pratijñāvacanamantareṇa sapakṣāsapakṣāpravibhāge sati tadarthāpratītana gamakamiti । atha abhidhīyamānānumānavyatirekeṇa anyadanumānaṃ prastutānumāna sāmarthyam, na, tasyāpi avinābhāvānapekṣitve na gamakatvam, pratijñāvacanacca vinā tadarthāpratīteriti pūrvadoṣānuṣaṅgāt । na cābhipretārthapratipādanāya anumānopanyāsakāle tadarthasiddhaye 'numānāntaraṃ paśyāmaḥ ।

[II,190,11]

na ca kṛtakatvānityatvayoḥ sāmānyena vyāptyabhidhāne samarthasādhanasya śabda evopasaṃhārād vijñāyate atraivānityatvam asyābhipretamiti, sambandhābhi dhānasya viruddhāviruddhābhiprāyeṇāpi samānatayā vivekapratipatterabhāvaprasaṅgāt ।

[II,190,14]

atha yadyat kṛtakaṃ tattannityaṃ dṛṣṭamiti vyāptivacane viruddhavādī, anityatvena ca kṛtakatvasya vyāptivacane tattvavādīti viniścayaḥ, tanna, kṛtakatvanityatvayoppteḥ pratipādayitumaśakyatvāt । tathā ca, na kṛtakaṣu ghaṭādiṣu nityatvam, nityeṣu cākāśādiṣu kṛtakatvamiti dṛṣṭāntadoṣaṇa gatārthatvāt kathaṃ viruddhatvam ? yadā ca nityaḥ śabda iti pratijñāya kṛtakatvā nityatvayorvyāpti brūte, tadā abhipretārthaviparītena vyāptikathanād viruddha vādyayamiti viśeṣādhyavasāyo bhavatyeva ।

[II,190,21]

nanu nityā nityābhiprāyeṇaivāpi nityaḥ śabda iti vacanasambhavāt pratijñā vacane satyapi tattvātattvavādinoraniścaya eva, na, vacanenaivābhiprāyaviśeṣa prasiddhaḥ । na hi vaktṛṇāṃ vacanādṛte 'bhiprāyāvabodhe pramāṇāntaramastīti nitya vacanānnityābhiprāya eva niścīyate, abhiprāyāntarakalpanāyāṃ pramāṇābhāvāt ' ata eva vādiprativādinorjayaparājayavyavasthā prāśnikaiḥ kriyate । yatrāpyayana pratipadyamānā vicitrābhiprāyatayā prakaraṇārthamanyathā bravate, tatrāpi vā viśeṣeṇaiva abhiprāyaviśeṣo 'numeyaḥ, vivakṣāntarād vacanāntarānutpattaḥ । <II,191> abhyupagame vā sambandhavacanādapi aniścaya eva syāt kiṃ nitya tva palakṣātaḥ kṛtakatvānityatvayoḥ sambandhavacanama, uta anityatvavivakṣāta iti ।

[II,191,3]

atha hetutadabhāvavyavasthāyā vāstavasambandhāpekṣitvād viparītavivakṣayāpi pakatvānityatvayorastyeva sambandha iti gamakatvam ? tarhi nityatvābhiprāyeṇāpi evasambandhamupadarśayataḥ tattvavāditvaṃ syāt, prakārāntareṇa sambandho sanasyavābhāvāt । tathā pratijñāvacanaṃ vinā sandigdhaviparyastāvyutpannapuruṣa pāṇā prameyaviśeṣeṣu ākāṅkṣāpratipattau vādino viśeṣeṇa puruṣamātrasya mātrapratipādanāya pravartamānasya unmattavāditvaṃ syāta ।

[II,191,9]

atha vivādāt puruṣaviśeṣasya prameyaviśeṣāpekṣitvapratipattiḥ ? tarhi । abhyupagataiva, vivādasya tadrapatvāt । pratijñā hi pratiyogipratijñāntarama yā vivādaḥ, sādhanasahitā tu pratijñeti । na ca śāstrādeva yathokta pratipattiḥ, anamānopanyāsakāle tasyāpramāṇatvāta, prāmāṇye vā mānanati ? tasmāta parārthānamānamicchatā avaśyaṃ kārya pratijñāvacanamiti । yaccedam
	arthādarthagatau śaktiḥ pakṣahetvabhidhānayoḥ //
	nārtha tena tayornāsti svataḥ sādhanasaṃsthitiḥ // <= pra. vā. 4.15>

ityutkam । tatra arthasyārthagatau sāmarthya na niṣidhyate. kevalayośca pakṣahetva pacānāthaparicchede sāmarthyama. avayavāntarasadabhāve ca svārthopasthāpanadvāreṇa sāmarthyamiṣyata eva । anyathā hetvabhidhānasyāpi asāmarthya parārthānumānasyāpravṛttireva ।

[II,191,21]

atha hetuvacanaṃ svayamasamarthamapi samarthahetusaṃsūcakatvāt parapratipattāvapa〈hīyate?ādīyate〉 na caivaṃ pratijñetyāha,
	sādhyābhidhānāta pakṣoktiḥ pāramparyeṇa nāpyalama /
	śaktasya sūcakaṃ hetuvaco 'śaktamapi svayam // <= pra. vā. 4.17>

[II,191,25]

tatra pakṣoktiḥ pratijñāvacanaṃ pāramparyeṇāpyalaṃ samarthaṃ na bhavatīti dhināṅgamiti । sādhye sādhyābhidhānamasādhāraṇameva, sapakṣāsapakṣayora<II,192>prasiddhaḥ । tathā sādhyābhidhānasya pakṣokteḥ paryāyatvāt sādhyāviśiṣṭatā ceti । atha sādhyānupayogitvāt sādhyānabhidhānam, tadapyavayavāntarasahitasya sādhya pratipādakatvādasiddham, viparyaye tu anaikāntikam, kevalasya hetuvacanasyāpi asādhakatvāt । tathā pratijñāvacanamapi asādhanāṅgamiti vadatā abhyupagatava pratijñeti vyāghātaḥ ।

[II,192,6]

atha svapratipattau pratijñāvacanasyānupalambhāt parapratipattāvanupādānam ? evaṃ tarhi hetuvacanasyāpi adarśanādanupādānaṃ syāt । atha hetvarthasyopalambhād yuktaṃ hetuvacanam ? tarhi pratijñārthasyopalabdheḥ kārya pratijñāvacanam । yathā hetvarthaḥ kāraṇaṃ sādhyapratipattau, evaṃ pratijñārthaḥ karmetyubhayoḥ kāraṇatvā viśeṣāt pakṣasyāvacane pramāṇaṃ nāstīti । upasthāpite ca karmaṇi karaṇānā pravṛtterupalambhāt tadupasthāpanārthamavaśyaṃ kārya pratijñāvacanamityalaṃ vistareṇa ।

[II,192,12]

* avirodhigrahaṇāt pratyakṣānumānābhyupagatasvaśāstrasvavacanavirodhino 'numeyoddeśā nirastā bhavanti * iti vyavacchedyaṃ darśayati । yo hānumeyoddeśo na pratyakṣādinā virudhyate, sā pratikṣeti ।

[II,192,15]

anye tu pratyakṣādyaviruddho 'numeyastasyoddeśaḥ pratijñeti vyākhyāṃ kurvate । yadyapi anumeyasya sādhyasya sādhanāhatayā pratyakṣādivirodhābhāvānna vyavacchedya tva masti, tathāpi kimbhūtaṃ sādhyamityapekṣāyāṃ svarūpopavarṇanātha pratyakṣādyaviruddhapadam, pratyakṣaśabdenaiva viśiṣṭārthapratītau indriyārthasanniko dipadavaditi । taccāsat, avirodhipadasyoddeśapadena sāmānādhikaraṇyāt, karmaṇaḥ karaṇena virodhābhāvācceti । yathābhūtamupalabhyamānaṃ karma tathābhūta manupalabhyamānamapi iti uddyotakarapādairuktam । pratijñā tu karāmāta yuktastatra virodhaḥ ।

[II,192,23]

tatra pratyakṣavirodhī * yathā anuṣṇo 'gniḥ * iti । 〈〉anu?uṣṇatāyā stvagindriyeṇa pratibhāsanāt । * dhanamambaramityanumānavirodhī * ākāśasya anumānādeva amūrtatvavibhutvaprasiddheḥ । ghanaṃ niviḍāvayavamityuddeśastena virudhyata eva, ghanatve sati asmadādīnāmasañcāraprasaṅgācceti । abhyupagata śāstravirodhī yathā * vaiśeṣikasya * sarvakāryamatpatteḥ pūrvaṃ sa dutpadyatat । <II,193> iti bruvataḥ । vaiśeṣikaśāstre hi asadutpadyata iti prasiddham । * na śabdo 'rtha atyāyaka iti svavacanavirodhī । yadi hi śabdo 'rthapratyāyako na bhavati, kathamasyārthasya jñāpanārthaṃ śabdoccāraṇaṃ na virudhyeta iti ।

[II,193,4]

atha pramāṇatritve sati kathaṃ virodhabahutvam ? lokaprasiddhayapekṣayā । para āgamaviruddhasya pratyakṣaviruddhasya cāmī bhedāstathāpi svavacanaviruddhaḥ śāstrāvaruddhaścetyādivyapadeśo janānāma atastathaivābhidhānam । anamānasya tu anumānāntareṇa virodhāsambhave 'pi svakīyānamānasya balavatvādayaṃ vyapadeśo 'numānena pratijñā bādhyata iti ।

{§ hetuvaidharmyam}

[II,193,10]

(“liṅgavacanamapadeśaḥ । yadanameyena sahacaritaṃ tatsamānajātīye ca sāmānyena prasiddha. tadaviparīte ca sarvasminnasadeva talliḍamaktama । tasya vacanamapadeśaḥ । yathā kriyāvattvāda gaṇavattvācca, tathā ca tadanu maya'sti tatsamānajātīye ca sarvasmin guṇavattvam asavasmin kriyāvattvam । ubhayamapyetad adravye nāstyeva, tasmāt tasya vacanamapadeśa iti siddham ।”)

[II,193,16]

pratijñānantaraṃ hetulakṣaṇamāha * liṅgavacanamavadeśaḥ * iti । arthalakṣaṇatvād vacasāmiti liṅgalakṣaṇānuvāde apadeśasya mānyana prasiddham
manyatrāvṛtteḥ । sarvatra ceti ca 5 vipakṣe sarvatra nāsta samakālātyayāpadiṣṭayośca vyudāsaḥ
da vacasāmiti liṅgalakṣaṇānuvādena apadeśasya lakṣaṇābhidhānamiti ।
vana sahacaritaṃ tatsamānajātīye sarvatra ca sāmānyena prasiddham * khā dhamaḥ pakṣe tatsamānaḥ sapakṣe prasiddho na pūnaviśeṣaḥ, anyadharmāṇā "taḥ । sarvatra ceti vyāpakāvyāpakabhedaṃ darśayati । * tadaviparīte pakṣa sarvatra nāstyeveti vipakṣādatyantavyāvṛtti darśayati । prakaraṇa tyayāpadiṣṭayośca vyudāsaḥ pūrvavadityetat * liṅgamuktam * iti diḥ । tasya vācakaṃ vacanaṃ tatīyāntaṃ paścamyantaṃ vā apadeśaḥ । ayamitarasmāt bhidyate yathoktaliṅgavacanatvāt, yastu na bhidyate
tathā ca ayamitarasmāt
cāsāvevam, yathā pratijñādiriti ।

[II,193,26]

tasya vyāpakāvyāpakasvarūpopadarśanārthama udāharaṇadvayam * yathā kriyā<II,194>vattvād guṇavattvācca * iti । ca śabdena prakārāntaraṃ kriyāvatvena guṇavatvena ceti darśayati । anayorlakṣaṇenābhisambandhopadarśanārthamanuvādaḥ । tathā ca tat kriyāvattvaṃ guṇavattvañcānumeye pakṣe 'sti । tatsamānajātīye ca sapakṣe sarvasmin guṇavattvam asarvasmin kriyāvattvamastīti । * ubhayamapyetad adravye * sattādā nāstyeveti tasya guṇavattvasya kriyāvattvasya ca yathoktam . vacanamapadeśa iti siddham ।

{§ hetvābhāsanirūpaṇam}

[II,194,8]

(“etenāsiddhaviruddhasandigdhānadhyavasitavacanānāmanapadeśatvamuktaṃ bhavati । tatrāsiddhaścatuvidhaḥ, ubhayāsiddho 'nyatarāsiddhastadbhāvāsiddho 'numayā siddhaśceti । tatrobhayāsiddhaḥ, ubhayorvādiprativādinorasiddho yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ sāvayavatvāditi । anyatarāsiddho yathā anityaḥ śabda kāryatvāditi । taddhāvāsiddho yathā dhamabhāvenāgnyadhigatau kartavyāyāma panyasyamāno vāṣpo dhūmabhāvenāsiddha iti । anumeyāsiddho yathā pāca dravyaṃ tamaḥ kṛṣṇarūpavattvāditi ।”)

[II,194,15]

* etena * sāmarthyād apadeśābhāsā nirastā bhavantīti svavākya parivarjanārthaṃ paravākye codbhāvanārthaṃ saṃlakṣyate । tatredaṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇam, apadeśavadābhāsamānāḥ samyaṅ matau apadeśābhāsāḥ । 〈aāhetravirapi va paryastabuddherhetu dā?d〉 bhāsate iti samyaṅmatāviti padam । etasmiraṇa pakṣe 'nyatarāsiddhasya samyaṅamatau hetuvadābhāsamānatvaṃ cintyama । tasya hi para dharmatvādimatvamityato hetuvadābhāsamānatvād hetvābhāsā iti siddhaṃ lakṣaṇam । yasya tu heturapi tasya pakṣadharmatvādyapadarśanena hetṛtvapratipattau yatnaḥ kāya tpratipatterthapratipattau kāraṇatvāditi । ata eva anyatarāsiddho yadyapi 1 vṛttyā hetustathāpi pakṣadharmatayā pareṇāpratipannatvād asiddhabuddhi janayatā pratipanne ca pramāṇataḥ pakṣadharmatvena sādhyasiddharbhāvād hetureveti ।

[II,194,25]

anye tu ahetavaḥ pakṣadharmatvādyanyatamarūpānavidhānāt samāna hetvābhāsā iti ।

<II,195>

[II,195,1]

atha kiyatāṃ punarevamanapadeśatvamityāha * asiddhaviruddhasandigdhānadhyava sitavacanānāmanapadeśatvamuktaṃ bhavati * iti । * tatrāsiddhaścaturvidhaḥ * iti vibhāgaḥ । sāmānyalakṣaṇañca āśaṅkyamānapakṣavṛttitvam arthāllabhyate । bhāśakyamāne hi pakṣe vattiḥ sarvasya viśeṣaṇāsiddhādiprapañcasyāstīti pakṣa pāpāda sāmānyalakṣaṇam । na caivaṃ pakṣāvṛttitvaṃ tasya asamarthaviśeṣaṇādibhedeṣu asambhavāt ।

[II,195,7]

kena rūpeṇa caturvidha ityāha * ubhayāsiddho 'nyatarāsiddhastadbhāvāsiddho 'numeyāsiddhaśceti । tatra * ubhayorvādiprativādinorasiddho yathā anityaḥ 5. sāvayavatvāditi * śabde hi sāvayavatvaṃ nityānityavādinorna prasiddha ta । * anyatarāsiddho yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatvāditi * mīmāṃsakasya 9 atyabhijñānādikamapalabhamānasya śabde kāryatvaṃ tāvadasiddhaṃ yāvad anyatara sadāsadvāreṇa pramāṇato (na?) vyavasthāpyata iti niścīyate । niścite 7 dhamatve tataḥ sādhyaṃ pratipadyata eva । * tadabhāvāsiddho yathā dhamabhāvenāgyadhigato * iti । dhamatvenāniścitaṃ vāṣpādikamupalabhamānasyāgnyadhi । kartavyāyāṃ tadbhāvāsiddho dhūmabhāvasyāniścitatvāditi । * anumeyā ddhā yathā pārthivaṃ dravyaṃ tamaḥ kṛṣṇarūpatvāvattvā〈〉 diti ।

[II,195,17]

sākhyābhyupagatasya tamaso 'prasiddhatvād ayamāśrayāsiddho na tu abhāvarūpatamo 'pekṣayā । tasya tu pramāṇena prasiddheḥ pakṣīkaraṇe kṛṣṇarūpatvaṃ?vattvaṃ | svarūpāsiddhaṃ, natvāśrayāsiddhamiti ।

[II,195,20]

nanvevaṃ viśeṣaṇāsiddhādiprapañcasyāsaṅagrahaṇādayukto 'yaṃ vibhāgaḥ ? na. siddha'nyatarāsiddhe vā antarbhāvāt । tathā ca ubhayoviśeṣaṇāsiddho yathā । śabdaḥ anabhidheyatve satibāhyendriyapratyakṣatvāt । bāhyendriyapratyakṣatve ca - anabhidheyatvāditi ubhayoviśeṣyāsiddhaḥ 〈yathā〉 nityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtakatve sati amūrtatvāt । evamanyeṣvapi puruṣaviśeṣābhiprāyeṇa atyādhuhyamiti । asamarthaviśeṣaṇāsiddho 〈yathā〉 nityaḥ śabdaḥ prameyatve " kṛtakatvāta । viparyayeṇa asamarthaviśeṣya siddha〈〉 iti । vyadhikaraṇaviśeṣaṇāsiddho 〈yathā〉 nityaḥ śabdaḥ cākṣuṣatve sati kṛtakatvāt । viparyayeṇa
ubhayāsiddhe 'nyatarāsiddha vā natyaḥ śabdaḥanabhidheyatve <II,196> vyadhikaraṇaviśeṣyāsiddha iti । viruddhaviśeṣaṇāsiddho yathā〈〉 <?> nityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatve sati amūrtatvāditi । anyathāsiddhaviśeṣaṇāsiddho 〈〉yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ abhyasyamānatve sati amūrtatvāditi ।

[II,196,4]

nanvevamapi eṣāmubhayāsiddhe 'nyatarāsiddhe 'ntarbhāvavat tadbhāvā siddhā〈〉 nu meyāsiddhayorapyantarbhāvaḥ syāditi kathaṃ cāturvidhyam ? tayoravāntarabhedāpekṣayā tadbhāvāsiddhaḥ, parārthānumānasya prastutatvād ubhayāsiddho 'nyatarāsiddhaśceti bhidyate । evam anumeyāsiddho 'pīti cāturvidhyam ।

[II,196,8]

anye tūbhayāsiddhaṃ yatra viśeṣaṇaṃ viśeṣyañca asiddhamiti । anyatarā siddhantu viśeṣaṇāsiddhaṃ viśeṣyāsiddhaṃ veti manyante । na caitad bhāṣyakatubhi pretam, vādyabhiprāyeṇa udāharaṇopanyāsāt ।

[II,196,11]

anye tu svārthānumānasya tadbhāvāsiddho 'numeyāsiddhaśceti bhada sakalabhedasaṅgrāhakaḥ, parārthānumānasya tūbhayāsiddho 'nyatarāsiddhaśceti । atra tu svārthānumānena parārthasya bhedanirūpaṇamiṣṭameva, svātantryantu niṣidhyate ।

[II,196,14]

(“yo hi anumeye 'vidyamāno 'pi tatsamānajātīye sarvasmin nāsti tadviparīte cāsti sa viparītasādhanād viruddho yathā yasmād viṣāṇā tasmād aśva iti ।”)

[II,196,17]

viruddhalakṣaṇamāha * yo hyanumeye * pakṣe vyāptyā avidyamāno 'pi tatsamā najātīye ca sapakṣe * sarvasmin nāsti tadviparīte ca * vipakṣe 'sti *sa viparītasādhanād viruddho yathā yasmād viṣāṇī tasmād aśva iti * । viṣāṇināṃ piṇḍaṃ pakṣīkṛtya aśvo 'yam iti sādhayato viṣāṇitvād hāta hetuviruddhaḥ, asya hi anaśvenaiva vyāptatvāt । ayantu vipakṣaikadeśavṛttiḥ । vidyamānasapakṣastathā vipakṣavyāpakaḥ nitya śabdaḥ kāryatvād iti । avidyamāna sapakṣo vipakṣavyāpakaḥ sarvaṃ kārya sarvajñakartakaṃ prameyatvāditi । vidyamānasapakṣā vipakṣaikadeśavṛttiḥ, jīvaccharīraṃ sātmakaṃ kāryatvāditi । ataścatuvidhaḥ ।

[II,196,25]

(“yastu sannanumeye tatsamānāsamānajātīyayoḥ sādhāraṇaḥ sanneva sandaha janakatvāt sandigdho yathā yasmād viṣāṇī tasmād gauriti ।”)

<II,197>

[II,197,1]

ekasmiśca dvayorhetvoryathoktalakṣaṇayoviruddhayoḥ sannipāte sati saśayadarśanādayamanyaḥ sandigdha iti kacita । yathā mūrtatvāmūrtatvaṃ prati manasaḥ kriyāvattvāsparśavatvayoriti ।

[II,197,4]

nanvayamasādhāraṇa eva acākṣaṣatvapratyakṣatvavata saṃhatayoranyatarapakṣā sambhavāt, tataścānadhyavasita iti vakṣyāmaḥ ।

[II,197,6]

nanu śāstre tatra tatra ubhayathā darśanaṃ saṃśayakāraṇamapadiśyata iti, na, saṃśayo viṣayadvaitadarśanāta । saṃśayotpattau viṣayadvaitadarśanameva kāraṇam, tulyabalatve ca tayoḥ parasparavirodhāt nirṇayānutpādakatvaṃ syānna tu saṃśayahetutvam । na ca tayostulyabalatvamasti anyatarasyānumeyohaśasyāgamabādhitatvād ayantu viruddhabheda eva ।

[II,197,11]

* yastu sannanumeye * vyāptyā * tatsamānāsamānajātīyayoḥ * sapakṣa pāḥ sanneva, sa sandigdho 'naikāntikaḥ । * sandehajanakatvāt * iti kāryopanyāso na tū lakṣaṇama. indriyādiṣvapi sadabhāvenātivyāpakatvāta । jantu * yathā yasmāda viṣāṇī tasmāda gauriti viṣāṇinaṃ piṇḍa
bhārati sādhayato viṣāṇitvāditi heturanaikāntikaḥ, pakṣatrayavṛtti ' ayantu sapakṣavyāpakatve sati vipakṣakadeśavṛttiḥ । agaurayaṃ viṣāṇi śata sapakṣakadeśavattitve sati vipakṣavyāpakaḥ । sapakṣavipakṣakadeśa nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśavattvāta iti catavidho 'nekāntikaḥ ।

[II,197,19]

jaya cāturvidhyamanapapannama. anekāntikasya lakṣaṇañcāvyāpakama, viruddhā bhicāryasādhāraṇayorakhyāpanāda ityāśaṅkāpratiṣedhārtham * ekasmiśca
ityādi prakaraṇam । dvayorhetvovibhinnadharmisthayoḥ sannipāte saṃśayā yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatvāta, nityamākāśam akāryatvād iti
vipakṣayoḥ sanneva, sa sa kāryopanyāso na tu lakṣaṇa
pakṣīkṛtya gauriti sādhayato vi
tvāt iti sapakṣakadeśavṛtti
dvayoḥ * ityādi prakaraṇam । hara darśanāt yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ kāya ekasmin dharmiṇīti padam । tathāthā na saṃśayo yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ । * yathoktalakṣaṇayoḥ * ।
maṇīti padam । tathāthāpyekasmin dharmiṇi dvayoḥ sannipāte 'pi yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatvāt, nityastvamūrtakāryatvāditi tadarthaṃ

[II,197,26]

tathāpyaviruddhārthasādhakayorevaṃvidhayorapi na saṃśayahetutvaṃ yathā nityaḥ <II,198> śabdaḥ kāryatvāt, āśrito guṇatvāt । ato * viruddhayoḥ * viruddhārthasādhakayoḥ sannipāte saṃśayasya darśanāt * ayamanyaḥ sandigdhaḥ * anekāntika iti kecit । udāharaṇantu * yathā mūrtatvāmūrtatvaṃ prati manasaḥ kriyāvattvāsparśavattvayoriti * । mūrta manaḥ kriyāvattvāt chatravat ityekaḥ, amūrta manaḥ asparśavattvāt ākāśavat ityaparaḥ । ubhayośca pakṣadharmānvayavyatirekavattvopalabdheḥ kiṃ mūrtaṃ manaḥ syā duta amūrtamiti saṃśayaḥ ।

[II,198,7]

tadasat, abhayoḥ prayogāsambhavāt । tathā hi, ekasmin sādhane prayukta tasya nirduṣṭatāyāṃ sādhyasiddharanyasya upanyāsānupapattiḥ, duṣṭatāyāṃ vā saiva asya abhidheyeti । na ca parasparaviruddhārthasādhakatvameva anumānayordoṣaḥ, pramā gena ubhayorekatra sadbhāvasiddhau virodhasyābhāvaprasaṅgāt । avyabhicāryānumā nayośca avaśyamarthavyavasthāpakatvam, avyabhicārasya tallakṣaṇatvāt, viparyaye tu vyabhicāritvameva । yathā mūrtaṃ mano 'sparśavattve sati kriyāvattvāt, amūrtañca kriyāvattve satyasparśavattvāt iti samastayoḥ prayogaḥ ।

[II,198,14]

tatrāpi asādhāraṇamityāha * nanvayamasādhāraṇa eva acākṣuṣatvapratyakṣa tvavat, saṃhatayoranyatarapakṣāsambhavāt * iti । yathā hi, rūpātīndriyaguṇavyati rekeṇa anyaguṇānāṃ guṇavyavahāre sādhyasāmānyavattvād dravyatve sati niyamenācā kṣuṣatvaṃ heturna sapakṣe rūpādāvasti, nāpi vipakṣe ghaṭādāvityasādhāraṇaḥ; tadvat sahacarayoḥ kriyāvattvāsparśavattvayoranyatarapakṣāsambhavādityanyatarasmin sapakṣe vipakṣe vā asambhavād asādhāraṇatvam । na cāsyāsaṅgraha ityāha * tataścānadhyavasita iti vakṣyāmaḥ * ।

[II,198,21]

yad vā cākṣuṣatvapratyakṣatvavat iti vaidhodāharaṇam । yathā hi guṇaḥ śabdaḥ sāmānyavattvād dravyatve sati niyamena acākṣuṣapratyakṣatvāt andhādiva diti । asya sapakṣakadeśe vartamānasya vipakṣādatyantaṃ vyāvṛttirna caivaṃ kriyāva ttvāsparśavattvayorityāha * saṃhatayoranyatarapakṣāsambhavāt * iti ।

[II,198,25]

saṅgrahoktevivaraṇamāha * anumeyadharmamātratvenābhihitaṃ liṅgasāmānyam * na tu samarthamiti mātrābhidhānena darśayati । * anupalabdhaśaktikam * iti । anupalabdhā śaktiravinābhāvo yasya tat tathoktam । punaḥ * nidarśane 'numeya dharmasāmānyena saha dṛṣṭam * । 〈〉anumeye pakṣe yena vacanena “anu” paścāt sandhīyate pakṣadharmatayā khyāpyate tad anusandhānam ।

[II,205,9]

tadapi dvividham, sādharmyaṇa vaidharyeṇa ca । tatra anumeyasāmānyena saha liṅgasāmānyasya nidarśane sattvamupalabhyābhisandhatte tathā cāyaṃ kriyāvān vāyu riti । vaidharmyanidarśane tu anumeyasya dravyatvasyābhāve ca tasya kriyāvattvasyā sattvamupalabhya na ca tathā vāyuniṣkriya ityupasaṃhāraḥ । niṣkriyatvapratiṣedhena kriyāvattvamupasaṃharatīti । pṛthagvacanantu pratiṣedhābhiprāyeṇaiva ।

[II,205,14]

nanu vyarthamanusandhānavacanam, tadantareṇāpi hetuvacanād gṛhītavyāptikāt sādhyasiddheḥ ? na, anena vinā abādhitaviṣayatvasyāpratipatteḥ । hetuvacanantu kāraṇamātropasthāpakam, na tu gṛhītavyāptikasya antarvyāptipratipādaka miti । yathābhūtena dravyatvāvinābhāvinā pramāṇāntarāviruddhena kriyāvattvena kriyāvān karaḥ, tathā ca vāyurityantāptipratipattiḥ । tadabhāve tu bahirvyāpti sadbhāve 'pi na gamakatvam । yathā śabdasya anityatve sādhye sāmānyavattve sati cākṣuṣapratyakṣaḥ, tasya kālātyayāpadiṣṭa〈 sya?tvaṃ〉 ceti । ata evātropanayavacanaṃ na nirviṣayatvādapramāṇam ।

[II,205,22]

na copasaṃhāra vinā dharmiviśeṣeṇa sambandhāprasiddhau tatraiva sādhyaviśeṣa pratipattiḥ syāt । svārthānumānakāle ca upanayārthasyopalabdheḥ kārya tad vacanam, svapratipattyanusāreṇa parārthānumānapravṛtteḥ । na ca svapratipattāvetasyā satvam, avinābhāvasambandhasmaraṇānantaraṃ parāmaśaṃjñānasyānubhavāt । anabhyu pagame ca sambandhasmaraṇasyāniyatatvāt niyatapradeśe pratipattirna syādityuktam ।

<II,206>

[II,206,1]

tasmād ayamityaparokṣatānirdeśasyāvinābhāvasambandhasmaraṇānantara mupalabdharasti parāmarśajñānam, atastadupanyāsārtha kāryamanusandhānavacanamiti ।

[II,206,3]

(“anumeyatvenoddiṣṭe cāniścite ca pareṣāṃ niścayāpādanārtha pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanaṃ pratyāmnāyaḥ । pratipādyatvenoddiṣṭe cāniścite ca pareṣāṃ hetvādibhiravayavairāhitaśaktīnāṃ parisamāptena vākyena niścayā pādanātha pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanaṃ pratyāmnāyaḥ, tasmād dravyameveti ।”)

[II,206,7]

atha pratyāmnāyasvarūpopadarśanārtham * anumeyatvenoddiṣṭe * ityādi prakaraṇam । * anumeyatvena * anumānayogyatvena । * uddiṣṭe cāniścite ca pareṣām * saṃśayitaviparyastāvyutpannānām । punaḥ * niścayāpādanārthaṃ pratijñāyāḥ 〈〉punaḥ vacanaṃ pratyāmnāyaḥ ।

[II,206,11]

saṅgrahoktevivaraṇamāha anumeye dharmamātre * pratipādyatvena * sādhyatvena, * uddiṣṭe cāniścite ca pareṣām * । kiṃ viśiṣṭānām ? * hetvādibhira 〈?vayavairā〉 hitaśaktīnām * iti । āhitā śaktiravinābhāvo yasya liṅgasya yastaistathoktaisteṣām । etasmāt sādhanād bhaviṣyati sādhyasiddhirityava kṛtāsthānāmiti bhāvaḥ । * niścayāpādanārthaṃ pratijñāyāḥ punarvacana pratyāmnāyaḥ * iti । punaruktamātravyavacchedārtha pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanamiti padam । tathāpi anityaḥ śabdo 'nityaḥ śabda iti punaruktavyu dāsārthaṃ niścayā pādanārthamiti padam । avipratipannasya etasmādapi niścayo bhavatīti tadaya pareṣāmiti । tathāpi teṣāṃ madhye kasyacid ekāvayavopadarśanena anvayavyātara kānusmaraṇadvāreṇa arthapratipattirbhavatīti * parisamāptena vākyena * iti grahaṇam । yasminnavayave sati vākyaṃ parisamāpyata iti । tadevaṃ pratyāmnāya. itarasmād bhidyate yathoktalakṣaṇatvāditi ।

[II,206,23]

nanu pratijñāvacanasya tu vināśitvena avasthānāsambhavāt kathaṃ punarvacana miti ? tatsamānaśabdoccāraṇāt । yathā kṣaṇikatve 'pi karmaṇaḥ pūrvaṃ samānāmi nayakaraṇāt punarnṛtyatīti vyapadeśastadvat pratijñāsamāna śabdaprayogakaraṇāra punarvacanabhiti vyapadeśo bhavatyeva । atiśaye “pūnaḥ”śabdo vivakṣita । pratijñā pakṣastasya punarvacanaṃ ghaṭata eva ।

<II,207>

[II,207,1]

liṅgavākyārthavādinastu pratijñāyate 'neneti pratijñā liṅgaṃ tasya punarvacanaṃ pratyāmnāya iti ।

[II,207,3]

udāharaṇantu * tasmād dravyameveti * । etena adravyatvapratipādaka pramāṇābhāvo 'pyupadarśita eva ।

[II,207,5]

atha vyarthaṃ pratyāmnāyavacanam, sambandhābhidhānādeva vivakṣitārthaprasiddhaḥ । taduktam,

[II,207,7]

'ḍiṇḍikarāgaṃ parityajyākṣiṇī nimīlya cintaya tāvat ki iyatārtha māttabhavati naveti । yadi iha bhavati kimanayā śabdamālayā ?na bhavatīti - vācyaṃ dṛṣṭatvāt' <= hetubinduḥ, baḍodā, pṛṣṭha. 56>

[II,207,10]

natadevaṃ, pratijñāvacanaṃ vinā anvayanyatirekāprasidvau sambandhābhidhāna syāgamakatvena pūrvameva vyavasthāpitatvāt ।

[II,207,12]

(“ne hyetasminnasati pareṣāmavayavānāṃ samastānāṃ vyastānāṃ vā tadartha pakatvamasti । gamyamānārthatvāditi cenna, atiprasaṅgāta । tathā hi. śānantaraṃ hetumātrābhidhānaṃ kartavyama, viduṣāmanvayavyatirekasmaraṇāta vigāṃtarbhaviṣyatīti । tasmādatraivārthaparisamāptiḥ ।”)

<II,208>

[II,208,1]

(“katham ? anitya śabdaḥ ityanena aniścitānityatvamātraviśiṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ kathyate । prayatnānantarīyakatvādityanena anityatvasādhanaṃ dharmamātra mabhidhīyate । iha yat prayatnānantarīyakaṃ tadanityaṃ dṛṣṭam, yathā ghaṭa ityanena sādhyasāmānyena sādhanasāmānyasya anagamamātramucyate । nityam aprayatnānantarīyakaṃ dṛṣṭam, yathā ākāśama ityanena sādhyābhāvena saha sādhanasya asattvaṃ pradarśyate । tathā ca prayatnānantarīyakaḥ śabdo dṛṣṭaḥ, na ca tathā ākāśavadaprayatnānantarīyakaḥ śabda ityanvayavyatirekābhyāṃ dṛṣṭa sāmarthyasya sādhanasāmānyasya śabdenasandhānaṃ gamyate । tasmād aninyaḥ śabda ityanena anitya eva śabda iti pratipipādayiṣitārthaparisamāpti rgamyate ।”)

[II,208,11]

(“tasmāt pañcāvayavenaiva vākyena pareṣāṃ svaniścitārthapratipādana kiyata ityetat parārthānumānaṃ siddha miti ।”)

[II,208,13]

atha pratijñāderevārthapratipādakatvamastu, ki pratyāmnāyena, tathā hi, pratijñāvacanaiviṣayavyavasthāpanād hetūdāharaṇābhyāṃ vahirvyāptiprasiddhau upanaya nāntaryāptyupadarśane sati avaśyamabhipretārthasiddhiriti । satyametata, tathāpi avaśyambhāvino 'rthasya pratijñādinā pratipāditasya pratipādanārthamavaśyaṃ kāya nigamanamityāha * na hyetasmin * iti । na pūrveṣāmavayavānāṃ samastānā tadarthavācakatvamasti । vyastānāmitaretaravyāvṛttasvārthavyavasthāpane caritāya tvamityanyadato vācyaṃ yasya sahakāriṇāṃ pūrvapadānāṃ samastānāmapi smṛtyupa sthāpitānāṃ vākyārthapratipādakatvamiti ।

[II,208,21]

atha sādhanasya antarvyāptibahirvyāptyabhidhāne sati sādhyaviśeṣo gamya evetyāha * gamyamānārthatvāditi cenna, atiprasaṅgāta । tathā hi, pratijñāna hetumātrābhidhānaṃ kartavyam * svata eva viduṣāṃ hetūpalambhe sati anvayamā rekānusmaraṇaṃ, tasmāccādhigatirbhaviṣyatīti viśeṣābhidhānavaiyayaṃ syāt ।

[II,208,25]

atha paraṃ pratipādayatā vacanenaiva pratipādana kāryamiti śeṣāṇā prayā hi vākyārthapratipādanārthaṃ nigamanamapi kāryama । na ca pratipādyāmitrā prayogo yuktaḥ, tasya manuṣyadharmaṇā sākṣādapratīteravyavasthāpanācca । tathā hi, <II,209> kāścadekasmādeva avayavādarthaṃ pratipadyate, kaścid dvābhyām, anyastribhiritya navasthitatvāt pratipādyānāṃ tadabhiprāyāniścaye prayogānupapattireva syāt । ataḥ paraṃ pratipādayatā svapratipattyupāyopadarśanaṃ kāryamiti pañcānāṃ prayogo purataḥ । tathā hi, pradeśasthaṃ dhamamupalabhya avinābhāvasambandhaṃ smṛtvā tathā pāya dhūmavāniti parāmṛśati, tataḥ sādhyaṃ pratipadyate tasmādagnimāniti jagamanārthasyāpyupalabdheḥ parapratipādanāya tadupanyāso yukta eveti pañcānāṃ bhāgaḥ kārya ityāha bhāṣyakāraḥ tasmādatraivārthaparisamāptiḥ iti ।

[II,209,8]

anye tu antarvyāptipratipādanārthaṃ nigamanamiti manyante । anusandhānāt vyāpakatvaprasiddhau viparītaprasaṅgapratiṣedhārthaṃ nigamanamiti ।

[II,209,10]

viparītārthavyavasthāpakapramāṇasyāprāmāṇyopadarśane sati pakṣe vyāptiḥ cāyata eva । yatra ca parapakṣāpratiṣedhastatra hetonaṃ gamakatvam । yathā mūryo 'tatputratvāt upalabhyamānatatputravaditi । atra hi tatputrasya amūrkhatve na cad bādhakamastīti tatsādhakapramāṇābhāvaśca niścita eveti anyathāsiddhaṃ sādhanametat ।

[II,209,15]

athāvinābhūtasya pramāṇavirodhābhāvāna yuktaṃ viparītapramāṇasyāprāmā padaśanamiti cenna, tadantareṇāvinābhāvasyaivāprasiddheḥ । tathā hi, nityatva "pādakapramāṇasya prāmāṇye sati na śabde kṛtakatvasyānityatvena vyāptiḥ yādāta । na ca parapakṣapratiṣedhakādeva svapakṣasiddhiḥ, vyadhikaraṇatvāt, vārāpa vaiyarthyaprasaṅgācceti । parapakṣapratiṣedhe tūpadarśitabahirvyāptikaṃ pakṣe palabhyamānaṃ bhavatyeva sādhanamiti nigamanaprayogaḥ kāryaḥ ।

[II,209,21]

atha pratijñāvacanameva parapakṣapratiṣedhasahāyaṃ sādhanamiti cenna, tasya mātrābhidhāyakatvāta, sādhyama iti arhatyarthe, śakyārthe vā kṛtya?tābhi " katha tadvacanāt tasya siddhiḥ? tasmād bahirvyāptivadantāpti samarthayatā taviṣayatvāsatpratipakṣatvapratipādanārthameva avayavāntaramabhidheyam ।

[II,209,25]

atha prakaraṇasamakālātyāpadiṣṭayorapi bahirvyāptisabhāvāt gamakatvaṃ , bhasti ca tayoḥ pakṣavyāpakatve satyanvayavyatirekasadbhāva iti ? ayukta<II,210>〈metat,〉 tādātmyatadutpattilakṣaṇapratibandhāyattastu avyabhicāro na bhavatī tyuktaṃ vyāptisamarthanāvasare । tasmāduktanyāyena atraivārthaparisamāptiriti ।

[II,210,3]

evaṃ vibhinnaprakaraṇeṣu avayavānāṃ svarūpopadarśane 'pi ekatra tatsvarūpa parijñānāpekṣayā praśnaḥ * katham * iti । * anityaḥ śabda ityanana aniścitānityatvamātraviśiṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ kathyate * iti pratijñaiṣā । * prayatnā nantarīyakatvādityanena anityatvasādhanadharmamātramabhidhīyate * na tu samarthamiti hetuvacanam । * iha yat prayatnānantarīyakaṃ tadanityaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yathā ghaṭa ityanena sādhyasāmānyena (saha ?) sādhanasāmānyasyānugamamātramucyate * hāta sādharyodāharaṇam । * nityam aprayatnānantarīyakaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yathā ākāśam ityanena sādhyābhāvena saha sādhanasyāsattvaṃ vyākhyāyate ? pradaśyate * śata vaidharyodāharaṇam । * tathā ca prayatnānantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ * na ca tathā prayatnā nantarīyako na bhavatīti, * anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ dṛṣṭasāmarthyasya sādhanasāmānya sya śabde 'nusandhāna gamyate । tasmādanityaḥ eva ? śabdaḥ ityanana anitya eva śabda iti pratipipādayiṣitārthaparisamāptirgamyate* ityabhipretātha siddhirbhavatīti । ataḥ * pañcāvayavenaiva vākyena pareṣāṃ svaniścitārthaprati pādanaṃ kriyate iti siddham ।

[II,210,17]

atra ca śabdaviśeṣasya pakṣīkaraṇe prayatnānantarīyakatvaṃ sādhanaṃ vivakṣita miti jñeyam । anyathā hi śabdamātraparigrahe prayatnānantarīyakatvaṃ bhāgāsincha syāt । na hi prayatnānantaraṃ sarvaśabdānāṃ janmāstīti ।

{§ nirṇayavaidharmyam}

[II,210,21]

(“viśeṣadarśanajamavadhāraṇajñānaṃ saṃśayavirodhī nirṇayaḥ । etadana pratyakṣamanumānaṃ vā । yadviśeṣadarśanāta saṃśayavirodhyutpadyate sa pratyā nirṇayaḥ । yathā sthāṇupuruṣayorūrvatāmātrasādṛśyālocanād viśeṣa pratyakṣeṣu ubhayaviśeṣānusmaraṇāt kimayaṃ sthāṇuḥ puruṣo 1 saṃśayotpattau 〈satyāṃ?〉 śiraḥpāṇyādi 〈〉viśeṣa? darśanāta puruṣa evāmitva vadhāraṇajñānaṃ pratyakṣanirṇayaḥ ।”)

<II,211>

[II,211,1]

(“viṣāṇamātradarśanād gaurgavayo veti saṃśayotpattau sāsnāmātradarśanāda gorevāyamityavadhāraṇajñālamanumānanirṇayaḥ ।”)

[II,211,3]

atha nirṇayo vidyāntaramiti kecit । taniṣedhārthaṃ * viśeṣadarśanajam - ityādi prakaraṇam । parārthānumānānantaramasyāntarbhāvanirūpaṇamatrāpi antarbhāva śāpanārtham । nirṇaya iti lakṣyanirdeśo 'vaśiṣṭaṃ lakṣaṇam । avadhāraṇajñānaṃ hi viṣayayajñānamapi bhavati na tu viśeṣadarśanājjāyate । viśeṣadarśanajaṃ cobha ? ca saṃśa〈〉 yajñānamapītyavadhāraṇagrahaṇam ।

[II,211,8]

tathāpi viśeṣadarśanajamavadhāraṇajñānaṃ nirṇaya ityukte vyabhicārābhāvād saṃśayavirodhīti padam ? na, viśiṣṭanirṇayalakṣaṇārthatvāt । yadyapi padarśanajamavadhāraṇajñānamiti sakalanirṇayavyāpīdaṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ tathāpi virodhīti padaṃ saṃśayapūrvakasya nirṇayasya lakṣaṇārtham । tathā ca naiyāyikai vimṛśya pakṣapratipakṣābhyāmarthāvadhāraṇaṃ nirṇayaḥ' <= nyā. sū. 1.1.41> taśayapūrvakasya lakṣaṇam । vimṛśyeti vimarśa kṛtvā, pakṣapratipakṣābhyāmiti nābhyām, sa punaḥ sādhanadūṣaṇābhyāṃ nirṇaya iti ।

[II,211,15]

atha viśeṣadarśanāt saṃśayo vyāvartate, na nirṇayāditi kathaṃ tadvirodhitvam । upacāreṇa, nirṇayakāraṇasya saṃśayavirodhitvāt nirṇayastavirodhītyuktam ।

[II,211,17]

asyāntarbhāvamāha * etadeva pratyakṣamanumānaṃ vā * na jñānāntaram । sāmagnījanyaṃ hi pratyakṣamanumānasāmagrījanyantu anumānamiti । * yad daśanāt saṃśayavirodhyutpadyate sa nirṇayaḥ * iti prāktanasya vivaraṇam ।
viśeṣadarśanāt saṃśayā

[II,211,21]

atra * sthāṇupuruṣayorūlatāmātrasādṛśyālocanād viśeṣaṣvapratyakṣeṣūbhaya pānusmaraṇāt - 〈kimayaṃ〉 sthāṇuḥ puruṣo veti saṃśayotpattau satyāṃ śiraḥ pāṇyādiviśeṣadarśanāt puruṣa evāyamityavadhāraṇajñānam indriyārthasannikarṣā ta. pratyakṣanirṇayaḥ । * viṣāṇamātradarśanāt * iti piṇḍavyavadhāne 'pi " syāvaśiṣṭaviṣāṇadarśanāt । *gaurgavayo veti saṃśayotpattau satyām । sāsnāmātradarśanāt * avinābhāvasambandhasmaraṇe sati parāmarśajñānānantaram । ravāyamityavadhāraṇajñānaṃ anumānanirṇayaḥ ।

<II,212>

{§ smṛtivaidharmyam}

[II,212,2]

(“liṅgadarśanecchānusmaraṇādyapekṣādātmamanasoḥ saṃyogaviśeṣāt paṭva bhyāsādarapratyayajanitācca saṃskārād dṛṣṭaśrutānubhūteṣvartheṣu śeṣānuvyava sāyānusmaraṇecchādveṣaheturatītaviṣayā smṛtiriti ।”)

[II,212,5]
