atha smṛteḥ kāryakāraṇaviṣayasvarūpanirūpaṇārthaṃ *liṅgadarśanecchānu । smaraṇādyapekṣāt * ityādi prakaraṇam । liṅgadarśanecchānusmaraṇādyapekṣāt * . liṅgadarśanañca icchā ca anusmaraṇañceti tathoktāni, tānyādiryeṣāmityādi padena praṇidhānādergrahaṇama, tānyapekṣata iti tadapekṣastasmāta । * ātmamanasā saṃyogaviśeṣāt * ityasamavāyikāraṇanirdeśaḥ । liṅgadarśanecchānusmaraṇādha pekṣāt * paṭavabhyāsādarapratyayajanitācca saṃskārāt * iti nimittakāraṇa nirdeśaḥ । * dṛṣṭaśrutānubhūteṣvartheṣu * iti dṛṣṭaḥ pratyakṣeṇa, śrutaḥ śabdena, anubhūtā 'numānena ।

[II,212,13]

anye tu dṛṣṭaścakṣuṣā, anubhūtastvagindriyeṇeti ।

[II,212,14]

tatra liṅgaṃ darśayati * śeṣānuvyavasāyānusmaraṇecchādveṣahetuḥ * iti । upayuktālliṅgād anumeyaḥ śeṣaḥ, so 'nuvyavasīyate aneneti śeṣānuvyavasāya parāmarśajñānam, tasya heturavinābhāvasambandhasmaraṇam, tathā padasmaraṇā vākyasmaraṇam, sukhasmaraṇādiccho duḥkhasmaraṇāda dveṣa iti । * atītaviṣayā * iti svarūpakathanam । atīto viṣayo yasyāḥ sā tathokteti ।

[II,212,19]

nanvayuktametat, vidyamāne 'pi vastuni smaraṇasya darśanādityavyāta, ativyāptiśca anumānāderatītaviṣayatvāditi ।

[II,212,21]

atha codanaiva bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyantaṃ viprakṛṣṭādikamarthaṃ prakāśayati nātha kiñcana indriyādikamiti cenna, anamānasyāpi atītādyarthaprakāśana palambhāt । tathā ca, meghonnatyā bhaviṣyati vṛṣṭirityanumīyate, nadāpūra viśiṣṭād upariṣṭād vṛṣṭirityuktam । pratyakṣañcātra avinābhāvagrāhaka yam, anyathā vyāptigrahaṇābhāve 'numānameva na pravarteta । na cānumānanā bhāvagrahaṇam, anavasthāprasaṅgāt । vartamānena cāvinābhāvagrahaṇe katham atītā<II,213>dyarthānumānaṃ syāt, anyenāvinābhāvagrahaṇe 'nyasyānumitau atiprasaṅgāt । tasmādatītaviṣayatvaṃ vyākhyeyampacāreṇa । yatra hi viṣaye 'nubhavo 'tītastatra smṛtirutpadyata iti ।

[II,213,4]

anye tu atīto vyavahito viṣayo yasyānubhavasyāsau atītaviṣayaḥ, saviṣayo yasyāḥ sā atītaviṣayeti prāpte sati ekasya viṣayasya lopo draṣṭavya ityatītānubhavaviṣayatvaṃ labhyata iti manyante ।

[II,213,7]

atha arthajatvameva smateḥ kasmānneṣyate ? arthavināśe 'pyutpādāt । 1 yaddaśakālāliṅgite 'nabhavajñānamatpannaṃ tadālambanameva nyāyyam, smṛtikāle tasyāvidyamānatayā viṣayatvābhāvāt । bāhyendriyāṇāñca smṛtijanmani 7 vyābhacārādantaḥkaraṇasya vyāpāro niścīyate । na ca tasya svātantryeṇa bāhaviṣaye vyāpāraḥ sambhavatīti anarthajatvameva nyāyyam । avaśyañca yatva sati avyabhicāritvādidharmopetatvāt pramārūpatāyāṃ smṛteḥ pramāṇā uttavācyā । anamānādeśca vyāpārānupalabdherantaḥkaraṇasya svātantryeṇa "uttiā prāmāṇye sati smateraparokṣatvaṃ syāta, na caitadasti, tasmāniviṣayatvameva ।

{§ ārṣajñānavaidharmyam}

[II,213,17]

(“āmnāyavidhātaṇāmṛṣīṇāmatītānāgatavartamāneṣvatīndriyeṣu dharmā dhu granthopanibaddheṣvanapanibaddheṣa ca ātmamanasoḥ saṃyogād dharmaviśeṣācca yat prātibhaṃ yathātmanivedanaṃ jñānamutpadyate tad ārṣamityācakṣate । " prastāreṇa devarṣīṇāma, kadācideva laukikānāma, yathā kanyakā pāta śvo me bhrātā āganteti hadayaṃ me kathayatīti ।”)

[II,213,22]

atha ārṣajñānasya kāraṇaviṣayapramāṇanirūpaṇārtham * āmnāyavidhāta "m * ityādi prakaraṇam । āmnāyo vedaḥ śrutismṛtilakṣaṇaḥ, tasya vidhātāraḥ katāraḥ, teṣāmṛṣīṇāmutpadyate * yat prātibhaṃ jñānam * iti pratibhayā kārāvaśeṣeṇa nirvatitama । yathātmanivedanam * yathā tasya padārtha mā svarūpaṃ tanivedanama tadālambanamutpadyate * tad ārṣamityācakṣate । <II,214> keṣvartheṣūtpadyate ? * atītānāgatavartamāneṣu * । kiviśiṣṭeṣu ? * atīndriyeṣu dharmādiṣu * ādipadena paramāṇvādergrahaṇamiti । * granthopanibadveṣvanupanibaddheṣu ca * granthopanibaddheṣu ātmādiṣu〈〉, anupanivaddheṣu ca paramāṇvādiṣa iyān dharma iti । kutaḥ kāraṇādeṣu yathārthavijñānam ? * ātmamanasoḥ saṃyogāt * asamavāyinaḥ - dharmaviśeṣācca * nimittāditi । tatta prastāreṇa ṛṣīṇāma tastadārṣam । tattu kadācideva laukikānāmapyarṣīṇāmevaṃvidhaṃ vijñānamastīti । kima smadādīnāṃ?tra pramāṇamityāha * kadācideva lokikānām * tat prātibha jñānamiti । * yathā kanyakā bravīti śvo me bhrātā āganteti * । na cendriyaja tat, 〈〉tadvyāpāraṃ vināpyutpatteḥ ।

[II,214,10]

atha bāhyendriyāṇāṃ vyāpārāsambhave 'pi antaḥkaraṇasya vyāpārāt pratyakṣaphalatvam । sambandho 'pi indriyeṇa saha bhrātuḥ saṃyuktaviśeṣaṇaviśeṣya bhāvaḥ । tathā hi, tadviśiṣṭamātmānaṃ deśaṃ kālaṃ vā ālambyotpadyate jñāna metad ityuktaṃ paraiḥ । taccāsat, asyāparokṣatvānupa? patteḥ । yatra hi aparokṣajñānaṃ tatraiva indriyavyāpārakalpanā kriyate । na cātra tadastīti । na ca bahirviṣaye viśeṣaṇe 'pi manasaḥ svātantryeṇa vyāpāraḥ sambhavatītyuktam । liṅgaliṅgisambandhānusmaraṇānanubhavācca nānumānajam । śabda vināpyutpattana śābdam । ataḥ pramāṇāntaraphalametat । tathā praśne kṛte sati na pratyakṣādika nirdiśati, api tu - hṛdayaṃ me kathayatīti * brūte ।

[II,214,19]

atha kasmāt pratyakṣānumānānantaramārṣajñānasya na nirūpaṇam ? asmadādīnāṃ tena vyavahārābhāvāt । yatastattu prastāreṇa ṛṣīṇāmeva, kadācideva laukikānāmiti ।

{§ siddhadarśanasya vidyāntaratvanirāsaḥ}

[II,214,23]

(“siddha darśanaṃ na jñānāntaram । kasmāta ? prayatnapūrvakama añjanapādā pakhaḍgalikādisiddhānāṃ dṛśyadraṣṭaṇāṃ sukṣmavyavahitaviprakṛṣṭaṣva yad darśanaṃ tatpratyakṣameva । atha divyāntarikṣabhaumānāṃ prāṇināṃ graha kṣatrasañcārādinimittaṃ dharmādharmavipākadarśanamiṣṭaṃ tadapyanumānameva । aba <II,215> liṅgānapekṣaṃ dharmādiṣu darśanamiṣṭaṃ tadapi pratyakṣārṣayoranyatarasmina antaḥ bhūtamityevaṃ buddhiriti ।”)

[II,215,3]

siddhadarśanaṃ vidyāntaramiṣṭaṃ paraistaniṣedhārthamāha * siddhadarśanaṃ na śānāntaram * iti । ārṣajñānānantaramasya antarbhāvanirūpaṇam ārṣe 'pyanta nāvātham । yat siddhānāṃ darśanamutpadyate tatpratyakṣameva । keṣvartheṣu ? * sūkṣma pāhatāvaprakṛṣṭeṣu * iti । sūkṣmāḥ paramāṇavaḥ, vyavahitā nāgabhavanādayo dādāndriyāpekṣayā । na tu siddhendriyāṇāṃ vyavadhāyakamasti । viprakṛṣṭā pādayaḥ, teṣu । siddhānāṃ kiṃ viśiṣṭānām ? muktātmavyavacchedārthaṃ * dṛśya *ṇām * iti । kiñca teṣāṃ sadbhāve pramāṇamityāha dṛśyānām । cid añjanādiviyuktāḥ pratyakṣeṇāpyupalabhyante । kā punasteṣāṃ siddhirityāha janapādalepakhaḍagagalikādisiddhānāma iti । ādipadena cintāmaṇi vānā grahaṇam । añjanādivaśācca siddhendriyāṇāṃ sūkṣmādyarthaprakāśanam, ataḥ tat pratyakṣameva* 〈na〉 jñānāntaramiti ।

[II,215,14]

atha jyotiṣāmayanaṃ dṛṣṭvā prāṇināṃ śubhamaśubhaṃ vā bhaviṣyatīti jñānaṃ śāntaramiṣṭaṃ taniṣedhārtham * divyāntarikṣabhaumānām * ityādi । bhavaṃ divyamulkāpātādi, antarikṣe bhavañcāntarikṣaṃ digdāhādi, bhūmau bhāvaṃ bhaumaṃ bhūsañcalanādi, teṣām । * grahanakṣatrasañcārādinimittam * upalabhya prāṇināṃ dharmādharmayovipākaḥ phaladānasāmarthyaṃ taddarśanaṃ 〈na〉 jñānāntaramiṣṭam * tadapyanumānameva * liṅgadarśanānubandha smaraṇādijanyatvāt ।

[II,215,20]

yad vā divyāntarikṣabhaumānāṃ surasiddhamanuṣyāṇāṃ prāṇināṃ grahanakṣatra dinimittamupalabhya dharmādharmayovipākadarśana miṣṭaṃ tadapyanumānameveti ।

[II,215,22]

atha liṅagānapekṣaṃ dharmādharmādiṣu darśanamiṣṭaṃ tadapi yadi indriyārtha pādaparokṣamutpadyate pratyakṣameva । athendriyārthasannikarṣaṃ vinaiva dharma dutpadyate tathāpyārṣamityāha pratyakṣārṣaya ranyatarasminnantarbhūtamiti । buddhiārati * upasaṃhāraḥ paropagatāyā baddhevināśapara iti ।

{§ sukhavaidharmyam}

[II,215,27]

(“anugrahalakṣaṇaṃ sukham । nagādyabhipretaviṣayasānnidhye sati iṣṭopa<II,216>labdhīndriyārthasannikarṣād dharmādyapekṣād ātmamanasoḥ saṃyogād anugrahā bhiṣvaṅganayanādiprasādajanakamutpadyate tat sukham । atīteṣu viṣayaṣu smṛtijam । anāgateṣu saṅkalpajam । yattu viduṣām asatsu viṣayānuḥ smaraṇecchāsaṅa kalpeṣvāvirbhavati tad vidyāśamasantoṣadharmaviśeṣanimitta miti ।”)

[II,216,6]

atha buddheranantaraṃ sukhasya kāryakāraṇasvarūpopadarśanārtham * anugrahalakṣaṇa sukham * ityādi । anugrahalakṣaṇamanugrahasvarūpam । yasminnutpanne sati ātmā anugṛhītamātmānaṃ manyata iti । * sragādyabhipretaviṣayasānnidhye sati * iti । sragādayaśca te abhipretaviṣayāśceti teṣāṃ sānnidhyam । anabhipratā rāgādayaḥ sukhahetavo na bhavantīti abhipretagrahaṇam । iṣṭopalabdhiśca indriyā rthasannikarṣaśceti tathoktaṃ tasmāt । dharmādyapekṣādityādipadena dikkālādena haṇam । tānyapekṣata iti tadapekṣastasmāt । iṣṭopalabdhīndriyārthasannikaṣād dharmādyapekṣād ātmamanasoḥ saṃyogāt asamavāyikāraṇād ātmani sukha mutpadyate । * anugrahābhiṣvaṅganayanādiprasādajanakam * iti kāryanirūpaṇam । anugṛhītiranugrahaḥ sukhaviṣayaṃ jñānam, āsattirabhiṣvaṅa gaḥ, nayanādiprasāda prasannatā । ādipadena mukhādiprasannatā gṛhyata iti । tadetat asādhāraṇatvā ditarasmād bhedakamiti jñeyam । na ca sarvaṃ vivekinaḥ svarūpato duḥkham, anugrahātmakasya sukhasyāpyanubhavāt । ataeva na duḥkhābhāve sukhavyavahāra iti vācyam । vibhinna kāraṇajanyasya tīvratarādibhedabhinnasya pratibhāsanāt । evaṃ duḥkhasyāpi na sukhābhāvarūpateti ।

[II,216,21]

yadetaduktaṃ sukhaṃ tat sannihite vastuni indriyārthasannikarṣādutpadyata, atītānāgateṣu smaraṇasaṅkalpābhyāmityāha atīteṣu * sukhasādhana * smṛtijam, anāgateṣu saṅkalpajam * ityetad heyamupadarśitam ।

[II,216,24]

* yattu viduṣāmasatsu 〈〉viṣayānusmaraṇecchāsaṅkalpeṣa * viṣayānus raṇañcecchā ca saṅkalpaśceti tathoktāḥ, teṣvavidyamāneṣvāvirbhavati tadupādaka meva । * vidyāśamasantoṣadharmaviśeṣanimittam * iti kāraṇopanyāsaḥ । vidyā tattvajñānaṃ tasmāt tattvajñānināṃ sukham । tathā śamo rāgādiāvināśaḥ, <II,217> tasmācca śāntamanasāṃ sukham । santoṣo viṣayeṣvalampratyayaḥ, tasmācca sukham । keṣāścid dharmaviśeṣācceti ।

[II,217,3]

anye tu vidyayā janitaḥ saḥ śamaḥ, tasmāt sukhamiti । śeṣaṃ pūrvavat ।

{§ duḥkhavaidharmyam}

[II,217,5]

(“upaghātalakṣaṇaṃ duḥkham । viṣādyanabhipretaviṣayasānnidhye sati aniṣṭo dhāndriyārthasannikarṣāda adharmādyapekṣādātmamanasoḥ saṃyogāda yad mapighātadanyānimittamutpadyate, tad duḥkham । atīteṣu sarpavyāghracaurā diṣu smṛtijam । anāgateṣu saṅkalpajamiti ।”)

[II,217,9]

duḥkhanirūpaṇārthamāha * upaghātalakṣaṇam * upaghātasvarūpaṃ duḥkhamiti । tyata'neneti upahatamātmānaṃ manyata iti । kāraṇamāha 〈〉 * viṣādyanabhi viṣayasānnidhye sati | viṣādayaśca te 'nabhipretaviṣayāśceti, teṣāṃ navya satīti । abhipretāśca viṣayādayaḥ sūkhahetava evetyanabhipretagrahaṇama । jānnaṣṭopalabdhīndriyārthasannikarṣādadharmādyapekṣāta *7 aniṣṭopalabdhiśca apāyasannikarṣaśceti tathoktaḥ, tasmādadharmāpekṣādityādipadena dikkālāde 9m । tasmādaniṣṭopalabdhīndriyārthasannikarṣāda adharmādyapekṣādātmamanasoḥ saṃyogādasamavāyikāraṇāda ātmani samavetaṃ yad utpadyate tad daḥkham । paghātadanyānāṃ nimittaṃ kāraṇam, taditarasmād bhedakamiti jñeyam । laghu sādiṣviti kāryanirūpaṇam । amarṣo 'sahiṣṇutā, upahatirupaghāto lālambanaṃ jñānamiti । dainyaṃ dīnarūpatā daḥkhātpadyata iti । tadetada māraṇatvād itarasmāda bhedakamiti jñeyam । * atīteṣu sarpavyāghracaurā * duḥkhasādhaneṣu, * smṛtijam, anāgateṣu saṅkalpajamiti ।

{§ icchāvaidharmyam}

[II,217,23]

(“svārtha parārtha vā aprāptaprārthanecchā । sā cātmamanasoḥ saṃyogāta ukhādyapekṣāta smatyapekṣā vā utpadyate । prayatnasmṛtidharmādharmahetuḥ । kāmo 'bhilāṣaḥ, rāṇaḥ saṅkalpaḥ, kāruṇyama, vairāgyama, upadhā, bhāva ityeva mādaya icchābhedāḥ । maithunecchā kāmaḥ, abhyavahāracchā abhilāṣaḥ, punaḥ <II,218> punarviṣayānurañjanecchā rāgaḥ, anāsannakriyecchā saṅkalpaḥ, svārthamanapekṣya paraduḥkhaprahāṇecchā kāruṇyam, doṣadarśanād viṣayatyāgecchā vairāgyam, paravañcanecchā upadhā, antarnigūḍhecchā bhāvaḥ । cikī jihīrṣetyādi kriyābhedād icchābhedā bhavanti ।”)

[II,218,5]

icchāyāḥ kāryakāraṇasvarūpanirūpaṇārthaṃ * svārthaṃ parārtha vā * ityādi । aprāpte vastuni prārthanārūpatvādiccheti । svārthaṃ parārthaṃ veti vipratipatti nirāsārthaṃ vibhāgakathanam, na kevalaṃ svārthameva parārthamapi । utpatti kāraṇamāha * sā cātmamanasoḥ saṃyogāt * asamavāyikāraṇādutpadyate । kimapekṣāt ? * sukhādyapekṣāt smṛtyapekṣād vā * iti । * prayatnasmṛti dharmādharmahetuḥ * iti kāryanirūpaṇam । śuddhābhisandhirdhamaheturduṣṭābhisandhi ścādharmaheturiti ।

[II,218,12]

anye 'pi guṇāḥ kāmādayaḥ santi ca śabde ? te ca kiṃ na sucitā iti codyasya parihārārthamantarbhāvaṃ nirūpayati * kāmo 'bhilāṣo rāgaḥ saṅkalpaḥ kāruṇyaṃ vairāgyam upadhā bhāva ityevamādaya icchābhedāḥ * tadviśeṣā iti । maithunecchā kāmaḥ, tatsadbhāve kāmīti vyapadeśāt, necchāmātramiti । abhyava haraṇecchā abhilāṣaḥ, abhilāṣalakṣaṇecchā । sāmānyena sarvasmin vastuni abhyavaharaṇamādānaṃ vivakṣitam । tadicchā abhilāṣa iti cānye । * punaḥ punarviṣayānurañjanecchā rāgaḥ * tena hi satā rāgīti vyapadeśāt । anāsanna kriyāyām anāgatakriyāyāmicchā saṅkalpaḥ । * svārthamanapekṣya paraduḥkhaprahā ṇecchā * tadvināśecchā kāruṇyam । doṣadarśanād viṣayeṣu parityāgecchā vairāgyam । tat sadbhāve viraktavyavahārāt । * paravañcanecchā upadhā । antarnigūḍhecchā bhāvaḥ * iti । yadyapi icchā sarvā antarna bāhyeti; tathāpi iyamanyāpekṣayā kathañcid vijñāyata ityantanigūḍhetyucyate । * cikīrṣā jihīretyādikriyābhedādicchābhedā bhavanti * kartumicchā cikīrṣā, hartumicchā jihīrṣeti ।

{§ dveṣavaidharmyam}

[II,218,27]

(“prajvalanātmako dveṣaḥ । yasmin sati prajvalitamivātmānaṃ manyate, <II,219> sa dveṣaḥ । sa cātmamanasoḥ saṃyogād duḥkhāpekṣāt smṛtyapekṣād votpadyate । prayatnasmṛtidharmādharmahetuḥ । drohaḥ, krodhaḥ, manyurakṣamā amarṣa iti dveṣabhedāḥ ।”)

[II,219,4]

dveṣanirūpaṇārthamāha 〈〉* prajvalanātmakaḥ prajvalanasvarūpo dveṣaḥ । * yasmin sati prajvalitamivātmānaṃ manyate, sa dveṣaḥ । iti pūrvasya vivaraṇam । * sa cātmanasoḥ saṃyogāt । asamavāyikāraṇāt, * duḥkhāpekṣāt smṛtyapekṣād vā * ātmanyutpadyata iti । * prayatnasmṛtidharmādharmahetuḥ * iti kāryanirūpaṇam । yathā hi dveṣād vadhādau pravarttamānasyādharmo bhavatyevaṃ yajanādau pravarttamānasya dharmo 'pīti । bhedanirūpaṇārthamāha *drohaḥ krodho manyurakṣamā amarṣa iti dveṣabhedāḥ * tadviśeṣā iti । svāmino 'pakāro drohaḥ, krodhastu yasminnutpanne śarīrendriyāvayavānāṃ vikāraḥ sampadyate । manyurapakṛtasyāpa kartumasamarthasya kaṇṭhākṣavikārajanakaḥ । akṣamā asahiṣṇutā । amarṣo 'pa karturvarṣādivyavadhānenāpya〈〉pa karaṇam ।

[II,219,14]

nanvete sukhaduḥkhecchādveṣāḥ kathaṃ vijñānād vyatiricyante, samānakāraṇa janyatvād antarmukhākāratayā pratīyamānatvācceti kāraṇabhedena hi padārthā bhidyanta ityuktam । 〈 taduktam 〉
	tadatadrūpiṇo bhāvāstadatadrūpahetujāḥ /
	tatsukhādi kimajñānaṃ vijñānābhinnahetujam //
	<= pra. vā. 2.251> iti ।

[II,219,20]

tathā hi, kecid bhāvastadrūpiṇo dhānyādirūpiṇaḥ, anye 'tadrūpiṇastad vidharmāṇa iti । kasmāt ? tadatadrūpahetujatvāt । dhānyarūpāt kāraṇādutpannā stadrūpiṇaḥ, anye tu vilakṣaṇā atadrūpiṇaḥ, ityukte satyāha yadyevaṃ tatsukhādi vijñānenābhinnahetujaṃ kimajñānamiṣṭam ? naitadevam, abhede sādhye samavāyya samavāyinimittāpekṣayāpi samānakāraṇajanyatvasya vyabhicārāt । tathā hi, ekasmāt samavāyikāraṇādutpadyante pākajāḥ parasparaṃ vibhinnāśceti । asamavāyikāraṇantu pārthivaparamāṇvagnisaṃyogasteṣāmeka eva । tathā eko 'pyuṣṇasparśasteṣāṃ nimittakāraṇamiti, tadapekṣayāpi vyabhicāraḥ । sāmagracapekṣayā <II,220> tvasiddhaṃ samānakāraṇajanyatvam, tasyāḥ pratikāryaniyatatvāt । uktañca ekatra sragādyapalakṣitā sāmagrī kāraṇam, anyatrānyathābhateti । tathā pratiniyatajātaḥ prāgabhāvasya cānupraveśe sarvatra sāmagrībhedo bhavatyeveti । antarmukhākāratayā pratīyamānatvañca jñānadharmarvyabhicārīti । asti ca dharmadharmiṇorbheda ityuktam । tathā jñānasyānutpattivināśābhyāṃ vyabhicāraḥ, tayorantarmukhākāratayā pratāya mānatvam, na ca bodharūpatetyalamatiprasaṅgena ।

{§ prayatnavaidharmyam}

[II,220,8]

(“prayatnaḥ saṃrambha utsāha iti paryāyāḥ । sa dvividho jīvanapūrvaka, icchādveṣapūrvakaśca । tatra jīvanapūrvakaḥ suptasya prāṇāpānasantānaprakā, prabodhakāle ca antaḥkaraṇasyendriyāntaraprāptihetuḥ । asya jīvanapūrva kasya ātmamanasoḥ saṃyogād dharmādharmāpekṣādutpattiḥ । itarastu hitāhita prāptiparihārasamarthasya vyāpārasya hetaḥ, śarīravidhārakaśca । saca ātmamanasoḥ saṃyogād icchāpekṣād dveṣāpekṣād botpadyate ।”)

[II,220,14]

atha prayatnasya kāraṇasvarūpavibhāganirūpaṇārthamāha * prayatnaḥ saramma utsāha iti paryāyāḥ * lakṣaṇam, asādhāraṇatvāt । tathā hi, prayatna itara smād bhidyate, anādikālapravāhāyātetthambhūtaparyāyābhidheyatvāt, yastu । bhidyate, na cāsāvevam, yathā rūpādiriti । sa dvividhaḥ kāraṇabhedādityāha * jīvanapūrvaka icchādveṣapūrvakaśca jīvanaṃ pūrva kāraṇamasyeti jīvanapūrvakaḥ । sa kathaṃ vijñāyata ityāha * suptasya prāṇāpānasantānaprerakaḥ * iti । 55 suptasya prāṇāpānasantānakriyā, sā prayatnakāryā śarīra〈〉 kriyātvāt, jāpa vasthāyāṃ prāṇakriyādivaditi । na paraṃ prāṇādisantānaprerakaḥ * prabāyakā. cāntaḥkaraṇasyendriyāntareṇa prāptihetuḥ * iti । yathā hi prabāyata yenaivendriyeṇopalambhastenaiva sambandhārthamantaḥkaraṇasya nirindriyātmā vartamānasyāvaśyaṃ karmābhyupeyam, tacca prayatnakārya parigṛhītāntara karmatvāt, jāgradavasthāyāṃ tatkarmavat । ata eva nādṛṣṭasyaivātra kāraṇa anamānena prayatnakāryatvopalabdheḥ । kāraṇāntarāsambhave cādṛṣṭasyavānā kāraṇatvamiṣyata iti ।

<II,221>

[II,221,1]

sthite hi sadbhāve jīvanapūrvakasyotpattikāraṇamāha * ātmamanasoḥ pāgāt * asamavāyikāraṇāda viśiṣṭadharmādharmāpekṣādatpattiriti । itarastu raṇadvaṣapūrvakaḥ * hitāhitaprāptiparihārasamarthasya vyāpārasya * kāyikavyāpārasya hetuḥ । tathā * śarīravidhārakaśca * । tena hi pratibaddhaṃ śarīre gurutvaṃ na patanamārabhate । tasyotpattikāraṇamāha * ātmamanasoḥ saṃyogāta * asamavāyi kāraṇāt । * icchāpekṣāda dveṣāpekṣād votpadyate * iti ।

{§ gurutvavaidharmyam}

[II,221,8]

(“gurutva jalabhūmyoḥ patanakarmakāraṇam । apratyakṣama, patanakarmānumeyama, palasaskāravirodhi । asya ca abādiparamāṇurūpādivannityānityatvaniṣpattayaḥ ।”)

[II,221,11]

gurutvasya lakṣaṇaparīkṣārthaṃ garutvaṃ jalabhamyoḥ' ityādi prakaraṇama । pratyakṣatve sati patanakarmakāraṇatvād gurutvam itarasmād miyata ।
padāpekṣaṃ vā lakṣaṇam । jā
gurutvam । raso 'pi jalabhūna 〈〉vā?ca kāraṇātiśayana bhāvena pātātiśayābhā nāstīti na rasaḥ kāraṇa
patanakarmakāraṇamityapratyakṣagrahaṇam । jalabhamyoti āśrayānarū vā lakṣaṇam । jalabhamyoreva vartamānatve sati patanakarmakāraṇatvāda
। raso 'pi jalabhamyoreva vartate, na tu patanakāraṇama, abhyupagame 'kāraṇātiśayena kāryātiśayasya anyatropalabdhaḥ pāṣāṇāde rasātiśayā
tātiśayābhāvaḥ. pippalyādau ca tatsadbhāvena sadabhāvaḥ syāta । sa śati na rasaḥ kāraṇaṃ patanotpattau । rūpādeśca kāraṇatve analādāvapi pat pātaḥ syāt, na cāstītyato rūpādivyatiriktaṃ kāraṇamanumīyata
maha* patanakarmānameyama iti । ādyasya hi patanakarmaṇo 'samavāyi " gurutvam, dvitīyādestu saṃskāro 'pīti । sa cāsau jalabhūmyoreva
kāraṇaṃ gurutvam, dvitīyādava vartate ।
pratyakṣatāprasaṅgāt । atha ca tat pṛthivyādigurutvaḥ

[II,221,22]

nanu tvagindriyasya vyāpārāta pañcapalaṃ daśapalamiti pratibhāsanād - satyakṣam ? na. tvagindriyeṇa sambandhopapatteḥ pṛthivyādigarutvasyāpi pratyakṣatāprasaṅgāt । atha ādheyagatameva gurutvaṃ paricchinatti tvagindriyam, na cavyādigurutve 'stīti । nanvevamapi makṣikādigurutvaṃ paricchindyāt, <II,222> tasyāpyādheyagatatvāditi । na ca tasya aviśiṣṭatvādaparicchedaḥ, pratyakṣadravyasa mavāyasyāviśeṣāt । atha adhogatihetutvaṃ vaiśiṣṭayam ? tarhi tvagindriyasamba ndhena adhogativiśeṣamupalabhamānasya pañcapalaṃ daśapalamityānumānika eva pratyayaḥ ।

[II,222,5]

atha daśapalaistantubhirārabdhe paṭe gurutvātiśayasyānupalabdheḥ, kāraṇa eva gurutvam, na tu kārye । tadasat, ubhayatrāpi pātopalabdheḥ । na ca svagatagurutvā bhāve 'pi āśrayāntaragurutvādeva patanam, vāyvāderapi pātaprasaṅgāt । tasmāduḥ bhayatrāpi kāryeṇa sadbhāvasiddhergurutvamastīti । avanativiśeṣānupalambhaśca kārye makṣikādigurutvasamparkeṇāpi samāna iti । tathā hi, tantuṣu mīyamāna makṣikādisamparke 'pi avanativiśeṣā nopalabhyante, na ca tadgurutvasyāsattva mityalam ।

[II,222,12]

atha gurutvasya pātahetutve kimiti sarvadā pāto na bhavati ? pratibandhā dityāha * saṃyogaprayatnasaṃskāravirodhi * iti । vṛntaphalasaṃyogena pratibaddha na phale patanamārabhate, prayatnapratibandhād ākāśāvasthiteṣu śakuniṣu gurutvaṃ na patanaṃ karoti, dhanunikṣipteṣu śareṣu gurutvaṃ na patanaṃ karoti vegākhyasaṃskā pratibandhāt, eṣāmapāye phalādiṣu pātadarśanāt ।

[II,222,17]

* tasya cābādiparamāṇurūpādivannityānityatvaniṣpattayaḥ iti । abādayaśca te paramāṇavaśceti tathoktāḥ, tatparamāṇurūpādīnāmiveti । yathā āpyaparamāṇurūpādīnāmaniṣpadyamānatvānnityatvam, evameva gurutvaṃ nityeṣvāna ṣpattainityam, anitye tu kāraṇaguṇapūrvaprakrameṇa niṣpadyamānatvāt tadrūpavadevāni tyamityatideśārthaḥ ।

{§ dravatvavaidharmyam}

[II,222,23]

(“dravatvaṃ spandanakarmakāraṇam । tridravyavṛtti । tatta dvividham, sāsira ddhikama, laimittikañca । sāṃsiddhikabhapāṃ viśeṣaguṇaḥ । naimittikaṃ pṛthivā tejasoḥ sāmānyaguṇaḥ । sāṃsiddhikasya gurutvavannityānityatvaniṣpattayaḥ ।”)

[II,222,26]

(“saṅghātadarśanāt sāṃsiddhikatvamayuktamiti cet, na, divyatejaḥ<II,223>saṃyuktānāmāpyānāṃ paramāṇanāṃ parasparaṃ saṃyogo dravyārambhakaḥ saṅghātākhyaḥ, sana paramāṇudravatvastha pratibandhāt kārye himakarakādau dravatvānutpattiḥ ।”)

[II,223,3]

(“namittikañca pathivītejasoragnisaṃyogajam । katham ? sapirjatu pūcchiṣṭādīnāṃ kāraṇeṣu paramāṇaṣvagnisaṃyogād vegāpekṣāt karmotpattī rājabhyo vibhāgebhyo dravyārambhakasaṃyogavināśāt kāryadravyanivṛttāvagni yāgād auṣṇyāpekṣāta svatantreṣa paramāṇaṣa dravatvamūtpadyate । tatasteṣa nāganāmadaṣṭāpekṣāda ātmāṇasaṃyogāta karmotpattau tajjebhyaḥ saṃyogebhyo vaṣaṇukādiprakrameṇa kāryadravyamutpadyate, tasmiṃśca rūpāyutpattisamakālaṃ kāraṇaguṇaprakrameṇa dravatvamutpadyata iti ।”)

[II,223,10]

dravatvasya lakṣaṇaparīkṣārthamāha*dravatvaṃ syandanakarmakāraṇam iti । syandana - vakṣyamāṇam । tatkāraṇaṃ dravatvamityukte vegena vyabhicāraḥ, tadarthaṃ tridravya ta । tathāpi nidravyavattitvaṃ vegasyāpi sambhavatīti niyameneti padamūhyam । rūpantu niyamena tridravyavṛtti, na tu syandanakamakāraṇam । sarasmā dbhidyate, niyamena tridravyavṛttitve sati syandanakarmakāraṇatvāditi ।

[II,223,15]

tattu dvividhamiti vibhāgaḥ । kena rūpeṇa ? sāṃsiddhikaṃ naimittika pati । tayoḥ parasparaṃ vailakṣaṇyanirūpaṇārthamāha * sāṃsiddhikamapāṃ viśeṣaguṇaḥ, naimittika pṛthivītejasoḥ sāmānyaguṇaḥ * iti parasparabhedaḥ । * sāṃsiddhi "tya gurutvavannityānityatvaniṣpattayaḥ iti । yathā gurutvaṃ nityeṣvaniṣpadya mānatvānnityama anityeṣa niṣpatteranityaṃ kāraṇaguṇapūrvakamāśrayavināśācca vinaśyati, evaṃ sāṃsiddhikadravatvamapītyatideśārthaḥ ।

[II,223,21]

nanu cāyuktametad apāṃ sāṃsiddhikadravyatvamiti, himakarakādāvanupa bhāt ? * tadāha saṅghātadarśanāt sāṃsiddhikatvamayuktamiti cet, * naitadevam । patra salile sāṃsiddhikadravatvasyopalabdheḥ, āpyaparamāṇuṣu tatsadbhāvasiddhau himakarakādo tasyānatpādāta pratibandhakamastīti niścīyate । tacca anyasyāna palambhād divyatejaḥsaṃyoga evetyāha - divyatejaḥsaṃyuktānāmāpyānāṃ paramāṇūnāṃ raspara saṃyogo dravyārambhakaḥ * । sa ca * saṅghātākhyaḥ, tena paramāṇudravatvasya tibandhāt kārye himakarakādau dravatvānutpattiḥ * iti । tejaḥsadbhāvastu <II,224> sphoṭādikāryānumeyaḥ । tathā ca himakarakāsambandhādupalabhyate sphoṭādilakṣaṇaṃ kārya śarīre vṛkṣādau ca dāha iti । vilayanañcāsya divyatejaḥsambandhāt । avayave kriyā, tato vibhāgastasmāt saṃyoganivṛttau dravyavināśe sati paramāṇavaḥ kāryamārabhante । tatra ca divyatejaḥsaṃyogasya pratibandhakasya nivṛtteḥ paramāṇudravatvaṃ kārye dravatvamārabhate ।

[II,224,6]

na cedaṃ naimittikam, sarpirādāviva punaḥ saṃgrahānupalabdheḥ । yathāhi naimittikadravatvaṃ sarpirādāviti drutasya saṃgrahaḥ, tathehā'pi syāt । na caitadastīti ।

[II,224,9]

* naimittikañca pṛthivītejasoragnisaṃyogajam * । kathamityavyutpannapraśnaḥ । tatrāha sarpirādīnāṃ kāraṇeṣvityādipadena sūtroktānāṃ saṃgrahaḥ । tathā hi sapirjatumadhūcchiṣṭānāṃ pārthivānāmagnisaṃyogād dravatvamadbhiḥ sāmānyam । trapusosaloharajatasuvarṇānāṃ taijasānāmagnisaṃyogādravatvamadbhiḥ sāmānyamiti <= vai. sū. 2.1154-55> । ataḥ sapirādikāraṇeṣu ca paramāṇuṣvagnisaṃyogā pekṣā vegāpekṣāt karmotpattau satyantato vibhāgā jāyante । tebhyo vibhāgebhyoṃ dravyārambhakasaṃyogavināśaḥ, tataḥ kāryadravyanivṛttistasyāñca satyāmagni saṃyogād auṣṇyāpekṣāt svatantreṣu paramāṇuṣu dravatvamutpadyate । paramāṇavaḥ sabhavāyikāraṇam, agnisaṃyogo 'samavāyikāraṇamuṣṇasparśī nimittakāraṇa miti । tato 'nantaramutpannadravatveṣu * bhogināmadṛṣṭāpekṣādātmāṇusaṃyogāt * karmotpadyata iti । paramāṇuḥ samavāyikāraṇam, ātmāṇusaṃyogo 'samavāya kāraṇam, bhogināmadṛṣṭo nimittakāraṇamiti । tato vibhāgebhyaḥ prāktana saṃyogavināśe sati tebhyaḥ karmabhyaḥ paramāṇvantareṇa saṃyogā jāyante । tebhyaḥ saṃyogebhyo dvacaṇukāṇyutpadyante । tadādikrameṇa dvyaṇukādikāryamutpadyata । tasmiṃśca dvyaṇukādau * rūpādyutpattisamakālaṃ kāraṇaguṇapūrvakrameṇa dravatvamutpadyara iti * pākajotpattinyāyo 'tra draṣṭavyaḥ । etāvāṃstuviśeṣaḥ, tatrāvaśyaṃ rūpāvi nivṛttirna caivaṃ dravatvasyeti ।

{§ snehavaidharmyam}

[II,224,27]

(“sneho 'pāṃ viśeṣaguṇaḥ । saṃgrahamṛjādihetaḥ । asyāpi guruvāra nityānityatvaniṣpattayaḥ ।”)

<II,225>

[II,225,1]

snehasya lakṣaṇaparīkṣārthaṃ * sneho 'pāṃ viśeṣaguṇaḥ saṅgrahamajādihetuḥ * śata । apāṃ viśeṣaguṇo rūpādirapīti saṅgrahamṛjādiheturiti padam । saṅgrahaḥ piṇḍīkaraṇam । mṛjā tu viśadatvam । taddhatutvāditarasmād bhidyate ।

[II,225,4]

nanu snehasyābhinavapallavādāvupalambhād udakaviśeṣaguṇatvamasiddham ? , sayuktasamavāyenopalambhāt । saṃyukta hi pallavādinā udakaṃ tatsamaveta nahā gṛhyate, tadapāye tasyānupalabdheḥ, tathā snānottarakālaṃ keśādau 'nagdhapratyayadarśanāt । yathā ca saṃyogyāśrayavaiguṇyābhāve sarvasminnudake snigdha sāna nave sarvasyāṃ pṛthivyāmiti । asyāpi gurutvavannityānityatvaniṣpattaya sasa । nityeṣu nityo 'nityeṣu kāraṇaguṇapūrvaḥ, āśrayavināśād vinaśyatīti ।

{§ saṃskāravaidharmyam}

[II,225,11]

(“sarakārastrividho go bhāvanā sthitisthāpakaśca । tatra " sūtimattu pañcasu dravye nivittaviśeṣāpekṣāta karmaṇo jāyate, pādikaliyāprabandhahetuḥ sparśavadāvyasaṃyogaviśeṣavirodhī kvacita kāraṇaguṇapūrvakrameṇotpadyate ।”)

[II,225,15]

saskāranirūpaṇārthamāha * saṃskārastrividhaḥ * । kena rūpeṇa ? vego bhāvanā tasthāpakatveneti । vibhāga evāsādhāraṇatvāllakṣaṇamiti, tallakṣaṇa citryajñāpanārthametat । tatra vegasya samānajātīyāt bhedamāśrayañca nirūpa nāha* mūrtimatsū * ityādi । mūrtimatsu dravyeṣu । na jñāyate kiyatsu, tadarthaṃ * pañcasu * । tathāpi na jñāyate keṣu, tadarthaṃ * mūrtimatsu * ityāśrayanirūpaṇam । "1 vā saṃskāratve sati pañcasu mūrtimatsveva vartamānatvād vega iti lakṣaṇam ।

[II,225,21]

kāraṇamāha nimittaviśeṣāpekṣāt karmaṇo jāyate iti । saṃyogavibhāgayoḥ tvamiti nimittaviśeṣāpekṣāditi viśeṣaṇam । nimittaviśeṣo nodanā atisaṃyuktasaṃyogāḥ, tadapekṣāditi । karma asamavāyikāraṇam, svakāraṇa sapā nodanādinimittakāraṇama, vegādhārastū samavāyikāraṇamitya raṇatvāllakṣaṇaṃ cedama । kāryasāha niyatāyāṃ diśi kriyāprabandhasya kriyāsantānasya heturiti ।

[II,225,27]

nanu cāyuktametat, aniyatadigadeśasya bhramaṇākhyasyāpi karmaṇaḥ kāraṇa<II,226>tvāt, satyametat, tathāpyadoṣaḥ, niyatadikriyāprabandhasyaiva heturityavadhāra ṇānabhyupagamāt । so 'pi niyatāyāmeva diśi kriyāprabandha iti cānye । ani yatadikriyāprabandhaheturityavadhāraṇasyātra pūrvarūpatāṃ manyamānā vyākhyāntara kurvate । tasya vināśakāraṇamāha * sparśavadravyasaṃyogaviśeṣavirodhī * iti । sparśavadravyasaṃyogamātravirodhitve vāyusaṃyogena virodhādiṣorgamanaṃ na syāt, taddhetoāgasya vināśāditi viśeṣagrahaṇama, kaṭhināvayavasaṃyogenādāvāpa tadvināśopalabdheḥ ।

[II,226,8]

nanvevamapyākāśe prakṣiptasyeṣonibiḍāvayavasaṃyogasya vegavināśakasyā bhāvādapātaḥ syāt, na, anekakāryakaraṇe sparśavadravyasaṃyogamātreṇāpi vinā śasyānvayavyatirekābhyāmupalambhāt । tathā ca kṣiptasyeṣorvegavināśopalabdha ravaśyaṃ kāraṇamabhidheyam, nirhetukavināśapratiṣedhāt । ato vāyusaṃyogenāpyaneka kāryakaraṇe sati virudhyate, adṛṣṭaprakṣayād veti । * kvacit kāraṇaguṇapūva prakrameṇotpadyate * yathā parvatasrotasāmadhaḥpatatāṃ saṃyoge satyekasminnudaka samutpanne rūpādivat kāraṇavegād bego 'pīti ।

[II,226,15]

(“bhāvanāsajñakastvātmaguṇo dṛṣṭaśrutānubhūteṣvartheṣu smṛtipratyābha jñānaheturbhavati, jñānamadaduḥkhādivirodhī । paṭvabhyāsādarapratyayajaḥ paṭṭa pratyayāpekṣādātmamanasoḥ saṃyogād āścarye 'rthe paṭaḥ saṃskārātiśayā jāyate । yathā dākṣiṇātyasyoṣṭradarśanāditi । vidyāśilpavyāyāmādi pvabhyasyamāneṣu tasminnevārthe pūrvapūrvasaṃskāramapekṣamāṇāduttarottarasmāra pratyayādātmamanasoḥ saṃyogāt saṃskārātiśayo jāyate । prayatnena manāna kṣuṣi sthāpayitvā aparvamartha didakṣamāṇasya vidyatasampātadarśanavadāra pratyayaḥ, tamapekṣamāṇādātmamanasoḥ saṃyogāta saṃskārātiśayo jāyate । yathā devahūde sauvarṇarājatapadmadarśanāditi ।”)

[II,226,24]

bhāvanāsaṃjñakastvātmaguṇatvāditarasmād bhidyate । na ca buddhayādiā' bhicāraḥ, saṃskārasya sato 'vāntaraviśeṣanirūpaṇāt । * smṛtipratyabhijñānahara iti kāryanirūpaṇam, sadbhāve pramāṇañceti । “smṛtirvāsanākhyāt” bhavati, <II,227> tathāktamātmādhikāre । keṣu smṛtipratyabhijñānaheturityāha * dṛṣṭa śrutānubhūteṣu । iti, nirṇītārtheṣviti bhāvaḥ ।

[II,227,3]

nāśakāraṇamāha * jñānamadadaḥkhādivirodhī * iti । jñānaṃ pratipakṣajñānaṃ vivakṣitam, tena virudhyate, yathā ātmādijñānajanitaḥ saṃskāro nairātmyā camyāseneti, tasmin sati tatrāsmaraṇāt । svamadena virodhaḥ, bālāvasthānubhavajanitasaṃskārasya punaryavāvasthāyāṃ viṣayābhibhūtasya tatrāsmaraṇāt । utkhana, yathā śāstrānubhavajanitasaṃskārasya tīvraṇa dārādiduḥkheneti, tena satā tatrāsmaraṇāt । ādipadena tu krodhāderapi saṃskāranivartakatvamuktam ।

[II,227,9]

tasyotpattikāraṇamāha paṭavabhyāsādarapratyayebhyo jātastatpratyayaja ta । paṭupratyayāpekṣādātmamanasoḥ saṃyogādasamavāyikāraṇādātmanyāścarye 'rthe " saṃskāro jāyate, * yathā dākṣiṇātyasyoṣṭradarśanāt । sa cātiśayena smṛtiheturbhavatīti । (abhyāsād) * vidyāśilpavyāyāmādiṣvabhya mānaṣu tasminnevārthe pūrvapūrvasaṃskāramapekṣamāṇādattarottarasmāt pratyayā
manasoḥ saṃyogāt saṃskārātiśayo jāyate । pūrvapūrvasaṃskārāpekṣo hi sarāttarapratyayo 'bhyāsaḥ, tamapekṣamāṇādātmamanasoḥ saṃyogādasamavāyikāraṇā "māna saskārātiśayo jāyate * । tatra vidyāyāma upādhyāyoccaritapadaśravaṇe ka saṃskāraḥ । pūnarvivakṣādikrameṇa svayamuccāraṇe sati tu jñānaṃ pūrva skārāpekṣaṃ saṃskārāntaramārabhate । punastaduccāraṇe sati tajjñānaṃ pūrvasaṃskā pakṣa saṃskārāntaramārabhata ityevaṃ tricaturādiparivarttane satyantyapadānubhavāt saskārāpekṣāta saṃskārātiśayo jāyate । etaccāvaśyamabhyupeyam, anyathā savayathya syāt । na cātiprasaṅgaḥ, adṛṣṭasya vyavasthāhetutvāt । na ca bhāsta sarvatra sadabhāvaḥ, kāryasya smaraṇasya sarvatrānupalabdheḥ । yatra hi ṇamāsta tatraiva pūrvasaṃskārāpekṣaṃ jñānaṃ saṃskāramārabhata iti । āntare pāsa pūrvapūrvasaṃskārāpekṣaṃ niyatārthasmaraṇameva saṃskāramārabhata iti yam । evaṃ śilpe 'pyapādhyāyalikhitacitradarśanāta saṃskāraḥ, punaḥ svayaṃ pādhopalabhate; tadanubhavaḥ pūrvasaṃskārāpekṣaḥ saṃskārāntaramārabhate, punaḥ svayaṃ khatvopalabhate, tadanabhavaḥ pūrvasaṃskārāpekṣaḥ saṃskārāntaramārabhate, ityevaṃ <II,228> dvinyādiparivarttanena saṃskārātiśayaḥ । vyāyāme 'pi upādhyāyena dhanurvedapari paṭhitanyāyena prayukteṣūpalambhādupajāte saṃskāre punastadanusāritayā svayaṃ prayukta tadanubhavena pūrvasaṃskārāpekṣeṇa saṃskārāntaramārabhyate, punastathaiva prayoge sati tadanubhavena pūrvasaṃskārāpekṣeṇānyaḥ saṃskāra ityevamantyānubhavāt saṃskārātiśaya iti ।

[II,228,6]

ādarapratyayajasaṃskāramāha * prayatlena manaḥ cakṣuṣi sthāpayitvā apūrvamartha didṛkṣamāṇasya - iti, draṣṭumicchato vidyutsampātadarśanena tulyaṃ vartate, iti tadarśanavadādarapratyayaḥ । tamapekṣamāṇādātmamanasoḥ saṃyogādasamavāyikāraṇā dātmani saṃskārātiśayo jāyate । * yathā devahrade sauvarṇarājatapadmadarśanā * - diti । tatra hi sauvarṇarājatapatrayorutthānamāgamāllokapravādato vā samupalabhya punaviśiṣṭayātrāsamaye prayatnena saṃskārātiśayo bhavatīti ।

[II,228,12]

(“sthitisthāpakastu sparśavadravyeṣu vartamāno dhanāvayavatanniveśa viśiṣṭeṣu kālāntarāvasthāyidhu svābhayamandhākṛtaṃ yathāvat sthāpayati । sthāvarajaṅgamavikāreṣu dhanuḥśākhādantaśṛṅgāsthisūtravastrādiṣu bhugnasaṃtiteṣu sthitisthāpakasya kārya saṃlakṣyate । nityānityatvaniṣpa ttayo 'syāpi gurutvavat draṣṭavyā ।”)

[II,228,17]

sthitisthāpakastu saṃskāratve sati sparśavatsveva dravyeṣu vartamānatvā ditarasmāda bhidyate । kiṃ bhūteṣu ? * dhanāvayavasanniveśaviśiṣṭaṣu 5 iti । ghanāśca te avayavāśca, teṣāṃ sanniveśo racanāviśeṣaḥ । ghana iti sanniveśasya vā viśeṣaṇam, tadviśiṣṭeṣu । * kālāntarāvasthāyiṣu svāśrayamanyathākṛtaṃ yathāvat sthāpayati * ityataḥ sthitisthāpakaḥ ।

[II,228,22]

sadbhāve pramāṇamāha sthāvarāśca jaṅgamāśceti tathoktāsteṣāṃ vikāreṣu dhanuḥśākhādantaśṛṅgāsthiṣu, sūtravastrādiṣu ca bhagneṣu saṃvartiteṣu piṇḍī kṛteṣu tasya kārya saṃlakṣyate । tathā hi dhanuṣi śākhādī ca ākarṣaṇakarmaṇyupa jāte nodanādibhyastannivṛttāvapi karmopalambhādavaśyamasamavāyikāraṇaṃ vācyam, vastunastadantareṇānutpatteḥ । na ca nodanāderanyatamaḥ sambhāvyata ityanyenāsama vāyikāraṇena bhavitavyam, kriyāvibhāgayośca kriyotpattāvakāraṇatvopalambhāt । <II,229> tathā tannivṛttāvapi pratibandhakābhāve sati śākhādau pūrvāvasthāvasthāpakakarmopa lambhānimittāntarameva nyāyyam । adṛṣṭa viśeṣasya tu sādhāraṇatvāt kāraṇatvaṃ na pratiṣiddhayata iti ।

[II,229,4]

* nityānityatvaniṣpattayo 'pyasya gurutvavad draṣṭavyā * iti । yathā hi garutvaṃ nityeṣu nityamutpattivināśakāraṇābhāvādanityeṣu kāraṇapūrvakamāśraya vināśād vinaśyati evaṃ sthitisthāpakasaṃskāro 'pīti । kārye tu sthiti sthāpakasaṃskāraprasiddhestadārambhakaparamāṇuṣvapi tatkalpanā kriyate ।

{§ dharmavaidharmyam}

[II,229,9]

(“dharmaḥ puruṣaguṇaḥ, kartuḥ priyahitamokṣahetuḥ, atīndriyo 'ntya sukhasaṃvijñānavirodhī, puruṣāntaḥkaraṇasaṃyogaviśuddhābhisandhijaḥ, varṇā śramiṇāṃ pratiniyatasādhananimittaḥ । tasya tu sādhanāni śrutismṛti vihitāni varṇāśramiṇāṃ sāmānyaviśeṣabhāvenāvasthitāni dravyaguṇa karmāṇi ।”)

[II,229,14]

dharmasya lakṣaṇaparokṣārthamāha * dharmaḥ puruṣaguṇaḥ * ityādi । puruṣaguṇatvaṃ buddhayādāvapītyataḥ * priyahitamokṣahetuḥ * iti । priyaṃ sukham, hitaṃ tatsādhanam । navānāmātmaviśeṣaguṇānāmatyantocchittirmokṣa iti । atheśvarajñānamapyeṣāṃ heturataḥ karturiti । yena hi kṛto dharmastatraiva priyahitamokṣahetuḥ, na caivamīśvarajñānasya, akāryatayā karturabhāvāditi । atha tattvajñānaṃ karturyathoktaphalahetustadarthamatīndriya iti । saṃskāro 'pi smṛtidvāreṇaiva bhavatītyato 'ntyasukhasaṃvijñānavirodhīti । antyamāvasānikaṃ sukhaṃ tatsaṃvedanena virudhyate ।

[II,229,22]

nanvevamapi atīndriyatve satyantyasukhasaṃvijñānavirodhitvāt, dharmaḥ itarasmād bhidyata ityukte vyabhicārābhāvād vyarthaṃ śeṣābhidhānam, na, anya svāt kartuḥ । priyahitamokṣaheturiti viśiṣṭārthakriyānirūpaṇam । puruṣaguṇa ityanyathābhāvapratiṣedhārtham ।

[II,229,26]

atha puruṣaguṇatve kiṃ pramāṇam ? anumānamāgamaśca । tathā hi tanu bhuvanādikāryam, puruṣaguṇapūrvakam, vicitrakāryatvād, rathādivaditi । yathāhi <II,230> rathādikartā bhokturabhiprāyaṃ vicitramapekṣamāṇastathaiva tadracanāṃ karoti evaṃ śarīrādikāpīti । na ca śarīrotpatteḥ pūrvamasmadādyātmani buddhayādayaḥ santi, saṃskārastu smaraṇotpattāvevāvagatasāmarthya iti guṇāntaraṃ tadgatama pakṣamāṇastadupabhoganiṣpattaye vicitraṃ śarīrādikamārabhata iti । āgamastu 'yāvadātmani dharmādharmoṃ tāvadāyuḥ śarīramindriyāṇi viṣayāśceti, tathā 'kṣīyante cāsya karmāṇī'ti ।

[II,230,7]

yeṣāntu buddhiguṇo dharmasteṣāṃ kathaṃ nākarmanimittaḥ svargaḥ ? tathā hi pralayāvasthāyāṃ buddheḥ pradhāne pralīnatayā dharmādharmayoranabhivyaktī pradhānasya buddhadhādibhāvena pariṇāmo na syāt, abhivyaktasya karmaṇaḥ kāraṇatvābhyupa gamāt । na cādāvanabhivyaktameva kāraṇam, buddhisthañcābhivyaktamiti vācyam, viśeṣahetvabhāvāt । buddhayādisampāditaṃ karma karturbhogasampādakamityabhyupagame ca aviśeṣeṇa sakalapuruṣopabhogasampādakaṃ syāt, niyamahetvabhāvāt । tathā muktātmano 'pi śarīrādisampādanāya pravarteta, aviśeṣāditi saṃsāritvaprasaṅgaḥ । guṇapuruṣāntaravivekādarśanañca pradhānapravṛtterna kāraṇam, pūrvameva pratiṣedhāt ।

[II,230,15]

ye 'pi paramāṇurūpo dharma iti manyante, teṣāmapi tasya nityatāyāṃ sakalakriyāvilopaprasaṅgaḥ, maraṇādyabhāvaśca । anityatā tu paramāṇurūpatāyāṃ na sambhavatyeva, tasya paramāṇutvenotpattivināśakāraṇābhāvāt । tathā paramāṇūnāṃ dharmaśabdenābhidhāne saṃjñābhedamātrameva syāt । atha paramāṇuguṇau dharmādhau ? evamapi sarvapuruṣāṇām ekākāro bhogaḥ syāt, puṇyāpuṇyā dhikaraṇaiḥ paramāṇubhirārambhāviśeṣāt ।

[II,230,21]

atha kecit puṇyādhikaraṇāḥ paramāṇavo 'nye cāpuṇyādhikaraṇāḥ । tatrādhikaiḥ puṇyādhikaraṇairārabdhe sukhātiśayo 'dhikaiścāpuṇyādhikaraṇairduḥkhamiti cet, atrāpi tayonityatve maraṇādyabhāvaprasaṅgaḥ । anityatvantu na yuktam । paramāṇuviśeṣaguṇānāmasmadādivyāpāreṇopapatteradarśanāt ।

[II,230,25]

anye tvanāśrito dharma iti manyante, tatrāpi anityapakṣe na kiñcid anāśritaṃ bastubhūtaṃ kārya sambhavatīti dūṣaṇam । nityapakṣe tu yāgādikriyā vilopaprasaṅgaḥ । atha kriyābhivyaktaḥ kāryakāraṇaḥ ? tarhi kṣaṇikatvena kriyā<II,231>vināśe svargādiphalaṃ na syāt । na ca pradīpasyevābhivyañjakatvaṃ tatprakāśa katvaṃ kriyāyāḥ, tadbhāve 'pi tasyānupalambhāt । atha yāgādikriyā dharmasya sāmarthyamupajanayatīti cet ? tarhi yat tat sāmarthyaṃ sa eva dharmaḥ, yatrāśritaḥ sa cātmeti saṃjñābhedamātraṃ syāt । tathā amūrtasyātmanā sambandhābhāvāt tatsambandhitvena phalābhāva ityalaṃ prasaṅgena । na ca bodhātmakameva karma, vyati rekānabhyupagame bodharūpatayā sarvatrāviśeṣeṇa jagadvaicitryāprasaṅgāt ।

[II,231,6]

tasyotpattikāraṇamāha puruṣāntaḥkaraṇasaṃyogādasamavāyikāraṇādupajāyate । * śuddhābhisandhija * iti abhisandhenimittakāraṇatvaṃ darśayati । varṇāśramiṇāṃ pratiniyatāni sādhanāni nimittaṃ yasyāsau tannimittaḥ ।

[II,231,10]

tadevāha * tasya tu sādhanāni śrutismṛtivihitāni * । varṇāśca brāhmaṇādayaḥ, āśramāśca brahmacaryādayasteṣām, sāmānyaviśeṣabhāvenāvasthitāni dravyaguṇakarmāṇīti ।

[II,231,13]

(“tatra sāmānyāni dharme śraddhā, ahiṃsā, bhūtarhitatvam, satyavacanam, asteyam, anupadhā, brahmacaryam, kodhavarjanam, abhiṣecanam, śucidravyasevanam, viśiṣṭadevatābhaktiḥ, upavāso 'pramādaśca ।”)

[II,231,16]

* tatra sāmānyāni * sādhanāni । * dharme śraddhā - bhaktiviśeṣaḥ kāraṇam । ahiṃsā tu yatyādeḥ sarvadā, anyasya deśaviśeṣeṣe kālaviśeṣe ceti । yathā tīrthe na haniṣyāmi, amāvāsyādau । bhūtarhitvamapi kasyacit sarvadā, kasyacid deśaviśeṣādāviti । satyavacanaṃ dharmasādhanam yanna pareṣāmaniṣṭam । uktañca 'na brūyāt satyamapriyami'ti । asteyamacauryam । kasyāñcidavasthāyāṃ caurye 'pi na dūṣaṇamityuktam । yathā mumūrṣodvijasyāśanamātrāharaṇamiti । anupadhā parādrohaḥ । brahmacaryam apatyasṛjaḥ karaṇasyopasthasya saṃyamaḥ, tacca kasyacit sarvadā, kasyacid deśakālaviśeṣa iti । krodhavarjanamapyevam । abhiṣecanaṃ snānam । śucidravyāṇāṃ sevanamāsanaparidhānāśanaiḥ । viśiṣṭa devatābhaktiriti trayīprasiddhānumānāvagatadevatāviśeṣabhaktiḥ । upavāso 'horātraṃ nairaśanatā, kālaviśeṣādau dharmasādhanam । apramādo vihitānuṣṭhāne nirālasyam ।

<II,232>

[II,232,1]

(“brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyānāmijyādhyayanadānāni । bāhmaṇasya viśiṣṭāni pratigrahādhyāpanayājanāni, svavarṇavihitāśca saṃskārāḥ । kṣatriyasya samyakaprajāpālanamasādhunigraho yuddheṣvanivartanam, svakīyāśca saṃskārāḥ । vaiśyasya kayavikraya kṛṣipaśupālanāli svakīyāśca saṃskārāḥ । śūdrasya ; pūrvavarṇapāratantryam, amantrikāca kriyāḥ ।”)

[II,232,6]

brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ sāmānyāni dharmasādhanāni, ijyā yajanam, adhyayana vedapāṭhaḥ, dānaṃ satpātrasya dravyanivedanamiti । brāhmaṇasyāsādhāraṇāni dharma sādhanāni * pratigrahādhyāpanayājanāni । pratigrahaḥ śāstreṇāninditadravyādānam, vedapāṭho, yājanaṃ yāge paurohityam, svavarṇaniyatāśca saṃskārāḥ । kṣatriyasyā sādhāraṇāni dharmasādhanāni 5 samyak prajāpālanam, asādhunigraho yuddhaṣva nivartanam, svakīyāśca saṃskārāḥ । vaiśyasya krayavikrayakṛṣipaśupālanāni, svakīyāśca saṃskārāḥ । śūdrasya sarvadā brāhmaṇādyājñayā vartanam, amantrakāścoṅkārādivijitāḥ kriyā iti * ।

[II,232,14]

(“āśramiṇāntu, brahmacāriṇaḥ gurukulanivāsinaḥ svaśāstra vihitāni śuruśuśrūṣānondhanabhaikṣyāvaraṇāni adhumāṃsadivāsvapnāñjanā bhyañjanādivarjana ca । vidyāvatasnātakasya kṛtadārasya gahastharava śālīna yāyāvaravṛttyupajitarā bhūtabanuṣyadevapitṛnahmākhyānāṃ pañcānā mahāyajñānāṃ sāyamprātaranuṣṭhānama, ekāgnividhānena pākayajñasaṃsthānāca nityānāṃ śaktau vidyamānāyām । agnyādheyādonāca haviryajñasaṃsthānām agniṣṭomādīnāma, somayajñasaṃsthānāñca । ṛtvantareṣa brahmacaryamapatyā tpādanañca । brahmacāriṇo gahasthasya vā nāmānirgatasya vanavāsa balkalājinakeśaśmanakharokhadhāraṇañca । vanyābahatātithiśeṣabhājannāna vanasthasya । trayāṇāmanyatamasya śraddhāvataḥ sarvabhalemyo nityamabhaya daramā saṃnyastha svāni karmāṇi yamaniyameṣvapramattasya ṣaṭpadārthaprasakhyāna yogaprasādhanaṃ pravajitasyeti । iṣṭañca prayojanamanahiśyaitāni sādhana bhāvaprasādañcāpekṣayā āgamanasoḥ saṃyogāddharmotpattiriti ।”)

[II,232,27]

*āśramiṇāntu dharmasādhanānyacyante । tatrabrahmacāriṇaḥ,ki viśiṣṭatva gurukūle vasatastacchīlaṃ veti tadvāsino * guruśuśraṣāgnīndhanabhaikṣyācaraṇāni
 * । <II,233> guruśuśrūṣā tadupāsanam । agnīndhanam agnyarthamindhanāharaṇam । bhikṣāṇāṃ samūhā bhakṣa mādhukarī bhikṣā, tadācaraṇam । madhumāṃsadivāsvapnāñjanābhyañja nādivarjanam । etatta prativedaṃ dvādaśavarṣāṇītyaṣṭacatvāriṃśad varṣāṇi vidyāvataṃ yāvad grahaṇaṃ bhavet ।

[II,233,5]

tato vidyāvratasnātakasya cīrṇavidyāvratasya kṛtadārasyodvahitapatnīkasya tyasya dharmasādhanānyucyante । te caturvidhāḥ, vārtāvṛttayaḥ, śālīnavṛttayaḥ, pāvarāḥ, ghorasaṃnyāsikāśceti । tatra vārtāvṛttayaḥ kṛṣivāṇijyādikama pata śāstraṇava yañjantaḥ śatasaṃvatsarābhiḥ kriyābhiryajanto yājayanta māna prārthayante । śālīnavattayastu yajanto yājayanto dadataḥ pratigṛhṇantaḥ śatasaṃvatsarābhiḥ kriyābhirātmānaṃ prārthayante । yāyāvarāstu adhīyanto । adhyāpayantaḥ, yajanto na, 7 yājayantaḥ, dadatto na pratigṛhṇantaḥ, ityātmāna prārthayante । tatra ghorasaṃnyāsikā nāma uddhṛtaparapūtābhirabhiḥ pya kurvāṇāḥ pratidinamāhatoñchavṛttimupajīvantaḥ śatasaṃvatsarābhiḥ kriyā janta ātmānaṃ prārthayante । udāharaṇārthañca gṛhasthadvayam । ukta lāna ! śālīna | yāyāvaravṛttyupājitadravyairbhūtamanuṣyadevapitṛbrahmākhyānāṃ yā mahāyajñānāṃ sāyaṃ prātaranaṣṭhānam । sāyamaparā, - bāhyabalinā bhatayajñaḥ. hantakāreṇa 〈〉 = atithideyataṇḍulena । manaṣya ' puṣpapatrādyutsargeṇāgnisantarpaṇena devayajñaḥ । atidānena pitṛyajñaḥ, pacanana brahmayajña ityeṣāṃ sāyaṃ prātaranaṣṭhānam । ekāgnividhānena eko 'gni kāle parigṛhīta iti । naimittikānāntu parasparaṃ vyāvṛttamanuṣṭhānabhedaṃ darśayati * pākayajñasaṃsthānāma * ityādinā । pākayajñasaṃsthāstu
	aṣṭakāḥ pārvaṇaṃ śrāddhaṃ śrāvaṇyāgrahāyaṇī tathā /
	catrī cāśvayujī caiva (sapta?) pākasaṃsthā imāḥ smṛtāḥ //
yajñaḥ, puṣpapatrādyutsagaṇa vedādhyayanena brahmayajña
na doṣa iti । tadevāha ।
।

[II,233,24]

eṣāśca nityānāṃ śaktau vidyamānāyāmanuṣṭhānam । asamarthasya tvakaraṇe 'pi na dośa iti । tadevāha “jarayā ha vā eṣa etasmāt satrād vipramucyate “mṛtyunā veti” । agnyādheyānāñca haviyajñasasyātām । agnyādheyānāñca haviryajñasaṃsthānām । agnyādheyo 'gnihotraṃ sā ca cāturmāsyāgrahāyaṇeṣṭinirūḍhapaśubandhasautrāmaṇī ceti sapta<II,234>haviryajñasaṃsthāḥ । agniṣṭomo 'tyagniṣṭoma ukthyaḥ ṣoḍaśī vājapeyo 'tirā trāptoryāma iti sapta homayajñasaṃsthāḥ । tadāha “somayajñasaṃsthānāmagniṣṭomā dīnāmiti” । evamanye 'pi yajñaviśeṣāstacchāstraprasiddhā eva grāhyā iti । ṛtvantareṣu brahmacaryamapatyotpādanañca ।

[II,234,5]

vanasthasya dharmasādhanamāha * brahmacāriṇo gṛhasthasya vā vanavāsaḥ * iti । uktañca “yadi vā brahmacaryādeva pravrajet” iti । ato brahmacāriṇo gṛhasthasya vā adhikāraḥ । te 'pi caturvidhāḥ, vaikhānasāḥ, audumbarāḥ, bālakhilyāḥ, phenapāśceti । tatra vaikhānasā nāma akṛṣṭa pacyābhirauṣadhībhimabahiṣkṛtābhiragniparicaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pañcamahāyajñakriyāṃ nivartayanta ātmānaṃ prārthayante । tatraudumbarā nāma prātarutthāya yāṃ diśaṃ prekṣante tadāhṛtairbadaranīvāraśyāmākairagniparicaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pañcamahāyajñakriyāṃ nivartayanta ātmānaṃ prārthayante । tatra bālakhilyā nāma jaṭādharā cīravalkalasaṃvṛtāṅgāḥ paurṇamāsyāṃ vā kāttikyāṃ puṣyādibhakṣa mutsṛjanta aṣṭau māsān vṛttyupārjanaṃ kṛtvā pañcamahāyajñakriyāṃ nivartayanta ātmānaṃ prārthayante । tatra phenapā nāma uddaṇḍakānanmattāḥ śīrṇapatrābhibhojino yatra tatra vā vasanta ātmānaṃ prārthayante । tadevāha * valkalājinakeśaśmaśrunakha romadhāraṇaṃ vanyāmbahutātithiśeṣabhojanāni vanasthasya * iti । yatyāśramamupadarśa yannāha * trayāṇāmanyatamasya * iti । trayāṇāṃ brahmacārigṛhasthavānaprasthānāmanya tamasya । kiṃ viśiṣṭasya ? * śraddhāvataḥ । sarvabhatebhyo nityaṃ sarvadā abhayaṃ datvā । uktañca “na hisyāt sarvabhūtānīti” । * saṃnyasya svāni karmāṇi * agni hotrādīni । * yamaniyameṣvapramattasya * iti । ahiṃsādayo yamāḥ, śuśrūṣādayā niyamāḥ, teṣvapramattasya । * ṣaṭpadārthaprasaṃkhyānāt * parijñānād * yogasādhana pravajitasya * iti । yoga eva tasya dharmasādhanam ।

[II,234,24]

uktanyāyena te 'pi caturvidhāḥ; kuṭīcakāḥ, bahadakāḥ, haṃsāḥ, paramahaṃsā śceti । kuṭīcakāstridaṇḍakamaṇḍalukanthādidhāriṇo jñātigaheṣu bhojinaḥ । bahudakā nāma brāhmaṇagṛheṣu bhikṣāśinaḥ śūnyāgāradevagṛhavāsinaḥ । haṃsā nā śikhākamaṇḍaludaṇḍahastā grāmaikarātravāsinastīrthādiṣa tripañcarātram, eka pakṣopavāsādibhirātmānaṃ prārthayante । paramahaṃsāstvekadaṇḍadharāḥ, muṇḍāḥ, <II,235> kaupīnavāsasaḥ, śikhāyajñopavītakamaṇḍalabhikṣākapālādīnāñca tyāginaḥ । sapā dho nādharmaḥ, na satyama, na cānatam । sarvasahāḥ, sarvasamāḥ, lāṣṭāśmakāñcanāḥ । eṣāṃ caturṇāmapi dṛṣṭaṃ prayojanamanuddiśyaitāni vanāni bhāvaprasādaṃ śaddhābhisandhiñcāpekṣya ātmamanaḥsaṃyogādasamavāyi kāraṇāddharmotpattiriti ।

{§ adharmavaidharmyam}

[II,235,7]

(“adharmo 'pyātmaguṇaḥ । kartarahitapratyavāyaheturatīndriyo 'ntyaduḥkhasaṃvi virādhī । tasya tu sādhanāni, śāstre pratiṣiddhāni dharmasādhanaviparītāni hiṃsāntasteyādoni. vihitākaraṇama, pramādaśca, etāni duṣṭābhi pacāpekṣyātmamanasoḥ saṃyogādadharmasyo 〈tpattiḥ ? tpādakāni 〉 ।”)

[II,235,11]

na paraṃ dharmo 'dharmopyātmagaṇaḥ । * kartarahitapratyavāyaheturatīndriyo 'ntyaduḥkha sānāvarādhī * iti । atondriyatve satyantyadūḥkhasaṃvijñānavirodhitvāt, adharṃaḥ, itarasmāda bhidyate । śeṣa parvavata । tasya sādhanāni śāstre viprati "māna dharmasādhanaviparītāni hiṃsānatasteyādīni । hiṃsā prāṇivadho 'natama 1 stayaṃ cauryama । ādipadenānyeṣāmapi dharmasādhanaviparītānāmavarodhaḥ, cakattavyasya saṃdhyāvandanāderakaraṇaṃ vihitakālātikrameṇāpyananuṣṭhānama, 52cālasyam । etāni nimittāni duṣṭābhisandhi duṣṭābhiprāyaṃ cāpekṣyā manāsayogādasamavāyikāraṇādātmanyadharmo 〈tpattiriti ? tpādakānīti । 〉

[II,235,19]

(“aviduṣo rāgadveṣavataḥpravartakādadharmāt prakṛṣṭāt svalpādhasahitād prajāpatipitamanaṣyalokeṣvāśayānurūpairiṣṭaśarīrendriyaviṣayasukhā pānā bhavati । tathā prakṛṣṭādadharmāta svalpadharmasahitāta pretatiryaga nasthāneṣa aniṣṭaśarorendriyaviṣayadaḥkhādibhiryogo bhavati, ityevaṃ lakṣaṇād dharmādadharmasahitād devamanuṣyatiryanārakeṣu punaḥ punaḥ saṃsāraprabandho bhavati ।”)

[II,235,25]

(“jñānapūrvakāttu kṛtādasaṅkalpitaphalāda viśuddhe kule jātasya duḥkhavigamopāyajijñāsorācāryamupasaṅgamyotpannaṣaṭapadārthatattvajñānasyājñāna - "tā viraktasya rāgadveṣādyabhāvāta tajjayordharmādharmayoranutpattau pūrva<II,236>sañcitayoścopabhogānirodhe santoṣasukhaṃ śarīrapari〈cche? khe〉dañcotpādya rāgādinivṛttau nivṛttilakṣaṇaḥ kevalo dharmaḥ paramārthadarśana sukhaṃ kṛtvā nivartate, tadā nirodhāt nirbījasyātmanaḥ śārīrādinivṛttiḥ । punaḥ śarīrādyanutpattau dagdhendhanānalavadupaśamo mokṣa iti ।”)

[II,236,5]

idānīṃ kasyopajātaṃ karma saṃsārasampādakaṃ kathañca nivarttakamityupa darśayati aviduṣo mithyājñānavato dharmādharmāvutpannau saṃsāraṃ sampādayatastadāha pravarttakāt saṃsārasampādakād dharmāt prakṛṣṭāt svalpādharmasahitāt । iṣṭāni ca tāni śarīrendriyaviṣayasukhādīni taiḥ । kiviśiṣṭaiḥ ? āśayānurūpa karmānurūpairyogaḥ sambandho bhavatīti । keṣu sthāneṣu ? brahmendraprajāpatipitṛ 〈〉ṛṣi? manuṣyalokeṣviti । * tathā prakṛṣṭādadharmāt svalpadharmasahitāt, aniṣṭa śarīrendriyaviṣayaduḥkhādibhiryogaḥ * । keṣu ? * pretatiyaṃgayonisthāneṣu * iti । upasaṃhāramāha * ityevaṃ pravṛttilakṣaṇāt * tatsvarūpād । * dharmādadharmasahitād devamanuṣyatiryaṅnārakeṣu punaḥ punaḥ saṃsārasya prabandhaḥ santāno bhavatīti ।

[II,236,14]

pravartakāddharmāt saṃsārotpattimupadiśya nivarttakāt tannivṛttimāha * jñāna pūrvakāttu kṛtāt * iti । jñānaṃ pūrvaṃ yasya sa tathoktastasmāt । kiṃ rūpāt । *asaṅkalpitaphalāt iti । itthaṃ me śarīrendriyaviṣayāḥ sampadyantām, netthamityava na saṅkalpitaṃ phalaṃ yasya sa tathoktastasmād, viśuddhe kule janma bhavati । tasya jātasya daḥkhavigamopāyajijñāsā sampadyate kṛtaḥ sādhanādatyantaṃ duḥkha santateviyogaḥ sampadyata iti । evaṃ jijñāsorācāryopasaṅgamaḥ sampadyata । tañcopasaṅgamya duḥkhasantānavyāvṛtteruṣāyaṃ vijānāti tattvajñānācchya sampadyata iti । tataḥ śāstrābhyāsāta ṣaṭapadārthatattvajñānamatpadyate । tara cotpannaṣaṭpadārthajñānasya ajñānanivṛttirbhavati । tannivṛttau virāgaḥ, kāraṇa bhāvena kāryasyānutpatteḥ । viraktasya rāgadveṣābhāvāt tābhyāṃ jāyate yā dhana dharmoṃ tau tajjau, tayoranutpattiriti, rāgadveṣayodharmādharmajanakatvenopalabdha tadabhāve tadabhāvo bhavatyeva । sañcitayośca nirodhastattvajñānādapabhogād vā । tato rāgādinivṛttau satyāṃ nivṛttilakṣaṇaḥ kevalo dharmaḥ santoṣasukhaṃ śarāra paricche?khe〈〉daṃ cotpādayati । taccotpādya paramārthaḥ sarvapadārthānāmāranā <II,237> taddarśanājjātaṃ paramārthadarśana sakhaṃ karoti । tata kṛtvā nivarttate । tadā nigata dharmādharmasamākhyātaṃ bījaṃ yasyāsau tathoktastasyātmanaḥ śarīrādinivṛttiḥ । bījābhāvādeva punaḥ śarīrādyanatpattau satyāṃ* dagdhendhanānalavadapaśamo mākṣaḥ * iti । yathā dagdhendhanasyānalasyopaśamo jvālādirahitasyāvasthānam avadatyanta viśeṣaguṇavimuktasyātmano 'vasthānaṃ mokṣa iti nirṇītamādivākye ।

[II,237,6]

(“śabdo 'mbaraguṇaḥ, śrotragrāhyaḥ, kṣaṇikaḥ, kāryakāraṇobhayavirodhī, māgavibhāgaśabdajaḥ, pradeśavattiḥ, samānāsamānajātīyakāraṇaḥ । vidhā varṇalakṣaṇo dhvanilakṣaṇaśca । tatra akāradivarṇalakṣaṇaḥ, śaṅakhā dānāmato dhvanilakṣaṇaśca । tatra varṇalakṣaṇasyotpattiḥ, ātmamanasoḥ pagāt smṛtyapakṣāda varṇoccāraṇecchā, tadanantaraṃ prayatnaḥ, tamapekṣamāṇā samavāyusaṃyogāda vāyo karma jāyate, sa covaṃ gacchan kaṇṭhādīnabhihanti, tataḥ sthānavāyusaṃyogāpekṣāta sthānākāśasaṃyogād varṇotpattiḥ । avarṇa lakṣaṇo 'pi bherīdaṇḍasaṃyogāpekṣād bheryākāśasaṃyogātpadyate । veṇaparva māgād veṇvākāśa vibhāgācca śabdācca saṃyogavibhāganiṣpannāda cāsantānavacchanda santāna ityevaṃ santānena śrotrapradeśamāgatasya raṇam (nāsti ?). pariśeṣāta santānasiviriti ।”)

[II,237,17]

śabdasya lakṣaṇaparīkṣārthamāha * śabdo 'mbaraguṇaḥ * ityādi । ambara ugatvācchabda ityukte saṃkhyādibhirvyabhicārastadarthaṃ śrotragrāhya iti । śabdaḥ, tarasmād bhidyate, ambaraguṇatve sati śrotragrāhyatvāditi । kṣaṇika iti parokṣārtham । parvapadāpekṣaṃ vā lakṣaṇam ।

[II,237,21]

nanu cāsiddhaṃ śabde kṣaṇikatvam, pratyabhijñānāderupalambhāt । yamahamaśrauṣaṃ śabdam, tametarhi śṛṇomi iti śroturvijñānamutpadyamānamupalabdham । na cedamapramāṇam, anyatāgrāhakapramāṇānupalabdheḥ । tathā arthāpattyā ca "dasya nityatvaṃ vijñāyate । anityatve hi saṅkatakālānubhūtaśabdavilayottara pala śabdāntaropalambhādasatitā tadarthapratipattirna syāt । sā copalabhyata śata tadanyathānupapattyā śabdasya nityatvaṃ jñāyate ।

<II,238>

[II,238,1]

tadetadasat, gṛhītagrāhitvena pratyabhijñānasyāpramāṇatvāt; “anadhiga tārthagantṛ pramāṇam” iti sāmānyalakṣaṇābhidhānāt । athānadhigatārthe pratya bhijñānam ? tanna, adṛṣṭārthatāyā mithyātvaprasaṅgāt । atha svarūpeṇādhi gatārthamapīdānīntanaṃ deśakālādyapekṣayānadhigatārthañceti ।

[II,238,5]

nanvevamapyubhayadoṣopanipātaprasaṅgaḥ । prameyasāmagryāñca deśakālāderanta rbhāvābhyupagame 'nadhimatārthatvam, etāvatā prameyasya pūrvamapratipatteḥ । na ca śrotravyāpāreṇa deśakālādebrahaṇaṃ dṛṣṭam । atha pramāṇasāmagryāmantarbhāvaḥ, tarhi pramāṇasyānyatve 'pi prameyasya tādavasthyādadhigatārthaviṣayatvameva । tadapekṣayā caṃda viśeṣaṇam, anyathā hi vyavacchedyābhāvādanupapannameva syāt, pramāṇasāmagryā niyatavijñānajanakatvāt । sarvatra prameyabhedādeva vijñānabheda ityabhyupagama pratijñānamanyatāyāṃ kṣaṇikatāprasaṅgaḥ । tasmādanadhigatārthagantṛ pramāṇamityava vādino pramāṇameva pratyabhijñānam । tathā chinnodbhūtakeśanakhādiṣvanyatve 'pi sādṛśyavaśāt pratyabhijñānam । sāmānyādau cārthatathābhāvāditi dvavidhyā palabdheviśeṣānupalabdhau śabde pratyabhijñānam । na ca vyañjakānāṃ sandigdha tvādapramāṇatvam, svataḥ prāmāṇyasya pūrvameva pratiṣedhāt; anyataḥ pramāṇāda abhedapratipattyabhyupagame ca tadevāstvalaṃ pratyabhijñānena । tathā vyañjakānā kṣaṇikatayā śabdajñānānantarameva tirobhāve śabdasya, niviṣayameva syāt pratyabhijñānam । na ca vyañjakānāṃ nityatvam, sarvadā śabdavyaktiprasaṅgāt ।

[II,238,19]

atha pratyabhijñānānyathānupapattyā tatkālaṃ yāvadavasthānam ? na, anyathāpi tadbhāvāt । anityatve 'pi sādṛśyavaśāt pratyabhijñānamutpadyata eveti । vivādagocarāpannaḥ śabdo 'bhivyaktaḥ pratyabhijñānakālaṃ yāvannāvatiṣṭhata, śabdapratyayaviṣayatvāt, pūrvānubhūtaśabdavat । na ca pratyabhijñānaṃ nityatvāta pādanāyālam, anitye 'pi bhāvāt ।

[II,238,24]

athāvasthāyitvaṃ sādhyate ? tatrāpi santatāvasthāne tadeva dūṣaṇam . avasthānamātrantu siddhasādhanam, upalambhasaṅketasmaraṇakrameṇārthopalambhakā yāvadavasthānābhyupagamāt । atha pūrvopalabdhe śabde varṣādivyavadhānamā pratyabhijñānād antarāle 'vasthānaṃ sādhyate ? na. anyatve 'pi pratyabhijñānopa<II,239>labdhaḥ । yathā bālāvasthāyāmupalabdhe devadatte anyatve 'pi vṛddhāvasthāyāmupa lambhāt pratyabhijñānam । na cātrāvasthābhedamātrameva śarīrasyeti vācyam, avayavaracanāparimāṇarūpādivyatirekeṇa tadanupalambhāt । bālāvasthāyāṃ hi śithilāvayavaracanā kumārāvasthāyāṃ cānyathābhūteti tadbhedāt śarīrasya bhado 'vaśyaṃ bhāvī, asamavāyikaraṇavināśena kāryadra vyasya vināśopalabdheḥ, parimāṇabhedopalabdheśca । pūrvaparimāṇanivṛttāvevottaraparimāṇam, parimāṇavati parimāṇārambhapratiṣedhāt । etad rupādiṣvapi samānam । parimāṇavināśaścā śrayavināśādeva ityanyatvameva । bālādiśarīrāṇāṃ parimāṇabhedasya kuvalayādā vanyatvenaiva vyāptatvāt । atha parasparaṃ vyāvṛtto bālādyavasthāśabdābhidheyo dhamaḥ, tasya ca vyatireke vṛddhāvasthāyāmapi bālādīnāmupalambhaḥ syāt, tenā virodhāt, virodhe vā kathamanyatvamasiddham; avyatireke 'pi teṣāmāvirbhāva tirobhāvābhyāṃ dharmiṇo 'pi tathābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ । tasmāccharīrabhede 'pi sādṛśyāt sa evāyaṃ devadatta iti jñānavacchabde 'pi pratyabhijñānaṃ bhaviṣyatīti śabdo palambhādanantaraṃ śrotravyāpāreṇaiva tadabhāvapratīterekatvagrāhakaṃ pratyabhijñānama pramāṇam ।

[II,239,16]

karṇaśaṣkulyabhyupagame 'pi kvacicchabdasyābhivyaktau tasya vyāpakatayā sarvadeśāvasthitapuruṣāṇāmupalambhaḥ syāt, nirāvaraṇasya vyāpakatvāviśeṣāt । tathaikadeśāstasyābhivyajyante teṣāmabhede śabdasyaivābhivyaktiriti tadeva dūṣaṇam । bhede tu tadabhivyaktau kathaṃ śabdo 'rthamabhidadhyāt । yadi ca śabdaviśeṣaṇaśca śabdābhāvaḥ paricchidyate, viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvalakṣaṇenaiva sambandhenetyuktaṃ pūrvam ।

[II,239,22]

atha śabdasyopalambhānantara〈〉mu?manupalabdhirmyañjakābhāvād nāsattvā diti cet, na, sadbhāve pramāṇābhāvād āvaraṇāderanupalambhācca । nahi aindriya kasyātīndriyamāvaraṇaṃ pramāṇena kvacidapalabdham । abhyupagame 'pi kvaci cchabdasyābhivyaktī tasya vyāpakatayā sarvadeśāvasthitapuruṣāṇāmupalambhaḥ syāt, nirāvaraṇasya vyāpakatvāviśeṣāt । yadi ca śabdātmakāniyatārthapratipāda kāścaikadeśāḥ ? saṃjñābhedamātrameva ।

<II,240>

[II,240,1]

atha bherīdaṇḍasaṃyogād vegāpekṣādutpannakriyo vāyurvegavāṃśchrotradeśenāga tyābhisambadhyate, tadgatāni tu stimitavāyvantarāṇi protsārayati, tataḥ pratibandhakābhāve sati śrotraṃ śabdasya grāhakamiti ? nanvevamapi aśeṣaśabdopa lambhaprasaṅgaḥ, saṃskṛte hi śrotra sarveṣāṃ sānnidhyam । na ca gośabdābhivyaktyartha prerito vāyu śvaśabdaṃ vyanaktīti vācyam, vyañjakeṣu niyamānupalabdhaḥ । yathā ghaṭābhivyaktyarthamutpāditaḥ pradīpaḥ samānendriyagrāhyasamānadeśāvasthita padārthābhivyañjaka iti । tathā hi na śrotraṃ pratiniyatasaṃskārakasaṃskāryam, samā nendriyagnāhyasamānadeśāvasthitavastuprakāśakatvāt, cakṣurvat । pradīpāvaṣṭabdha deśavyatirekatājñānaṃ pradīpasaṃskṛtaṃ na cakṣuṣā grahaṇamiti samānadeśāvasthita padam । evaṃvidhāśca rūparasādayo na gṛhyanta iti samānendriyagrāhyagrahaṇam । śabdā vā vivādaviṣayāḥ pratiniyatavyañjakavyaṅgyā na bhavanti, samānendriya grāhyasamānadeśāvasthitatvāt, ghaṭādivat । atra ca ye pratiniyatasaṃskāraka saṃskāryā na bhavanti cakṣaghaṃṭādayaste sapakṣāstatra hetoḥ sadbhāvaḥ । tadvipa rītāstu vipakṣāstasmādatyantaṃ vyāvṛttiriti । pradīpena ca saṃskṛtaṃ cakṣuryugapad ghaṭādiprakāśakamiti dṛṣṭam । evaṃ śrotramapyaśeṣaśabdopalambhakaṃ syāt । atra cāpekṣābuddhivadanekapadārthālambanamevaikaṃ jñānamāśubhāvena vā yugapacchabdaprayoga iti । nanvekasyāmapi pṛthivyāṃ śuklādibhedānāṃ saṃskṛtenāpi cakṣuṣā na yugapat prakāśanam, evaṃ ghrāṇādinā gandhāderiti । evamapi na hetoyvyabhicāraḥ, sapakṣakadeśavṛtterapi gamakatvāt ।

[II,240,20]

atha yathā cakṣuḥ samānendriyagrāhyasamānadeśāvasthitānāmapi śuklādi bhedānāṃ na yugapat prakāśakamevaṃ śrotramapi syāt । iṣṭañca pṛthivyāmanaka rūpādhikaraṇatvamapi citrarūpasamarthanāvasare । satyametata; tathāpi rūpabhedānā magrahaṇaṃ sahakāryabhāvāt । tathā ca nānārūpāvayavopalambhasahakārīndriyamavaya vinyanekarūpagrāhakamityuktam । tatsadbhāve vicitrapratibhāsanāt । na para śrotrasya vāyunā saṃskṛtasya sarvaśabdānāṃ tatra sānnidhyādagrahaṇe kāraṇamastīti । sāmānyāni tu pratiniyatavyañjakavyaṅgyāni, na tu samānadeśāni svāvadha sarvagatatvādeveti vyabhicārābhāvaḥ । tathā ātapasampattaiile gandhābhivyaktiḥ, <II,241> grīṣmāvasāne tu dagdhasthalīṣu prathamajaladharadhārāsamparkāt, na ca samānadeśatvam । yad vā jaladharadhārāsamparkād bhūgatānilodbhave satyavayavakriyākrameṇa pravadravyanivṛttāvutpannapākaidvaryaṇukādiprakrameṇa dravyāntarotpāde sati gandho 'bhi vyajyata iti । yaccābhivyajyate sāmānyarūpādi, tad āśrayasthameveti dṛṣṭam, eka śabde 'pi syāt । tattu nāstīti vyakti dharmakatvābhāvaḥ ।

[II,241,6]

tathā vīṇāśabdābhivyañjakena rāsabhaśabdasyāpyabhivyaktatvād grahaṇe vīṇā śabdasya sarvadānupalambha eva syāt । na caitadasti । kvacideva rāsabhaśabdena vāṇāśabdādiśabdānāmabhibhavopalabdheḥ । na cāyaṃ nityapakṣe abhibhāvyābhi mavikabhāvo ghaṭate, tīvratarādibhedāsambhavāt । tīvrasya ca dhvanegrahaṇānmanda tyāgrahaṇamabhibhavaḥ । na ca tīvraṇa vyañjakenaikasya grahaṇādanyasyāgrahaṇamupapadyate, pajakeṣu niyamānupalabdherityuktam । śabdapratyayasamānādhikaraṇaścāyaṃ tīvraḥ śabdo mandaḥ śabda iti pratyayaḥ, na vyañjakapratyayeneti kathaṃ tīvratarādi yajakadharmaḥ । tadevaṃ tībrādibhedabhinnatvāt sukhādivadanityatvaṃ śabdānām । 1jakānupalabdhau cābhūtvā bhavanasyopalabdheḥ kāryatvādanityatvaṃ ghaṭādivat । tathā paramātmaguṇānyatve sati vyāpakaviśeṣaguṇatvāt sukhādivat । taccokta mākāśādhikāre । anityaviśeṣagaṇamākāśama, salilādiparamāṇuvyatireke sati bhūtatvāt kṣityādivat । pārimāṇḍalyādhāraparatvānumeyaparamātmānyatve sati samavāyikāraṇatvāta kṣityādivadeva ।

[II,241,19]

atha guṇatve śabdasyānumānam; na dravyakarmajātīyaḥ śabdaḥ, śrotragrahaṇa gyatvāt, śabdatvādivat । guṇaḥ, śabdaḥ, dravyakarmānyatve sati sattāsambandhi pāt, rūpādivat । yaccedam arthapratipattyanyathānupapattyā śabdānāṃ nityatvaṃ vajñāyata ityuktam, tadasat, anityatve 'pi sādṛśyopādāne satyarthapratipatte bhāvāt । yatra yatra gakāraukāravisarjanīyānāmitthambhūtānupūrvīmupalabhase, tatra * gotvaviśiṣṭo 'rthaḥ pratipattavyaḥ, pratipādayitavyaśceti saṅketagrahe sati pāvidhaṃ śabdamupalabhamānastamarthaṃ pratipadyate pratipādayati ceti ।

[II,241,26]

tadevamanityatve vyavasthite vināśakāraṇamāha kāryakāraṇobhayavirodhīti । ādyaḥ śabdaḥ kāryeṇa virudhyate । antyastu kāraṇaṃ viruṇaddhi । madhyamatāstu yaṇa virudhyante. kāraṇañca virudhantīti ।

<II,242>

[II,242,1]

saṃyogavibhāgaśabdaja ityutpattikāraṇam । “saṃyogād vibhāgācchabdācca śabdaniṣpattiḥ” iti <= vai. sū0> ।

[II,242,3]

sa dvividhaḥ । kena rūpeṇa ? varṇalakṣaṇo 'varṇalakṣaṇaśceti । akārā dihakāraparyanto varṇalakṣaṇaḥ । śaṅkhādinimittaṃ yasyāsau tannimitto 'vaṇa lakṣaṇa iti । ādipadenānyeṣāmapi nimittakāraṇānāmavarodhaḥ ।

[II,242,6]

tatra varṇalakṣaṇasyotpattirabhidhīyate । ātmamanasoḥ saṃyogādasama vāyikāraṇāt smṛtyapekṣādvarṇoccāraṇecchā bhavati । tadanantaraṃ prayatnaḥ । tamapekṣamāṇād ātmavāyusaṃyogādasamavāyikāraṇād vāyau samavāyikāraṇa karma । sa cotpannakarmā vāyurūvaṃ gacchan kaṇṭhādīnabhihantīti । ādipadā tālvoṣṭhādergrahaṇam । tataḥ sthānavāyusaṃyogāpekṣāt sthānākāśasaṃyogāhaṇā tpattiriti । ākāśaṃ samavāyikāraṇaṃ sthānākāśasaṃyogo 'samavāyikāraṇa sthānavāyusaṃyogaścāpekṣākāraṇamiti ।

[II,242,13]

avarṇalakṣaṇo 'pi bheryākāśasaṃyogādutpadyate । bherīdaṇḍasaṃyogāya pekṣād ityādipadena dikkālādegrahaṇam । atrāpyākāśaṃ samavāyikāraṇam । bheryākāśasaṃyogo 'samavāyikāraṇaṃ bherīdaṇḍasaṃyogādinimittakāraṇamiti. tathā veṇuparvavibhāgāpekṣāt parvākāśavibhāgādasamavāyikāraṇādākāra śabdo niṣpadyata iti ।

[II,242,18]

śabdajaṃ śabdamupadarśayati । evaṃ saṃyogāda vibhāgācca pariniṣpanna śabdaḥ samantāt śabdāntarāṇyārabhate । tasmādapyasamavāyikāraṇāt svakāra pratyāsatyapekṣādākāśe 'nyaḥ śabda iti vīcīsantānavacchabdasantāna yathā hi mahataḥ pāṣāṇādyabhighātādūpajātā vīcī vīcyantaramārabhate, sāpi punarvīcyantaramiti santānāstadvacchabdasantāna ityevaṃ santānanyāyena śrotra deśamāgatasya grahaṇam ।

[II,242,24]

etacca kalpyate; anyathā karṇaśaṣkalyā
kāśasaṃyogopalakṣitanabhaḥ pradeśavyatirekeṇa pradeśāntarasamavāyātteṣāmavyāpyavattitvena viśiṣṭapratyāsatterabhāvādagrahaṇameva syāt । tadāha śrotraśabdayorgamanāsambhavāt santānānabhyupagame na parasparaṃ prāptiḥ । prāptasya copalambha iti santānaḥ kalpyate ।

<II,243>

[II,243,1]

nanvetasmin pakṣe śabdāḥ svāvaruddhanabhodeśa eva yadi śabdāntaramāra bharan, na kasyāpyupalambhaḥ syāta, sarveṣāmekatraivopakṣayāt । atha pradeśāntare, tāha brahmabhāṣitasyāpyupalambho 'smadādiśrotradeśe śabdāntarārambhāt ।

[II,243,4]

athāṇuvivaramātre svadeśānantaramārabhate । tarhi teṣāṃ kṣaṇaśatādi yavadhānena grahaṇaṃ syāt । tattu na dṛṣṭaṃ kṣaṇadvayādivyavadhānena śravaṇāt । yā ādyaḥ śabdaḥ śabdāntaraṃ nārabhate, śabdatvādantyaśabdavat । antyaśabdo pā śabdāntaramārabhate śabdatvādādyaśabdavat । ataḥ santānapratiṣedhe śabdopa sambhānyathānupapattyā vāyorvyañjakasyāgamanaṃ kalpyata ini manyante ।

[II,243,9]

na caitadyuktam । vyaktipakṣasya pūrvameva pratiṣedhādvāyārāgamane pramā māvācca । na ca śabdopalabdhi reva pramāṇam, santānanyāyenāpi tadupapattaḥ । paścātra dūṣaṇamupanyastaṃ tadvīcīnidarśanopanyāsānnirastam । yathā hi mahataḥ pāṣāṇābhighātādapajātā vīcī svadeśānantaradeśa eva vīcyantaramārabhate, na dādāvevaṃ śabdo 'pi svakāraṇapratyāsattimapekṣyānantaradeśa eva śabdāntara bhārabhata iti । na ca kṣaṇaśatādivyavadhānena grahaṇaprasaṅgaḥ, ṣaṇṇāmeva śabdānāṃ tībrādibhedānāmutpatteḥ । tathā hi bherīdaṇḍābhighātādupajāte śabde sānnihitasya tīvratamaḥ śabda iti jñānam, tadanantaraṃ vyavahitasya ca tīvataraḥ śabda iti jñānam, tatastīvo mando mandataro mandatamaśceti ṣaḍbhedāḥ maṇānubhūyanta iti na ānantyapakṣokto doṣaḥ । tathā hi bherīdaṇḍābhiṣā pādaka eva śabdaḥ kalpitaṃ bhūyāṃsaṃ pradeśa vyāpyopajāyata ityanekairapyu palabhyata vāta na sarvatra santānaḥ । yaccedamuktam-~-nādyaḥ śabdaḥ śabdāntaramārabhate śabdatvādantyaśabdavad iti, tanna svatantrasādhanam, svayamādyantaśabdāprasiddhaḥ । na ca dṛṣṭāntadāāntikarmiṇoraprasiddhau hetoḥ pakṣadharmatvaṃ bahirvyāptirvā sambhavatīti । atha paravyāptyā parasyāniṣṭāpādanametat । tanna । yadi pramāṇa pāvakā paravyāptistayaiva vādhyamānatvād viparītānumānasyānutthānam । jayāpramāṇapūrvikā ? tarhi prameyāprasiddharāśrayāsiddhaṃ sādhanam, dhāsiddhaśca dṛṣṭānta iti, śabdasya śabdāntarārambhapratiṣedhe svayamādyantaviśeṣaṇāprasiddhaḥ । tasmād vyaktipakṣapratiṣedhe śabdopalambhānyathānupapattyā santānakalpanā <II,244> kriyata iti । na cāntyaśabdasyārambhakatvaparikalpanāyāṃ pramāṇamasti, sarvadopalambhaprasaṅagāt । ato 'ntyaśabdasya sparśavadadravyasaṃyogaikārthasamavāyena pralayaḥ svajñānādupabhogaprāpakādṛṣṭāpakṣayād veti vināśasya pramāṇenopalabdhaḥ, tasya ca nirhetukatvapratiṣedhāduktakāraṇādeva vināśaḥ kalpyata ityalam ।

<॥ iti śrīvyomaśivācāryaviracitāyāṃ padārthadharmasaṅgrahaṭīkāyāṃ vyomavatyā guṇapadārthaḥ>

{§§ karmasādharmyanirūpaṇam}

[II,244,8]

(“utkṣepaṇādīnāṃ pañcānāmapi karmatvasambandhaḥ । ekadravyavasva kṣaṇikatvaṃ bhūtadravyatitvam aguṇavattvaṃ gurutvadvatvaprayatnasaṃyogajasva svakāryasaṃyogavirodhitvaṃ saṃyogavibhāganirapekṣakāraṇatvam asamavāya kāraṇatvam svaparāśrayasamavetakāryārambhakatvaṃ samānajātīyānārambhakatva dravyānārambhakatvañca pratiniyatajātiyogitvama । digaviśiṣṭakāryārambha katvañca viśeṣaḥ ।”)

[II,244,14]

idānomitarapadārthavaidhapeṇa svabhedavyāpakamutkṣepaṇādīnāṃ sādhamyaṃ tathā parasparavyāvṛttaṃ vaidhayaṃ kāraṇañca nirūpayannāha utkṣepaṇādīnām iti । na paraṃ dvayostrayāṇāñca । ki tarhi ? pañcānāmapi karmatvasambandhaḥ, kamatvā palakṣitaḥ samavāyaḥ । tathā cotkṣepaṇādīni, itarasmād bhiyanta, karmāṇoti vā vyavahartavyāni, karmatvābhisambandhāditi । ekadravyavatva miti । ekañca tad dravyañcetyekadravyam, tadasyāstīti ekadravyavāda । tasya bhāva ekadravyavatvam । ekaṃ karmakasminneva dravye vartata, tara mevaikasminniti । kūta etata ? ekasmiścalite sarveṣāṃ calanānupalabdhaḥ । yatrāpi bahanāmekakālaṃ calanaṃ tatrāpyanekatvameva. kāraṇasyābhidhātā pratyāśrayaṃ bhedāt । anyatra ca samavetamabhighātādi anyatra samacāra kāraṇamityabhyupagame cāśeṣadravyāśritasyotpattiḥ, aviśeṣāt । tathakāna dravye saṃyogād vinaṣṭe karmaṇi āśrayāntare 'pi tasyaikatāyāṃ vināśaḥ syāta ekasmiścānekakarmābhyupagame viruddhadigabhimukhatāyāṃ parasparaṃ prativara agamanameva syāt । ekadigabhimukhatāyāñca ekenaiva karmaṇā saṃyoga<II,245>vibhāgayorjanitatvāt na dvitīyasya sadbhāve pramāṇamasti । taduttara sayogācca prāktanakarmavināśaḥ karmāntarotpattiśca kvacidiṣyata eva । tasmādyatra karmadvayapratibhāsastatra āśubhāvitvenaiveti draṣṭavyam । athaika dravyavattvaṃ rūpāderapīti kṣaṇikagrahaṇam; tathāpi buddhayādibhirvyabhicāra parihārārthaṃ mūrtadravyavṛttitvapadam ।

[II,245,6]

atha kṣaṇikatve sati mūrtadravyeṣveva vartamānatvāt karmetyukte vyabhi cārābhāvaḥ ? satyam, tathāpi padāntaraṃ sādharmyamātrapratipādanārtham, parīkṣārthañceti । gurutva dravatva prayatnasaṃyogebhyo jāyata iti gurutva 〈〉dravatva prayatnasaṃyogajam tasya bhāvastattvamiti । udāharaṇañcaitat, anyasmādapi kāraṇāt tadutpatteḥ । vyastañca gurutvādikaṃ kāyantira sampādakamapi na samaditaṃ karmavyatirekeṇānyasya ityasādhāraṇameva । nacaivaṃ sakalakarmabhedavyāpakamiti vaidharnāmātrameva । yad vā gurutvādyanyatama kāraṇajanyatvaṃ vivakṣitama । tathā svakāryasaṃyogavirodhitvamiti । saṃyoga mātreṇa vināśādarśanāditi svakāryagrahaṇam । karmakāryatvañca vibhāgavega yorapīti tatra vyabhicāravāraṇāya saṃyogagrahaṇam । ataḥ svakāryasaṃyoga virādhitvamasādhāraṇamapi kvacidāśrayavināśenāpi vināśānna pakṣavyāpaka miti vaidharmyamātrameva । tathā vibhāge saṃyoge 'pi ca kartavye nirapekṣa kāraṇatvaṃ karmaṇaḥ svarūpam ।

[II,245,19]

nanu vibhāge 'napekṣakāraṇatvamiṣṭam, saṃyoge tu paścābhāvinaṃ prāktana sayogavināśamapekṣata ityanapekṣatvamasiddham ? vastubhūtakāraṇāpekṣayā tadupapatteḥ । abhāvavyatirekeṇa ca vastubhūtaṃ kāraṇaṃ nāpekṣata ityanapekṣa mityuktam । na cānyasyaitat sambhavatītyasādhāraṇam ।

[II,245,23]

asamavāyikāraṇatvamiti asādhāraṇamitarasmād vyāvṛttam । guṇānāṃ hi vaividhyam asamavāyitvaṃ nimittatvañca । utkṣepaṇādīnāṃ cāsamavāyi kāraṇatvameva na dvaividhyamastīti vipakṣādatyantaṃ vyāvṛttireva, dvaividhya jātapaṃdhasya vivakṣitatvāta । tathā svaparāśrayasamavetakāryārambhakatvam । yāsmannāśraye samavetaṃ karma, tatra āśrayāntare ca samavetaṃ vibhāgaṃ saṃyogaṃ <II,246> cārabhata iti । samānajātīyānārambhakatvam । tathā cotpannaṃ karma vibhāgaṃ saṃyogaṃ cārabhamāṇamupalabdhaṃ na karmāntaramiti । ekasmim dharmiṇya nekasya karmaṇaḥ pūrvameva pratiṣedhāt । dravyānārambhakatvam । na karma dravyamā rabhate, tasyottarasaṃyogena vinaśyadavasthasya kāraṇatvāsambhavāditi svabhedavyāpakaṃ sādharmyam । pratiniyatajātiyogitvamiti । pratiniyatajāti rutkṣepaṇatvādikā, tadyogitvaṃ pañcānāmapi । diviśiṣṭakāryārambhakatvañca viśeṣaḥ 〈parasparamiti ?〉 ।

[II,246,8]

(“tatrokṣepaṇaṃ śarīrāvayaveṣu tatsambaddheṣu ca yaduprabhāgbhiḥ pradeśaḥ saṃyogakāraṇamadhobhāgbhiśca pradeśaḥ vibhāgakāraṇaṃ karmotpadyate gurutva prayatnasaṃyogebhyastadutkṣepaṇam ।
	tadviparotasaṃyogavibhāgakāraṇaṃ karmāpakṣepaṇam /”)

[II,246,12]

(“ṛjuno dravyasyānāvayavānāṃ taddeśaivibhāgaḥ saṃyogaśca mūlapradeśaḥ, yena karmaṇāvayavī kuṭilaḥ saṃjāyate, tadākuñcanam ।”)

[II,246,14]

(“tadviparyayeṇa saṃyogavibhāgotpatto yena karmaṇāvayavī ṛjuḥ sampadyate, tatprasāraṇam ।
	yadaniyatadipradeśasaṃyogavibhāgakāraṇaṃ tad gamanamiti //”)

[II,246,17]

tadevāha tatrotkṣepaṇam । yadūrdhvaṃ bhajanta ityūrvabhājastaiḥ saṃyoga kāraṇam, adhābhābhiśca vibhāgakāraṇaṃ karmotpadyate । kebhyaḥ keṣu ceti ? gurutvadvatvaprayatnasaṃyogebhyaḥ samastavyastebhyaḥ । tadutkṣepaṇamityudāharaṇārtham, vegāderapi tat kāraṇatvāt । śarīrāvayaveṣu hastapādādiṣu tatsambaddheṣu musalādiṣvityāśrayanirūpaṇam ।

[II,246,22]

tadviparītasaṃyogavibhāgakāraṇaṃ karmāpakṣepaṇamiti । ūrdhvabhābhivibhāga kāraṇamadhobhāgbhiśca saṃyogakāraṇamiti ।

[II,246,24]

ākuñcanam ṛjuno dravyasya ye 'yāvayavāsteṣāṃ taddeśastadupalakṣitākāśā dipradeśaivibhāgaḥ, saṃyogaśca mūlapradeśairiti tadupalakṣitākāśādipradeśaireva ।

<II,247>

[II,247,1]

yena karmaṇā samutpannenāvayavī kuṭilaḥ san nṛjuḥ sampadyate, tat prasā raṇamiti ।

[II,247,3]

yadaniyatadigdeśasaṃyogavibhāgakāraṇaṃ tad gamanamiti । uktapradeśebhyo 'nye 'niyatadikapradeśāstaiḥ saṃyogavibhāgakāraṇamiti ।

[II,247,5]

(“etat pañcavidhamapi karma śarīrāvayaveṣu tatsambaddheṣu ca satpratya yam asatpratyayaśca । yadanyat tadapratyayameva, teṣu anyeṣu ca tadgamanamiti ।”)

[II,247,7]

upasaṃhāramāha ityetat pañcavidhamapi karma satpratyayam asatpratyayañceti । pratyayaḥ kāraṇam, tacca sāmānyapadenāpi saditi viśeṣaṇāt prayatnākhyameva vivakṣitam । pāramparyeṇa vā pratyayakāryatvāt prayatnaḥ pratyaya ityuktaḥ । ataḥ satpratyayo yasya tattathoktaṃ karma, prayatnapūrvakamiti yāvat । asatpratyayamayatna pūrvakam । tacca śarīrāvayaveṣu tatsambaddheṣu bhavatīti । etasmād yadanyat, tadapratyayamayatnapūrvakam, asmadādiprayatnasya tatrāvyāpārāt । taccaiteṣvanyeṣu ca dravyeṣu bhavatyutkṣepaṇādivilakṣaṇatvād gamanameveti ।

[II,247,14]

(“karmaṇāṃ jātipañcakatvamayuktam, gamanāviśeṣāt । sarvaṃ hi kṣaṇika karma gamanamātram utpannaṃ svāśrayasyordhvamastiryag vāpi aṇumātraiḥ pradeśaiḥ saṃyogavibhāgān karoti, sarvatra gamanapratyayo 'viśiṣṭastasmād gamanameva sarvamiti । na, vargaśaḥ pratyayānuvṛttivyāvṛttidarśanāt । iho tkṣepaṇaṃ paratrāpakṣepaṇamityevamādi sarvatra vargaśaḥ pratyayānuvṛttivyāvṛttī daṣṭe, taddhetuḥ sāmānyaviśeṣabhedo 'vagamyate । teṣāmudādyupasargaviśeṣāt pratiniyatadiviśiṣṭakāryārambhatvādupalakṣaṇabhedo 'pi siddhaḥ ।”)

[II,247,21]

karmaṇāṃ jātipañcatvamayuktam । kutaḥ ? gamanāviśeṣāt । gamanādabhedā dityākṣepaḥ । tadevāha sarva kṣaṇikam । kṣaṇikatvaṃ nāma sarvakarmasu samāna miti na svarūpabhedād bhedaḥ । calanamātramutpannaṃ svāśrayasya saṃyogavibhāgān karoti । kaiḥ saha ? ūrdhvamadhastiryakaparamāṇuvivaramātraiḥ pradeśairiti । yāvati pradeśe paramāṇoraṇapraveśaḥ sambhavatīti, na kāryabhedādapi bhedaḥ, sarvasyāpyetatkāryajanakatvāt । tathā sarvatra ca gamanapratyayo 'viśiṣṭa iti । ūrdhvaṃ gacchatyagrapradeśācca 〈mūla〉 pradeśaṃ gacchati mūlapradeśāccāgrapradeśaṃ <II,248> gacchatoti । tasmād gamanameva sarvamityupasaṃhāraḥ । na, vargaśaḥ pratyayānu vṛttivyāvṛttidarśanāditi pratisamādhānavākyam । yaduktaṃ sarvaṃ gamana miti, etanna, utkṣepaṇādivargeṣu pratyayānuvṛttivyāvṛttidarśanāt । tadevāha ihotkṣepaṇam, paratrāpakṣepaṇamityevamādi sarvatra vargaśa iti varge varge pratyayā nuvṛttiāvṛttiśca dṛṣṭā । tathā hi utkṣepaṇamutkṣepaṇamityutkṣepaṇavarge 'nuvartate, apakṣapaṇādivargācca vyāvarttate । tathā apakṣepaṇaṃ svavarge 'nuvartate bhedāntarācca, vyāvatteta iti । taddhatuḥ anugatavyāvṛttajñānahetuḥ utkṣepaṇatvādisāmānya viśeṣo 'vagamyata iti । na gamanatvamekameva sāmānyam, utkṣepaṇādibhedānāṃ parasparavyāvṛttajātisambandhināṃ sadbhāvāt । udādhupasargaviśeṣātteṣāṃ parasparaviśeṣaḥ । tathā hi utpūrva kṣepaṇamutkṣepaṇam, apapūrvam apakṣepaṇam, āt pūrva kuñcanam ākuñcanam, prapūrvaṃ sāraṇaṃ prasāraṇam, gamanaṃ tūpasargābhā vādeva viśiṣyate । pratiniyatadigaviśiṣṭakāryārambhatvād upalakṣaṇabhedo 'pyu rakṣepaṇādīnāṃ siddha iti । tathā covaṃ saṃyogakāraṇamadhaśca vibhāgakāraṇa mutkṣepaṇasyopalakṣaṇamityevamāyuktam । upalakṣaṇasya cotkṣepaṇatvāderbheda iti ।

[II,248,15]

(“evamapi pañcaivetyavadhāraṇānupapattiḥ । nikaṣaṇaśamāliyara vargaśaḥ pratyayānuvṛttivyāvṛttidarśanāt । yāropaṇādidhu sarvatra vargaśaḥ pratyayānuvattidhyāvattidarśanājjātibheda iyate, evaśva nilamaṇa praveśanādiṣvapi । kāryabhedāt leṣu pratyayānuvṛttiāvṛttī iti cet, na, utkṣepaṇādiṣvaṣi kāryabhedādeva satyayānuvṛttivyāvṛtti. prasaṅgaḥ । atha samāne vargaśaḥ pratyayānukṛttivyāvṛtti sajhāḍe lakṣe paṇādīnāmeva jātibhedo na nikramaṇāhīnābhityanna viśeṣaheturastīti । na, jātisaṅkaraprasaṅgāt । niṣkramaṇādīnāṃ jātibhedāt pratyayānuvṛtti vyāvṛttau jātisaṅkaraḥ prasajyate । katham ? yoṣṭrorekaramāyabara kāda pavarakāntaraṃ gacchato yugapanniṣkramaṇapraveśalapratyāyo iṣṭau, tathā dvārapradeśa praviśati niṣkāmatīti ca । yadā tu pratitorāapanīlaṃ bhavati, tadā na praveśanapratyayo nāpi niṣkramaṇapratyayaḥ; kintu gamana pratya eva bhavati । tathā nālikāyāṃ vaṃśapatrādau patati bahūnāṃ draṣṭaṇāṃ yugapad bhramāṇapatana<II,249>praveśanapratyayā dṛṣṭā iti jātisaṅkaraprasaṅgaḥ । na caivamutkṣepaṇādiṣu pratyayasakaro dṛṣṭaḥ । tasmādutkṣepaṇādīnāmeva jātibhedāt pratyayānu vṛttivyāvṛttī, niṣkramaṇādīnāntu kāryabhedāditi ।”)

[II,249,4]

evamapi pañcaivetyavadhāraṇānupapattiḥ, utkṣepaṇādibhyo 'tiricyamāneṣu niṣkramaṇaṃ praveśanamityādiṣu vargaśaḥ pratyayānuvṛttivyāvṛttidarśanāt । sāmānyaviśeṣasadbhāve sati karmaṇām ānantyamaniṣṭamanuṣajyate । atha kārya bhedānniṣkramaṇādiṣu pratyayānuvṛttisadbhāvo na, sāmānyaviśaṣesadbhāvāditi parāśayamāśaṅkyāha utkṣepaṇādiṣvapi kāryabhedādeva pratyayānuvṛttivyāva tiprasaṅga iti ।

[II,249,10]

yathā bahirdeśena saṃyogakaraṇādantardeśena ca vibhāgajananāt niṣkramaṇam, viparītañca praveśanam, evam urdhvadeśena saṃyogajananādadhodeśena vibhāgajananā ccotkṣepaṇamityādi bhaviṣyatoti । athotkṣepaṇādiṣu niṣkramaṇādiṣu ca samāne vargaśaḥ pratyayānuvṛttivyāvṛtti sadbhāve satyutkṣepaṇādīnāmeva jātibhedo na niṣkramaṇādīnāmityatra na viśeṣaheturastīti ।

[II,249,15]

etanna, jātisaṅkaraprasaṅgāt । tadāha niṣkramaṇādīnāṃ jātibhedāt pratyayānuvṛttivyāvṛttau satyāṃ jātisaṅkaro viruddhajātisamāveśaḥ prasajyate । sa cānyatrānupalabdheraniṣṭaḥ । yadyapi sattādravyatvādiparāparabhedabhinnamekasyāṃ vyaktāvasti, tathāpi na gotvāśvatvādyupalabdham । atra caikasyāṃ vyaktau niṣka maṇatvapraveśanatvajātiprasaṅgaḥ । kathamityāha dvayordraṣṭrorekasyāṃ karmavyaktī yugapanniṣkramaṇapraveśanapratyayau dṛṣṭāviti । kasya tat karmatyāha ekasmāda pavarakādapavarakāntaraṃ gacchataḥ puruṣasyeti । tathā hi dvayorapavarakayorekameva dvāramityubhayatra vyavasthitayoḥ puruṣayoranyasmiśca brajati puruṣe viśiṣṭasaṃyoga vibhāgopalambhād yugapanniṣkramaṇapraveśanapratyayau dṛṣṭāveva, tathā ca dvārapradeśe praviśati niṣkramatīti ca । yo hi draṣṭā svāpavarakāntadeśe vibhāgaṃ bahirdeśe ca saṃyogamupalabhate, tasya niṣkramatīti pratyayo bhavati । yastu svāpavarakā ntadeśe saṃyoga bahirdeśe ca vibhāgamupalabhate, tasya praveśanapratyayo bhavati । yadā tu pratisīrādijavanikādyapanītaṃ bhavatītyādipadenānyasyāpi kuḍyāde<II,250>rāvaraṇasyāpanayanastadā viśiṣṭasya kāryabhedasyānapalabdharna niṣkramaṇapratyayaḥ, nāpi praveśanapratyayaḥ । kiṃ tarhi ? gamanapratyaya eva bhavati । tasmādatasyā gamanavyaktau viruddhajātisamāveśaprasaṅgāt kāryabhedādeva pratyayabheda ityuktam । tathā nālikāyāṃ vaṃśapatrādau patati draṣṭaṇāmadhistiryagvyavasthitānā yugapadbhramaṇapatanapraveśanapratyayā dṛṣṭā iti jātīnāṃ bhramaṇatvādīnāṃ saṅkara prasaṅga iti ।

[II,250,7]

svapakṣe doṣaparihārārthamāha na caivamutkṣepaṇādiṣu pratyayasako dṛṣṭaḥ । yasya bhayād viruddhajātisamāveśaprasaṅgaparihārārthaṃ kāryabhedena bhedā'bhyupa gamyata iti । upasaṃhāramāha tasmādutkṣepaṇādīnāmeva jātibhedāt pratyayā vṛttivyāvṛttī, niṣkramaṇādīnāntu kāryabhedāditi ।

[II,250,11]

(“kathaṃ yugapatpratyayabheda iti cet, atha mataṃ yathā jātisara nāsti, ebamanekakarmasaro 'ṇi ekasmin vastuni jāstītyekaritā karmaṇi yugapada gaṇāṃ bhramaṇapatananaveśanapratyayāḥ kathaṃ avantīti ! bramaḥ, na, avayavāvavinodiviśiṣṭasaṃyoga vibhāgānāṃ bhedāt । thāha draṣṭā avayavānāṃ pārśvataḥ paryāyeṇa dikapradeśaḥ saṃyogavibhāgāna paśyāta, tastha śramaṇapratyayo bhavati, yo baryāvana ayapradeśa vibhāga saṃyogavāvekṣale tasya patanapratyayo bhavati । yaḥ panalikāladaśa saba bahirdeśe ca vibhāgaṃ paśyati tasya praveśanapratyayo bhavatīti siddhaḥ kā bhedānniṣkramaṇādīnāṃ pratyayabheda iti ।”)

[II,250,20]

paramatamāśaṅkate kathaṃ yugapat pratyayabheda iti cet, iti । ara vivaraṇam atha mataṃ yathā jātisaṅkaro nāstyevamanekakarmasakarāyā vastuni nāstītyuktameva । ataḥ kathamekasmin karmaṇi kāraṇābhāvād draṣṭaṇā bhramaṇapatanapraveśanapratyayāḥ parasparavyāvattātmāno bhavanti, bhāvena kāryasyānutpatteriti । atra bramaḥ ityādi pratisamācā yat tvayoktaṃ kāraṇābhāvenānutpattireva bhramaṇādipratyayānāmityat । adhyavāvayavinodigdeśasaṃyogavibhāgabhedāt tadupapatteḥ । avayavaścāvayavī <II,251> cetyavayavāvayavinau tayodigdeśaviśiṣṭasaṃyogavibhāgāḥ, tadbhedāditi । tadavāha yo hi draṣṭā avayavānāṃ pārvataḥ paryāyeṇa dikpradeśaiḥ saṃyogavibhāgān paśyati tasya bhramaṇapratyayo bhavati । yastvavayavinyūjapradeśād vibhāgamadhaḥ sayāgañcāvekṣate tasya patati patramiti patanapratyayo bhavati । yaḥ punarnāli kāntadaśe garlāntardeśe saṃyogaṃ bahirdeśe ca vibhāgaṃ paśyati tasya praviśati patramiti praveśanapratyayaḥ । tasmāta siddhaḥ kāryabhedānniṣkramaṇādīnāṃ pratyayabhedo na jātibhedāditi ।

[II,251,8]

anye tu bhramaṇarecanasyandanojvalanādibhedena karmaṇāmasaṅkhyātatvā niṣkramaṇādīnāṃ jātibhedāt pratyayabhedasiddhau na kiñcid bādhakamastītyato 16 svamatamiti । na ca bhramaṇarecanādīnāṃ gamana evāntarbhāva iti manyante । etattu na yuktam, tasya karmatvaparyāyatvena vakṣyamāṇatvāt, jātisaṅkaraprasaṅgasya ca bādhakasya dṛḍhatvāditi ।

[II,251,13]

(“bhavatūtoṣaṇādīnāṃ jātibhedāt pratyayabhedaḥ, niṣkramaṇādīnāntu kāya bhedāditi । atha gamanatvaṃ ki karmatvaparyāyaḥ ? āhosvidaparaṃ sāmānyamiti । kutaste saṃśayaḥ ? samasteṣatkṣepaṇādiṣu karmapratyayavada manapratyayāviśeṣāta karmavaparyāya iti gamyate । yatastūtkṣapaṇādivad aśaṣasajñayābhihitaṃ tasmādaparaṃ sāmānyaṃ syāditi ? na । karmatva yāyatvāt । ātmatvapuruṣatvavata karmatvaparyāya evaṃ gamanatvamiti । atha paśaṣasaṃjñayā kimartha vāmana mahaṇaṃ kṛtamiti ? na, bhramaṇācavarodhārthatvāt । utkṣepaṇādiśabdairanavasvānāṃ bhramaṇapatanasyandanādīnāmavarodhārtha gamana "haṇa kṛtamili । anyathā hi yānyeva catvāri viśeṣasaṃjñayoktāni tānyeva sāmānya viśeṣajñāviṣayāṇi prasajyeraniti । athavā astvaparaṃ mānya gamanatvamaniyatadigadeśasaṃyogavibhāgakāraṇeṣu bhramaṇādiṣveva vartate । gamana śābadastakṣeṣaṇādiṣa bhākto draṣṭavyaḥ, svāśrayasayā kartṛtvasāmānyāditi ।”)

[II,251,26]

bhaktūtkṣepaṇādīnāṃ jātibhedād bhedo na niṣkramaṇādīnām । atha gama va ki karmatvaparyāyaḥ “ghaṭaḥ kalaśaḥ” iti paryāyavata, āhosvidaparaṃ sāmānyam, <II,252> utkṣepaṇatvādivaditi cintyam । kutaḥ kāraṇāt te saṃśaya ityācāryasya praśnaḥ । sa cānupapannaḥ । tathā hi sandigdhena praśne kṛte sati tatpratisamādhānaṃ nyāyyam, na tu saṃśayakaraṇena vacanam, tasya sāmānyadharmādibhyaḥ pūrvamevotpattinirūpaṇāt । naiṣa doṣaḥ । saṃśayakāraṇajñāne sati taducchittāvupāyānuṣṭhānam upalabdhavyādhikāraṇasya vaidyasyeva aprayāsenaiva ghaṭata iti manyamānaḥ kāraṇaṃ praśnayatīti । tadāha samasteṣūtkṣepaṇādiṣu bhramaṇādiṣu ca karmapratyayavad gamanapratyayāviśeṣāt karmatvaparyāya iti gamyate । yathā hyatkṣepaṇakarmāpakṣepaṇakarmetyādivyavahāropalambhādaśeṣabhedavyāpakaṃ karmatvam, evamadhvaṃ gacchatyadhogacchatītyādivyavahāropalambhād gamanamapya śeṣabhedavyāpakamityataḥ karmatvaparyāya iti jñāyate ।

[II,252,11]

na cātra niścaya evetyāha yatastutkṣepaṇādivad viśeṣasaṃjñayā bhihitam, tasmādaparaṃ sāmānyaṃ syāditi । na hi viśeṣadarśanena gaṇanāyāṃ tadavasare sāmānyasaṃjñānirdeśo dṛṣṭaḥ । yathā pṛthivyādi saṃjñāvasare dravyasaṃjñāyāḥ । tasmādubhayarūpadharmopalambhād viśeṣānupalambhādibhyaśca kiṃ karmavad gamanatvaṃ paraṃ sāmānyam, āhosvidutkṣepaṇatvādivadaparamiti saṃśayaḥ kāryaḥ ? na saṃśayaḥ kāryaḥ, karmatvapayāṃyatvādātmatvapuruṣatvavat paryāya eva gamanatvamiti, sarvatra karmapratyayavad gamanapratyayopalambhāditi nyāyāt । atha viśeṣasaṃjñayā kimarthaṃ gamanagrahaṇaṃ kṛtamiti, viśeṣasaṃjñāvasare sāmānya saṃjñopadarśanasyādarśanāt । na, bhramaṇādyavarodhārthatvāt । utkṣepaṇādiśabdai ranavaruddhānāmasagṛhītānāṃ bhramaṇavatanasyandanādīnāmavarodhārtham, karmatva jñāpanārthamiti । anyathā hi gamanagrahaṇamantareṇa yānyeva catvāri viśeṣa saṃjñoktānyutkṣepaṇādīni tānyeva sāmānyaviśeṣasaṃjñāviṣayāṇi prasajyeraniti । sāmānyasaṃjñā karmasaṃjñā, viśepasaṃjñā cotkṣepaṇādisaṃjñā, tadviṣayāṇi catvāryeva prasajyeran, na bhramaṇādīni । kuta etat ? viśeṣasaṃjñāviṣayāṇāmeva sāmānya saṃjñāviṣayatvāt । tasmādutkṣepaṇādivad bhramaṇādīnāmapi karmatvajñāpanārthaṃ gamanagrahaṇaṃ kṛtamiti । na caitasmin pakṣa bhramaṇādīnāmaparajātisambandhe 'pi dūṣaṇam, tadapekṣayā ānantyasyābhyupagamāt । yacca gamanagrahaṇād bhramaṇādayaḥ saṅagṛhītā iti vākyam, tadanyathā vyākhyātam ।

<II,253>

[II,253,1]
